Tool Verification for Test-Time Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Ruotong Liao, Nikolai Röhrich, Xiaohan Wang, Yuhui Zhang, Yasaman Samadzadeh, Volker Tresp, Serena Yeung-Levy
First: 2026-03-02T18:57:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:57:52+00:00
Comments: 12 pages, 11 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Test-time reinforcement learning (TTRL) has emerged as a promising paradigm for self-evolving large reasoning models (LRMs), enabling online adaptation on unlabeled test inputs via self-induced rewards through majority voting. However, a spurious yet high-frequency unverified consensus can become a biased and reinforced reward signal, leading to incorrect mode collapse. We address this failure mode with T^3RL (Tool-Verification for Test-Time Reinforcement Learning), which introduces test-time tool verification into reward estimation. Concretely, a verifier uses an external tool as evidence (e.g., from code execution) to upweight verified rollouts in a verification-aware voting, producing more reliable pseudo-labels for training. Across various math difficulties (MATH-500, AMC, and AIME 2024) and diverse backbone types, T^3RL significantly improves over TTRL, with larger gains on harder problems. More broadly, T^3RL can be viewed as verified online data synthesis, highlighting test-time tool verification as a key mechanism for stabilizing self-evolution.
中文标题/摘要
标题：测试时强化学习的工具验证方法
测试时强化学习（TTRL）已成为一种前景广阔的自进化大型推理模型范式，通过多数投票产生的自诱导奖励，实现对未标注测试输入的在线适应。然而，高频但未经核实的虚假共识可能成为有偏且被强化的奖励信号，导致错误的模式坍缩。我们提出T^3RL（测试时强化学习的工具验证）来解决这一失效模式，将测试时工具验证引入奖励估计。具体而言，验证器使用外部工具（如代码执行结果）作为证据，在验证感知的投票中提升已验证轨迹的权重，从而为训练生成更可靠的伪标签。在多种数学难度数据集（MATH-500、AMC及AIME 2024）和不同骨干模型上的实验表明，T^3RL较TTRL有显著提升，且在难题上增益更大。更广泛而言，T^3RL可视为经过验证的在线数据合成方法，凸显了测试时工具验证作为稳定自进化过程的关键机制。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the problem that test-time reinforcement learning (TTRL) for large reasoning models can suffer from incorrect mode collapse due to spurious, high-frequency consensus from unverified majority voting, which provides biased reward signals. To address this, the method T^3RL introduces test-time tool verification into reward estimation, where a verifier uses external tool evidence, such as code execution, to upweight verified rollouts in a verification-aware voting process, thereby generating more reliable pseudo-labels for training. Experimental results across various math datasets (MATH-500, AMC, and AIME 2024) and diverse backbone models show that T^3RL significantly outperforms TTRL, with greater improvements on harder problems, demonstrating its effectiveness as a mechanism for stabilizing self-evolution through verified online data synthesis.
本文的动机是，针对大型推理模型的测试时强化学习（TTRL）可能因未经验证的多数据决产生虚假高频共识，导致有偏的奖励信号和错误的模式崩溃。为解决此问题，方法T^3RL在奖励估计中引入了测试时工具验证，通过验证器使用外部工具证据（如代码执行）在验证感知投票中提升已验证轨迹的权重，从而为训练生成更可靠的伪标签。在多种数学数据集（MATH-500、AMC和AIME 2024）和不同骨干模型上的实验结果表明，T^3RL显著优于TTRL，且在更难问题上提升更大，凸显了测试时工具验证作为稳定自我进化机制的关键作用。
Return Augmented Decision Transformer for Off-Dynamics Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Ruhan Wang, Yu Yang, Zhishuai Liu, Dongruo Zhou, Pan Xu
Venue: Transactions on Machine Learning Research, 2026
First: 2024-10-30T20:46:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:38:36+00:00
Comments: 26 pages, 11 tables, 8 figures. Published in Transactions on Machine Learning Research (TMLR)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study offline off-dynamics reinforcement learning (RL) to utilize data from an easily accessible source domain to enhance policy learning in a target domain with limited data. Our approach centers on return-conditioned supervised learning (RCSL), particularly focusing on Decision Transformer (DT) type frameworks, which can predict actions conditioned on desired return guidance and complete trajectory history. Previous works address the dynamics shift problem by augmenting the reward in the trajectory from the source domain to match the optimal trajectory in the target domain. However, this strategy can not be directly applicable in RCSL owing to (1) the unique form of the RCSL policy class, which explicitly depends on the return, and (2) the absence of a straightforward representation of the optimal trajectory distribution. We propose the Return Augmented (REAG) method for DT type frameworks, where we augment the return in the source domain by aligning its distribution with that in the target domain. We provide the theoretical analysis demonstrating that the RCSL policy learned from REAG achieves the same level of suboptimality as would be obtained without a dynamics shift. We introduce two practical implementations REAG$_\text{Dara}^{*}$ and REAG$_\text{MV}^{*}$ respectively. Thorough experiments on D4RL datasets and various DT-type baselines demonstrate that our methods consistently enhance the performance of DT type frameworks in off-dynamics RL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向异动态强化学习的回报增强决策变换器
本研究探讨离线异动态强化学习（RL），旨在利用易获取源域的数据提升目标域（数据有限）的策略学习。方法核心是基于回报条件的监督学习（RCSL），聚焦于决策变换器（DT）类框架，该类框架能依据期望回报指导和完整轨迹历史预测动作。先前研究通过调整源域轨迹的奖励以匹配目标域最优轨迹来解决动态偏移问题，但该策略无法直接适用于RCSL，原因在于：（1）RCSL策略类显式依赖回报的独特形式；（2）缺乏最优轨迹分布的直观表示。我们提出用于DT类框架的回报增强（REAG）方法，通过对齐源域与目标域的回报分布实现源域回报增强。理论分析表明，基于REAG学习的RCSL策略能达到与无动态偏移时相当的次优性水平。我们进一步提出两种实践实现：REAG$_\text{Dara}^{*}$ 与 REAG$_\text{MV}^{*}$。在D4RL数据集及多种DT类基线模型上的系统实验表明，本方法能持续提升DT类框架在异动态RL中的性能。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses offline off-dynamics reinforcement learning, aiming to leverage abundant data from a source domain to improve policy learning in a target domain with scarce data, focusing on return-conditioned supervised learning frameworks like Decision Transformer. The proposed method, Return Augmented (REAG), tackles the dynamics shift by augmenting the return in source domain trajectories to align their distribution with the target domain, circumventing limitations of prior reward-augmentation strategies that are incompatible with the return-dependent policy class and lack an optimal trajectory representation. Theoretical analysis shows the learned policy achieves suboptimality comparable to a no-shift scenario, and practical implementations REAG_Dara* and REAG_MV* are validated through experiments on D4RL datasets, consistently enhancing the performance of Decision Transformer-type baselines in off-dynamics settings.
本文研究离线异动态强化学习，旨在利用源域中易于获取的数据来增强目标域中数据有限时的策略学习，重点关注基于回报条件监督学习的框架，如决策变换器。所提出的回报增强方法通过调整源域轨迹中的回报分布，使其与目标域对齐，以解决动态偏移问题，克服了先前奖励增强策略因策略类显式依赖回报且缺乏最优轨迹表示而无法直接应用的局限。理论分析表明，学习到的策略能达到与无动态偏移时相当的次优性，并通过在D4RL数据集上的实验验证了两种实用实现REAG_Dara*和REAG_MV*，证明其能持续提升决策变换器类基线在异动态强化学习中的性能。
Near-Optimal Regret for KL-Regularized Multi-Armed Bandits
Authors: Kaixuan Ji, Qingyue Zhao, Heyang Zhao, Qiwei Di, Quanquan Gu
First: 2026-03-02T18:17:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:17:33+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent studies have shown that reinforcement learning with KL-regularized objectives can enjoy faster rates of convergence or logarithmic regret, in contrast to the classical $\sqrt{T}$-type regret in the unregularized setting. However, the statistical efficiency of online learning with respect to KL-regularized objectives remains far from completely characterized, even when specialized to multi-armed bandits (MABs). We address this problem for MABs via a sharp analysis of KL-UCB using a novel peeling argument, which yields a $\tilde{O}(ηK\log^2T)$ upper bound: the first high-probability regret bound with linear dependence on $K$. Here, $T$ is the time horizon, $K$ is the number of arms, $η^{-1}$ is the regularization intensity, and $\tilde{O}$ hides all logarithmic factors except those involving $\log T$. The near-tightness of our analysis is certified by the first non-constant lower bound $Ω(ηK \log T)$, which follows from subtle hard-instance constructions and a tailored decomposition of the Bayes prior. Moreover, in the low-regularization regime (i.e., large $η$), we show that the KL-regularized regret for MABs is $η$-independent and scales as $\tildeΘ(\sqrt{KT})$. Overall, our results provide a thorough understanding of KL-regularized MABs across all regimes of $η$ and yield nearly optimal bounds in terms of $K$, $η$, and $T$.
中文标题/摘要
标题：KL正则化多臂老虎机的近最优遗憾界
近期研究表明，与经典无正则化设定中$\sqrt{T}$型遗憾相比，采用KL正则化目标的强化学习可获得更快的收敛速度或对数遗憾。然而，即使专门针对多臂老虎机问题，在线学习在KL正则化目标下的统计效率仍远未完全刻画。我们通过新颖的剥离论证对KL-UCB算法进行精细分析，解决了该问题，得到了$\tilde{O}(ηK\log^2T)$上界：这是首个与$K$呈线性依赖关系的高概率遗憾界。其中$T$为时间跨度，$K$为臂数，$η^{-1}$表示正则化强度，$\tilde{O}$隐藏了除$\log T$外所有对数因子。我们通过首个非常数下界$Ω(ηK \log T)$证明了分析的近紧性，该下界源于精妙的困难实例构造和贝叶斯先验的定制化分解。此外，在低正则化区域（即$η$较大时），我们证明MAB的KL正则化遗憾与$η$无关且按$\tildeΘ(\sqrt{KT})$缩放。总体而言，我们的结果全面揭示了KL正则化MAB在所有$η$区域的性质，并在$K$、$η$、$T$维度上给出了近乎最优的界。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates the statistical efficiency of KL-regularized multi-armed bandits (MABs), motivated by the need to better characterize the convergence and regret properties of reinforcement learning with KL-regularized objectives, which have shown promise for faster convergence compared to unregularized settings. The method centers on a sharp analysis of the KL-UCB algorithm using a novel peeling argument, leading to a high-probability regret upper bound of Õ(ηK log² T), which is the first to exhibit linear dependence on the number of arms K. The main experimental results, supported by theoretical analysis, demonstrate near-optimality: a matching lower bound of Ω(ηK log T) is established via hard-instance constructions, and in the low-regularization regime (large η), the regret is shown to be η-independent and scales as Õ(√(KT)), providing a comprehensive understanding across all regularization intensities.
本文研究了KL正则化多臂老虎机（MAB）的统计效率，其动机在于需要更好地刻画带有KL正则化目标的强化学习的收敛性和遗憾特性，这类目标相比无正则化设置已显示出更快的收敛潜力。方法核心在于使用一种新颖的剥离论证对KL-UCB算法进行精细分析，得到了一个高概率的遗憾上界Õ(ηK log² T)，这是首个展现出与臂数K线性依赖关系的界。主要实验结果得到理论分析支持，证明了近乎最优性：通过困难实例构造建立了匹配的下界Ω(ηK log T)，并且在低正则化区域（大η）下，遗憾被证明与η无关且按Õ(√(KT))缩放，从而对所有正则化强度提供了全面的理解。
Data-to-Energy Stochastic Dynamics
Authors: Kirill Tamogashev, Nikolay Malkin
First: 2025-09-30T15:03:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T18:11:04+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
The Schrödinger bridge problem is concerned with finding a stochastic dynamical system bridging two marginal distributions that minimises a certain transportation cost. This problem, which represents a generalisation of optimal transport to the stochastic case, has received attention due to its connections to diffusion models and flow matching, as well as its applications in the natural sciences. However, all existing algorithms allow to infer such dynamics only for cases where samples from both distributions are available. In this paper, we propose the first general method for modelling Schrödinger bridges when one (or both) distributions are given by their unnormalised densities, with no access to data samples. Our algorithm relies on a generalisation of the iterative proportional fitting (IPF) procedure to the data-free case, inspired by recent developments in off-policy reinforcement learning for training of diffusion samplers. We demonstrate the efficacy of the proposed data-to-energy IPF on synthetic problems, finding that it can successfully learn transports between multimodal distributions. As a secondary consequence of our reinforcement learning formulation, which assumes a fixed time discretisation scheme for the dynamics, we find that existing data-to-data Schrödinger bridge algorithms can be substantially improved by learning the diffusion coefficient of the dynamics. Finally, we apply the newly developed algorithm to the problem of sampling posterior distributions in latent spaces of generative models, thus creating a data-free image-to-image translation method. Code: https://github.com/mmacosha/d2e-stochastic-dynamics
中文标题/摘要
标题：数据到能量的随机动力学
薛定谔桥问题旨在寻找连接两个边缘分布的随机动力系统，以最小化特定传输成本。该问题将最优传输推广至随机情形，因其与扩散模型、流匹配的联系及在自然科学中的应用而备受关注。然而，现有算法仅适用于两个分布均存在数据样本的情况。本文首次提出一种通用方法，可在无法获取数据样本、仅通过未归一化密度函数给定一个（或两个）分布时建模薛定谔桥。受近期扩散采样器训练中离策略强化学习的启发，本算法将迭代比例拟合（IPF）过程推广至无数据场景。我们在合成问题上验证了所提数据到能量IPF的有效性，证明其能成功学习多峰分布间的传输机制。基于强化学习框架（假设动力学采用固定时间离散方案）的衍生发现表明：通过动态学习扩散系数，现有数据到数据薛定谔桥算法可获得显著改进。最后，我们将新算法应用于生成模型隐空间的后验分布采样问题，从而构建了一种无需数据的图像到图像转换方法。代码：https://github.com/mmacosha/d2e-stochastic-dynamics
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the limitation in existing Schrödinger bridge algorithms, which require samples from both marginal distributions, by proposing a novel method that works when one or both distributions are specified only by their unnormalized densities without data samples. The method generalizes the iterative proportional fitting (IPF) procedure to this data-free setting, drawing inspiration from off-policy reinforcement learning techniques used in diffusion sampler training. Experimental results on synthetic problems show the method successfully learns transports between multimodal distributions, and it also improves existing data-to-data algorithms by learning the diffusion coefficient; furthermore, it is applied to sample posterior distributions in generative model latent spaces, enabling data-free image-to-image translation.
本文针对现有薛定谔桥算法需要两个边缘分布样本的局限性，提出了一种新方法，适用于一个或两个分布仅由其未归一化密度指定而无数据样本的情况。该方法将迭代比例拟合（IPF）过程推广至这种无数据设置，灵感来源于扩散采样器训练中的离策略强化学习技术。在合成问题上的实验结果表明，该方法能成功学习多峰分布间的传输，并通过学习扩散系数改进了现有的数据到数据算法；此外，该方法被应用于生成模型潜在空间的后验分布采样，实现了无数据的图像到图像转换。
MuFlex: A Scalable, Physics-based Platform for Multi-Building Flexibility Analysis and Coordination
Authors: Ziyan Wu, Ivan Korolija, Rui Tang
First: 2025-08-19T05:44:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:55:58+00:00
Comments: The platform is released open-source on GitHub: https://github.com/BuildNexusX/MuFlex
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
With the increasing penetration of renewable generation on the power grid, maintaining system balance requires coordinated demand flexibility from aggregations of buildings. Reinforcement learning has been widely explored for building controls because of its model-free nature. Open-source simulation testbeds are essential not only for training RL agents but also for fairly benchmarking control strategies. However, most building-sector testbeds target single buildings; multi-building platforms are relatively limited and typically rely on simplified models (e.g., Resistance-Capacitance) or data-driven approaches, which lack the ability to fully capture the physical intricacies and intermediate variables necessary for interpreting control performance. Moreover, these platforms often impose fixed inputs, outputs, and model formats, restricting their applicability as benchmarking tools across diverse control scenarios. To address these gaps, MuFlex, a scalable, open-source platform for multi-building flexibility coordination, was developed. MuFlex enables synchronous information exchange and co-simulation across multiple detailed building models programmed in EnergyPlus and Modelica, and adheres to the latest OpenAI Gym interface, providing a modular, standardized RL implementation. The platform's physics-based capabilities and workflow were demonstrated in a case study coordinating demand flexibility across four office buildings using the Soft Actor-Critic algorithm. The results show that under four buildings' coordination, SAC effectively reduced the aggregated peak demand by nearly 12% with maintained indoor comfort to ensure the power demand below the threshold. Additionally, the platform's scalability was investigated through computational benchmarking on building clusters with varying sizes, model types, and simulation programs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MuFlex：一个可扩展的、基于物理的多建筑灵活性分析与协调平台
随着可再生能源在电网中的渗透率不断提高，维持系统平衡需要建筑集群的协调需求灵活性。强化学习因其无模型特性在建筑控制领域得到广泛探索。开源仿真测试平台不仅对训练强化学习代理至关重要，也为公平评估控制策略提供了基准。然而，大多数建筑领域测试平台针对单一建筑；多建筑平台相对有限，通常依赖简化模型（如电阻-电容模型）或数据驱动方法，这些方法难以全面捕捉解释控制性能所需的物理细节和中间变量。此外，这些平台常采用固定的输入、输出和模型格式，限制了其作为跨不同控制场景基准测试工具的适用性。为弥补这些不足，我们开发了MuFlex——一个可扩展的开源多建筑灵活性协调平台。MuFlex支持在EnergyPlus和Modelica编程的多个详细建筑模型之间进行同步信息交换和协同仿真，并遵循最新的OpenAI Gym接口，提供模块化、标准化的强化学习实现。该平台的基于物理功能和工作流程通过一个案例研究得到验证，该案例使用软演员-评论家算法协调四栋办公建筑的需求灵活性。结果表明，在四栋建筑协调下，SAC算法将聚合峰值需求有效降低了近12%，同时保持室内舒适度，确保电力需求低于阈值。此外，通过对不同规模、模型类型和仿真程序的建筑集群进行计算基准测试，验证了平台的可扩展性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for coordinated demand flexibility in buildings to balance power grids with high renewable penetration, this paper introduces MuFlex, a scalable open-source platform for multi-building flexibility analysis and coordination. The method addresses limitations of existing testbeds by enabling synchronous co-simulation of detailed physics-based building models (EnergyPlus/Modelica) through a modular OpenAI Gym interface, facilitating standardized reinforcement learning implementation. In experimental validation using the Soft Actor-Critic algorithm across four office buildings, the platform demonstrated effective coordination, reducing aggregated peak demand by nearly 12% while maintaining indoor comfort and adhering to power thresholds, with additional benchmarks confirming scalability across varying building clusters.
本文的动机是应对高比例可再生能源并网下电网平衡的需求，需协调建筑群的灵活性响应。为此，作者提出了MuFlex，一个可扩展的开源多建筑灵活性分析与协调平台。该方法通过支持基于物理的详细建筑模型（EnergyPlus/Modelica）的同步协同仿真，并采用模块化的OpenAI Gym接口，克服了现有测试平台模型简化或灵活性不足的限制，实现了标准化的强化学习应用。在采用Soft Actor-Critic算法对四栋办公建筑进行的案例实验中，平台有效协调了需求，将总峰值负荷降低了近12%，同时保持了室内舒适度并使电力需求低于设定阈值，进一步的算力基准测试也验证了平台在不同规模建筑集群上的可扩展性。
Pencil Puzzle Bench: A Benchmark for Multi-Step Verifiable Reasoning
Authors: Justin Waugh
First: 2026-03-02T17:40:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:40:54+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce Pencil Puzzle Bench, a framework for evaluating large language model reasoning through pencil puzzles, a family of constraint-satisfaction problems closely related to NP-complete problems, with deterministic, step-level verification. From a database of 62,231 puzzles across 94 varieties with verified unique solutions, we select a benchmark of 300 puzzles spanning 20 varieties and evaluate 51 models from 11 providers in two modes: direct ask (single-shot) and agentic (multi-turn with iterative verification). A key differentiator of our benchmark is that every intermediate board state can be checked against variety-specific constraints, localizing errors to the exact rule violated, providing the infrastructure for dense, per-move reward signals for process supervision and reinforcement learning. Our evaluation reveals two distinct axes of capability: (1) reasoning effort scaling, where GPT-5.2 improves 81x from no reasoning to maximum effort; and (2) agentic iteration, where Claude Opus 4.6 rises from 0.3% to 30.0% through iterative checking, while GPT-5.2@xhigh improves from 20.2% to 56.0%. Agentic attempts span a median of 29 turns over 17 minutes, with the longest exceeding 1,221 turns and 14.3 hours - a demanding test of long-context utilization, not just reasoning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：铅笔谜题基准：面向多步可验证推理的评测框架
我们提出铅笔谜题基准——一个通过铅笔谜题（一类与NP完全问题紧密相关、具备确定性步级验证机制的约束满足问题）评估大语言模型推理能力的框架。我们从包含94个种类、62,231道已验证唯一解谜题的数据库中，选取涵盖20个种类的300道谜题作为基准集，并以两种模式评估来自11家提供商的51个模型：直接提问（单次）与智能体模式（多轮迭代验证）。本基准的核心特色在于每个中间棋盘状态均可按种类特定约束进行校验，能将错误定位至违反的具体规则，从而为过程监督与强化学习提供密集的逐步奖励信号基础设施。评估揭示了两类能力维度：（1）推理努力扩展性：GPT-5.2在无推理到最大努力区间实现81倍性能提升；（2）智能体迭代能力：Claude Opus 4.6通过迭代检查从0.3%提升至30.0%，而GPT-5.2@xhigh从20.2%提升至56.0%。智能体尝试中位数达29轮对话（耗时17分钟），最长记录超过1,221轮对话（14.3小时），这不仅是对推理能力的考验，更是对长上下文利用能力的严苛测试。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to evaluate large language models on complex, verifiable reasoning tasks, this paper introduces Pencil Puzzle Bench, a benchmark built from a large database of pencil puzzles with unique solutions to test multi-step constraint satisfaction. The method involves evaluating models in two modes—single-shot direct ask and multi-turn agentic with iterative verification—where each intermediate puzzle state can be checked against specific constraints to localize errors. Key experimental results show that models like GPT-5.2 and Claude Opus 4.6 achieve significant performance gains through agentic iteration, with improvements from 20.2% to 56.0% and 0.3% to 30.0% respectively, while also demonstrating extensive reasoning effort scaling and demanding long-context utilization.
本文旨在评估大语言模型在复杂、可验证推理任务上的能力，为此引入了Pencil Puzzle Bench基准，该基准基于一个包含大量唯一解铅笔谜题的数据库，用于测试多步约束满足问题。方法包括在两种模式下评估模型：单次直接提问和多轮代理迭代验证，其中每个中间谜题状态可根据特定约束进行检查以定位错误。主要实验结果表明，如GPT-5.2和Claude Opus 4.6等模型通过代理迭代实现了显著性能提升，分别从20.2%提高到56.0%和从0.3%提高到30.0%，同时展示了推理努力的大幅扩展和对长上下文利用的高要求。
SPARE: Single-Pass Annotation with Reference-Guided Evaluation for Automatic Process Supervision and Reward Modelling
Authors: Md Imbesat Hassan Rizvi, Xiaodan Zhu, Iryna Gurevych
Venue: AAAI 2026 Oral
First: 2025-06-18T14:37:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:34:48+00:00
Comments: Accepted to AAAI 2026 (Oral)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Process or step-wise supervision has played a crucial role in advancing complex multi-step reasoning capabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs). However, efficient, high-quality automated process annotation remains a significant challenge. To address this, we introduce Single-Pass Annotation with Reference-Guided Evaluation (SPARE), a novel structured framework that enables efficient per-step annotation by jointly aligning solution steps to reference solutions and determine its accuracy with explicit reasoning in single generation. We demonstrate SPARE's effectiveness across four diverse datasets spanning mathematical reasoning (GSM8K, MATH), multi-hop question answering (MuSiQue-Ans), and spatial reasoning (SpaRP), showing consistent improvements in two applications: (1) training Process Reward Models (PRMs) for ranking and aggregating multiple generations, and (2) fine-tuning models via offline reinforcement learning for greedy decoding. On ProcessBench, SPARE demonstrates data-efficient out-of-distribution generalization, using only $\sim$16% of training samples compared to human-labeled and other synthetically trained baselines. Additionally, it achieves competitive performance with MCTS-based methods while offering 2.3$\times$ speedup in terms of total token count. Manual analysis reveals complementary precision-recall characteristics with MCTS approaches, suggesting potential for ensemble methods. These results establish SPARE as a practical and scalable solution for automatic process supervision in LLM reasoning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SPARE：基于参考引导评估的单次标注框架——面向自动过程监督与奖励建模
过程或分步监督对提升大语言模型（LLM）的复杂多步推理能力至关重要，但高效、高质量的自动过程标注仍是重大挑战。为此，我们提出基于参考引导评估的单次标注框架（SPARE），该结构化框架通过将解题步骤与参考答案对齐，并在单次生成中通过显式推理判断准确性，实现高效的分步标注。我们在数学推理（GSM8K、MATH）、多跳问答（MuSiQue-Ans）和空间推理（SpaRP）四个数据集上验证了SPARE的有效性，并在两个应用中展现出一致改进：（1）训练过程奖励模型（PRM）以排序和聚合多轮生成结果；（2）通过离线强化学习对模型进行微调以支持贪婪解码。在ProcessBench上，SPARE仅需约16%的训练样本（相较于人工标注及其他合成训练基线），即展现出高效的数据分布外泛化能力。同时，其性能与基于MCTS的方法相当，但总标记数处理速度提升2.3倍。人工分析表明SPARE与MCTS方法在精确率-召回率特性上具有互补性，为集成方法提供了潜力。这些结果证明SPARE是LLM推理中实用且可扩展的自动过程监督解决方案。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces SPARE, a framework designed to address the challenge of efficiently generating high-quality automated process annotations for large language models (LLMs) engaged in multi-step reasoning. The method involves a single-pass, structured annotation process that aligns solution steps to reference solutions and evaluates their accuracy with explicit reasoning. Experimental results across mathematical, multi-hop QA, and spatial reasoning datasets show that SPARE enables data-efficient training of process reward models and fine-tuning via offline RL, achieving strong out-of-distribution generalization with only about 16% of the training samples required by baselines and offering a 2.3x speedup in token count compared to MCTS-based methods.
本文提出了SPARE框架，旨在解决为大语言模型在多步推理任务中高效生成高质量自动过程标注的挑战。该方法采用单次生成的结构化标注流程，将解答步骤与参考答案对齐，并通过显式推理判断其准确性。在数学推理、多跳问答和空间推理等多个数据集上的实验结果表明，SPARE能够以数据高效的方式训练过程奖励模型并通过离线强化学习进行微调，仅需约16%的基线训练样本即可实现良好的分布外泛化性能，且相比基于MCTS的方法在总token数上实现了2.3倍的加速。
Distributions as Actions: A Unified Framework for Diverse Action Spaces
Authors: Jiamin He, A. Rupam Mahmood, Martha White
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-06-19T21:19:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:30:05+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce a novel reinforcement learning (RL) framework that treats parameterized action distributions as actions, redefining the boundary between agent and environment. This reparameterization makes the new action space continuous, regardless of the original action type (discrete, continuous, hybrid, etc.). Under this new parameterization, we develop a generalized deterministic policy gradient estimator, Distributions-as-Actions Policy Gradient (DA-PG), which has lower variance than the gradient in the original action space. Although learning the critic over distribution parameters poses new challenges, we introduce Interpolated Critic Learning (ICL), a simple yet effective strategy to enhance learning, supported by insights from bandit settings. Building on TD3, a strong baseline for continuous control, we propose a practical actor-critic algorithm, Distributions-as-Actions Actor-Critic (DA-AC). Empirically, DA-AC achieves competitive performance in various settings across discrete, continuous, and hybrid control.
中文标题/摘要
标题：分布即行动：多样化行动空间的统一框架
我们提出了一种新颖的强化学习（RL）框架，将参数化的行动分布视为行动，重新定义了智能体与环境之间的边界。这种重新参数化使得新的行动空间变为连续，无论原始行动类型如何（离散、连续、混合等）。在此新参数化下，我们开发了一种广义确定性策略梯度估计器——分布即行动策略梯度（DA-PG），其方差低于原始行动空间中的梯度。尽管在分布参数上学习评论家面临新挑战，我们引入了插值评论家学习（ICL），这是一种简单而有效的策略，通过多臂赌博机设置的洞见支持以增强学习。基于连续控制的强基线TD3，我们提出了一种实用的行动者-评论家算法——分布即行动行动者-评论家（DA-AC）。实验表明，DA-AC在离散、连续和混合控制的各种设置中均取得了有竞争力的性能。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for a unified reinforcement learning framework that can handle diverse action spaces (discrete, continuous, hybrid) without specialized algorithms, this paper reparameterizes actions as parameterized distributions, making the action space continuous. The method introduces a generalized deterministic policy gradient estimator called Distributions-as-Actions Policy Gradient (DA-PG), which reduces variance, and addresses critic learning challenges with Interpolated Critic Learning (ICL). The resulting practical algorithm, Distributions-as-Actions Actor-Critic (DA-AC), built on TD3, demonstrates competitive experimental performance across discrete, continuous, and hybrid control tasks.
本文的动机是需要一个统一的强化学习框架，以处理离散、连续和混合等多种动作空间，而无需专门算法。其方法将动作重新参数化为参数化分布，使动作空间连续化，并提出了分布作为动作策略梯度（DA-PG）这一广义确定性策略梯度估计器以降低方差，同时通过插值评论家学习（ICL）解决评论家学习难题。基于TD3构建的实用算法——分布作为动作演员-评论家（DA-AC），在实验中于离散、连续和混合控制任务上均取得了有竞争力的性能。
Goal Reaching with Eikonal-Constrained Hierarchical Quasimetric Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Vittorio Giammarino, Ahmed H. Qureshi
First: 2025-12-12T21:37:11+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:21:38+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Goal-Conditioned Reinforcement Learning (GCRL) mitigates the difficulty of reward design by framing tasks as goal reaching rather than maximizing hand-crafted reward signals. In this setting, the optimal goal-conditioned value function naturally forms a quasimetric, motivating Quasimetric RL (QRL), which constrains value learning to quasimetric mappings and enforces local consistency through discrete, trajectory-based constraints. We propose Eikonal-Constrained Quasimetric RL (Eik-QRL), a continuous-time reformulation of QRL based on the Eikonal Partial Differential Equation (PDE). This PDE-based structure makes Eik-QRL trajectory-free, requiring only sampled states and goals, while improving out-of-distribution generalization. We provide theoretical guarantees for Eik-QRL and identify limitations that arise under complex dynamics. To address these challenges, we introduce Eik-Hierarchical QRL (Eik-HiQRL), which integrates Eik-QRL into a hierarchical decomposition. Empirically, Eik-HiQRL achieves state-of-the-art performance in offline goal-conditioned navigation and yields consistent gains over QRL in manipulation tasks, matching temporal-difference methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于Eikonal约束的层次拟度量强化学习实现目标抵达
目标条件强化学习（GCRL）通过将任务框架设定为目标抵达而非最大化人工设计的奖励信号，缓解了奖励设计的困难。在此设定下，最优目标条件值函数自然构成拟度量，由此催生了拟度量强化学习（QRL），该方法将值学习约束于拟度量映射，并通过基于离散轨迹的约束强制局部一致性。我们提出Eikonal约束拟度量强化学习（Eik-QRL），这是一种基于Eikonal偏微分方程（PDE）的QRL连续时间重构。这种基于PDE的结构使Eik-QRL无需依赖轨迹，仅需采样状态与目标，同时提升了分布外泛化能力。我们为Eik-QRL提供了理论保证，并识别了复杂动力学下出现的局限性。为应对这些挑战，我们引入层次化Eik-QRL（Eik-HiQRL），将Eik-QRL整合至层次分解框架中。实验表明，Eik-HiQRL在离线目标条件导航任务中达到最先进性能，并在操作任务中较QRL取得稳定提升，其表现与时序差分方法相当。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of reward design in Goal-Conditioned Reinforcement Learning (GCRL) by leveraging the quasimetric properties of optimal value functions. The method introduces Eikonal-Constrained Quasimetric RL (Eik-QRL), a continuous-time, trajectory-free reformulation based on the Eikonal PDE that improves generalization using only state-goal samples, and further proposes Eik-Hierarchical QRL (Eik-HiQRL) to handle complex dynamics through hierarchical decomposition. Experimental results show that Eik-HiQRL achieves state-of-the-art performance in offline goal-conditioned navigation and consistently outperforms prior QRL methods in manipulation tasks, matching temporal-difference approaches.
本文针对目标条件强化学习（GCRL）中奖励设计困难的问题，利用最优值函数的拟度量特性进行改进。方法上提出了基于Eikonal偏微分方程的Eikonal约束拟度量强化学习（Eik-QRL），这是一种连续时间、无轨迹的框架，仅需状态-目标样本即可提升泛化能力，并进一步引入分层分解的Eik-Hierarchical QRL（Eik-HiQRL）以处理复杂动态。实验结果表明，Eik-HiQRL在离线目标导航任务中达到最先进性能，并在操作任务中持续优于先前的QRL方法，与时间差分方法表现相当。
Learning from Synthetic Data Improves Multi-hop Reasoning
Authors: Anmol Kabra, Yilun Yin, Albert Gong, Kamilė Stankevičiūtė, Dongyoung Go, Johann Lee, Katie Z. Luo, Carla P. Gomes, Kilian Q. Weinberger
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-03-02T17:08:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T17:08:43+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning (RL) has been shown to significantly boost reasoning capabilities of large language models (LLMs) in math, coding, and multi-hop reasoning tasks. However, RL fine-tuning requires abundant high-quality verifiable data, often sourced from human annotations, generated from frontier LLMs, or scored by LLM-based verifiers. All three have considerable limitations: human-annotated datasets are small and expensive to curate, LLM-generated data is hallucination-prone and costly, and LLM-based verifiers are inaccurate and slow. In this work, we investigate a cheaper alternative: RL fine-tuning on rule-generated synthetic data for multi-hop reasoning tasks. We discover that LLMs fine-tuned on synthetic data perform significantly better on popular real-world question-answering benchmarks, despite the synthetic data containing only fictional knowledge. On stratifying performance by question difficulty, we find that synthetic data teaches LLMs to compose knowledge -- a fundamental and generalizable reasoning skill. Our work highlights rule-generated synthetic reasoning data as a free and scalable resource to improve LLM reasoning capabilities.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于合成数据学习提升多跳推理能力
强化学习（RL）已被证明能显著提升大语言模型（LLM）在数学、编程和多跳推理任务中的推理能力。然而，RL微调需要大量高质量可验证数据，这些数据通常来源于人工标注、前沿LLM生成或基于LLM的验证器评分。这三种方式均存在明显局限：人工标注数据集规模小且标注成本高昂，LLM生成数据易产生幻觉且代价昂贵，基于LLM的验证器则存在准确率低、速度慢的问题。本研究探索了一种更经济的替代方案：在多跳推理任务中使用规则生成的合成数据进行RL微调。我们发现，尽管合成数据仅包含虚构知识，但基于其微调的LLM在主流现实世界问答基准测试中表现显著更优。通过按问题难度分层分析性能，我们发现合成数据能教会LLM进行知识组合——这是一种基础且可泛化的推理技能。本研究凸显了规则生成的合成推理数据作为免费、可扩展资源对提升LLM推理能力的重要价值。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the high cost and limitations of existing data sources for reinforcement learning fine-tuning of large language models in multi-hop reasoning tasks, proposing the use of rule-generated synthetic data as a cheaper alternative. The method involves fine-tuning LLMs on synthetic data that contains only fictional knowledge, rather than relying on expensive human annotations, hallucination-prone LLM-generated data, or inaccurate LLM-based verifiers. Experimental results show that models fine-tuned on this synthetic data perform significantly better on real-world question-answering benchmarks, with analysis indicating that the synthetic data teaches LLMs to compose knowledge, a generalizable reasoning skill, particularly benefiting performance on difficult questions.
本文针对大型语言模型在多跳推理任务中强化学习微调所需数据成本高且现有来源受限的问题，提出使用规则生成的合成数据作为更经济的替代方案。方法是在仅包含虚构知识的合成数据上对LLMs进行微调，而非依赖昂贵的人工标注、易产生幻觉的LLM生成数据或不准确的LLM验证器。实验结果表明，基于合成数据微调的模型在真实世界问答基准测试中表现显著更优，分析发现合成数据教会了LLMs组合知识这一可泛化的推理技能，尤其在困难问题上提升了性能。
Accelerating PDE Surrogates via RL-Guided Mesh Optimization
Authors: Yang Meng, Ruoxi Jiang, Zhuokai Zhao, Chong Liu, Rebecca Willett, Yuxin Chen
First: 2026-03-02T16:55:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T16:55:08+00:00
Comments: Accepted at AISTATS 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Deep surrogate models for parametric partial differential equations (PDEs) can deliver high-fidelity approximations but remain prohibitively data-hungry: training often requires thousands of fine-grid simulations, each incurring substantial computational cost. To address this challenge, we introduce RLMesh, an end-to-end framework for efficient surrogate training under limited simulation budget. The key idea is to use reinforcement learning (RL) to adaptively allocate mesh grid points non-uniformly within each simulation domain, focusing numerical resolution in regions most critical for accurate PDE solutions. A lightweight proxy model further accelerates RL training by providing efficient reward estimates without full surrogate retraining. Experiments on PDE benchmarks demonstrate that RLMesh achieves competitive accuracy to baselines but with substantially fewer simulation queries. These results show that solver-level spatial adaptivity can dramatically improve the efficiency of surrogate training pipelines, enabling practical deployment of learning-based PDE surrogates across a wide range of problems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于强化学习网格优化的偏微分方程代理模型加速方法
参数化偏微分方程（PDE）的深度代理模型虽能提供高保真近似，但其训练过程仍受制于海量数据需求：通常需要数千次精细网格模拟，每次均产生高昂计算成本。为应对这一挑战，我们提出RLMesh——一种在有限模拟预算下实现高效代理训练的端到端框架。其核心思想是运用强化学习（RL）在模拟域内非均匀自适应分配网格点，将数值分辨率集中于对PDE解精度最关键的区域。轻量级代理模型通过提供无需完整重训练的高效奖励估计，进一步加速RL训练过程。在PDE基准测试中，RLMesh以显著更少的模拟查询量达到了与基线模型相当的精度。这些结果表明，求解器层面的空间自适应性能极大提升代理训练流程的效率，为基于学习的PDE代理模型在广泛问题中的实际部署提供了可能。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the high computational cost of training deep surrogate models for parametric PDEs, which typically require thousands of expensive fine-grid simulations. To reduce this burden, the authors propose RLMesh, an end-to-end framework that uses reinforcement learning to adaptively allocate mesh grid points non-uniformly, concentrating resolution in regions critical for accurate PDE solutions, and employs a lightweight proxy model to accelerate RL training by estimating rewards efficiently. Experimental results on PDE benchmarks show that RLMesh achieves competitive accuracy compared to baselines while using substantially fewer simulation queries, demonstrating that solver-level spatial adaptivity can significantly enhance the efficiency of surrogate training pipelines for broader practical deployment.
该论文针对参数化偏微分方程深度代理模型训练计算成本高的问题，通常需要数千次昂贵的细网格模拟。为降低这一负担，作者提出了RLMesh端到端框架，利用强化学习自适应地非均匀分配网格点，将数值分辨率集中在关键区域以提高PDE求解精度，并通过轻量级代理模型高效估计奖励以加速强化学习训练。在PDE基准测试中的实验结果表明，RLMesh在达到与基线方法相当精度的同时，显著减少了模拟查询次数，证明求解器级别的空间自适应能大幅提升代理训练流程的效率，从而促进基于学习的PDE代理模型在更广泛问题中的实际应用。
Expanding LLM Agent Boundaries with Strategy-Guided Exploration
Authors: Andrew Szot, Michael Kirchhof, Omar Attia, Alexander Toshev
First: 2026-03-02T16:28:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T16:28:39+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) has demonstrated notable success in post-training large language models (LLMs) as agents for tasks such as computer use, tool calling, and coding. However, exploration remains a central challenge in RL for LLM agents, especially as they operate in language-action spaces with complex observations and sparse outcome rewards. In this work, we address exploration for LLM agents by leveraging the ability of LLMs to plan and reason in language about the environment to shift exploration from low-level actions to higher-level language strategies. We thus propose Strategy-Guided Exploration (SGE), which first generates a concise natural-language strategy that describes what to do to make progress toward the goal, and then generates environment actions conditioned on that strategy. By exploring in the space of strategies rather than the space of actions, SGE induces structured and diverse exploration that targets different environment outcomes. To increase strategy diversity during RL, SGE introduces mixed-temperature sampling, which explores diverse strategies in parallel, along with a strategy reflection process that grounds strategy generation on the outcomes of previous strategies in the environment. Across UI interaction, tool-calling, coding, and embodied agent environments, SGE consistently outperforms exploration-focused RL baselines, improving both learning efficiency and final performance. We show that SGE enables the agent to learn to solve tasks too difficult for the base model.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过策略引导探索拓展LLM智能体边界
强化学习（RL）在将大型语言模型（LLM）作为智能体进行计算机操作、工具调用和编码等任务的后训练中已取得显著成功。然而，探索仍是LLM智能体强化学习的核心挑战，尤其是在其运作于具有复杂观察和稀疏结果奖励的语言-动作空间时。本研究通过利用LLM在语言层面进行环境规划与推理的能力，将探索从底层动作转移到高层语言策略，从而解决LLM智能体的探索问题。我们提出策略引导探索（SGE），该方法首先生成简洁的自然语言策略，描述如何朝着目标取得进展，然后基于该策略生成环境动作。通过在策略空间而非动作空间进行探索，SGE实现了针对不同环境结果的结构化、多样化探索。为增强强化学习过程中的策略多样性，SGE引入混合温度采样以并行探索多样化策略，并结合策略反思过程，使策略生成基于先前策略在环境中的实际结果。在UI交互、工具调用、编码和具身智能体环境中，SGE始终优于以探索为核心的强化学习基线方法，提升了学习效率和最终性能。研究表明，SGE使智能体能够学会解决基础模型难以完成的任务。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the exploration challenge in reinforcement learning (RL) for large language model (LLM) agents, which often struggle in complex language-action spaces with sparse rewards. The method proposed, Strategy-Guided Exploration (SGE), shifts exploration from low-level actions to higher-level natural-language strategies by first generating a concise strategy describing how to progress toward a goal, then conditioning environment actions on it; to enhance diversity, SGE employs mixed-temperature sampling for parallel strategy exploration and a reflection process that grounds new strategies on past outcomes. Experimental results across UI interaction, tool-calling, coding, and embodied agent environments show that SGE consistently outperforms exploration-focused RL baselines in both learning efficiency and final performance, enabling agents to solve tasks beyond the capabilities of the base model.
本研究的动机是解决大型语言模型（LLM）智能体在强化学习（RL）中的探索难题，这些智能体在具有稀疏奖励的复杂语言-动作空间中常面临挑战。所提出的方法——策略引导探索（SGE）——将探索从低层动作转向高层自然语言策略，首先生成描述如何向目标推进的简洁策略，然后基于该策略生成环境动作；为增强多样性，SGE采用混合温度采样进行并行策略探索，并通过反思过程使新策略基于过往结果。在UI交互、工具调用、编码和具身智能体环境中的实验结果表明，SGE在学习和最终性能上均持续优于以探索为重点的RL基线方法，使智能体能够解决基础模型难以完成的任务。
Reason Like a Radiologist: Chain-of-Thought and Reinforcement Learning for Verifiable Report Generation
Authors: Peiyuan Jing, Kinhei Lee, Zhenxuan Zhang, Huichi Zhou, Zhengqing Yuan, Zhifan Gao, Lei Zhu, Giorgos Papanastasiou, Yingying Fang, Guang Yang
First: 2025-04-25T16:05:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T16:27:49+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Radiology report generation is critical for efficiency but current models lack the structured reasoning of experts, hindering clinical trust and explainability by failing to link visual findings to precise anatomical locations. This paper introduces BoxMed-RL, a groundbreaking unified training framework for generating spatially verifiable and explainable radiology reports. Built on a large vision-language model, BoxMed-RL revolutionizes report generation through two integrated phases: (1) In the Pretraining Phase, we refine the model via medical concept learning, using Chain-of-Thought supervision to internalize the radiologist-like workflow, followed by spatially verifiable reinforcement, which applies reinforcement learning to align medical findings with bounding boxes. (2) In the Downstream Adapter Phase, we freeze the pretrained weights and train a downstream adapter to ensure fluent and clinically credible reports. This framework precisely mimics radiologists' workflow, compelling the model to connect high-level medical concepts with definitive anatomical evidence. Extensive experiments on public datasets demonstrate that BoxMed-RL achieves an average 7% improvement in both METEOR and ROUGE-L metrics compared to state-of-the-art methods. An average 5% improvement in large language model-based metrics further underscores BoxMed-RL's robustness in generating high-quality radiology reports.
中文标题/摘要
标题：像放射科医生一样推理：用于可验证报告生成的思维链与强化学习
放射学报告生成对提升效率至关重要，但现有模型缺乏专家式的结构化推理能力，因未能将影像发现与精确解剖位置关联，阻碍了临床可信度与可解释性。本文提出BoxMed-RL——一个开创性的统一训练框架，用于生成空间可验证且可解释的放射学报告。该框架基于大型视觉语言模型构建，通过两个集成阶段革新报告生成：(1) 预训练阶段：通过医学概念学习优化模型，采用思维链监督内化类放射科医生工作流，随后进行空间可验证强化——运用强化学习将医学发现与边界框对齐；(2) 下游适配器阶段：冻结预训练权重并训练下游适配器，确保生成流畅且临床可信的报告。该框架精准模拟放射科医生工作流，迫使模型将高层医学概念与明确解剖证据相关联。在公开数据集上的大量实验表明，BoxMed-RL在METEOR和ROUGE-L指标上平均优于现有最优方法7%。基于大语言模型的指标平均提升5%，进一步印证了BoxMed-RL生成高质量放射学报告的鲁棒性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to enhance clinical trust and explainability in radiology report generation, which current models lack by failing to link visual findings to precise anatomical locations, this paper proposes BoxMed-RL, a unified training framework that integrates Chain-of-Thought supervision and reinforcement learning to mimic radiologists' structured reasoning. The method involves a pretraining phase where the model learns medical concepts and aligns findings with bounding boxes via reinforcement, followed by a downstream adapter phase to generate fluent reports, ensuring spatial verifiability. Experimental results on public datasets show that BoxMed-RL achieves an average 7% improvement in METEOR and ROUGE-L metrics over state-of-the-art methods, with a 5% gain in LLM-based metrics, demonstrating robust performance in generating high-quality, explainable reports.
本文的动机是解决当前放射学报告生成模型缺乏结构化推理、难以将视觉发现与精确解剖位置关联的问题，从而提升临床可信度和可解释性。为此，提出了BoxMed-RL这一统一训练框架，该方法基于大型视觉语言模型，通过预训练阶段结合思维链监督和强化学习来学习医学概念并实现空间可验证性，再在下游适配器阶段生成流畅报告，以模拟放射科医生的工作流程。在公开数据集上的实验结果表明，BoxMed-RL在METEOR和ROUGE-L指标上平均提升了7%，在基于大语言模型的指标上平均提升了5%，验证了其在生成高质量、可验证报告方面的有效性。
AgentMath: Empowering Mathematical Reasoning for Large Language Models via Tool-Augmented Agent
Authors: Haipeng Luo, Huawen Feng, Qingfeng Sun, Can Xu, Kai Zheng, Yufei Wang, Tao Yang, Han Hu, Yansong Tang
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-12-23T19:57:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T16:15:29+00:00
Comments: This paper has been accepted to ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Reasoning Models (LRMs) like o3 and DeepSeek-R1 have achieved remarkable progress in reasoning tasks with long cot. However, they remain computationally inefficient and struggle with accuracy when solving problems requiring complex mathematical operations. In this work, we present AgentMath, an agent framework that seamlessly integrates language models' reasoning capabilities with code interpreters' computational precision to efficiently tackle complex mathematical problems. Our approach introduces three key innovations: (1) An automated method that converts natural language chain-of-thought into structured tool-augmented trajectories, generating high-quality supervised fine-tuning (SFT) data to alleviate data scarcity; (2) A novel agentic reinforcement learning (RL) paradigm that dynamically interleaves natural language generation with real-time code execution. This enables models to autonomously learn optimal tool-use strategies through multi-round interactive feedback, while fostering emergent capabilities in code refinement and error correction; (3) An efficient training system incorporating innovative techniques, including request-level asynchronous rollout scheduling, agentic partial rollout, and prefix-aware weighted load balancing, achieving 4-5x speedup and making efficient RL training feasible on ultra-long sequences with scenarios with massive tool invocation. The evaluations show that AgentMath achieves state-of-the-art performance on challenging mathematical competition benchmarks including AIME24, AIME25, and HMMT25. Specifically, AgentMath-30B-A3B attains 90.6%, 86.4%, and 73.8% accuracy respectively, surpassing OpenAI-o3-mini and Claude-Opus-4.0-Thinking while remaining competitive with OpenAI-o3, Gemini-2.5-Pro, and DeepSeek-R1-671B-0528.These results validate the effectiveness of our approach and pave the way for building scalable mathematical reasoning agents.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AgentMath：通过工具增强智能体赋能大语言模型的数学推理能力
如o3和DeepSeek-R1等大型推理模型在长链思维推理任务中取得了显著进展，但其计算效率仍显不足，且在解决需要复杂数学运算的问题时准确性受限。本研究提出AgentMath——一个将语言模型的推理能力与代码解释器的计算精度无缝整合的智能体框架，以高效处理复杂数学问题。我们的方法包含三项关键创新：（1）一种自动化方法，将自然语言思维链转化为结构化工具增强轨迹，生成高质量监督微调数据以缓解数据稀缺问题；（2）一种新颖的智能体强化学习范式，动态交织自然语言生成与实时代码执行，使模型能通过多轮交互反馈自主学习最优工具使用策略，同时激发代码优化与错误修正的涌现能力；（3）一个高效训练系统，融合请求级异步推演调度、智能体部分推演及前缀感知加权负载均衡等创新技术，实现4-5倍加速，使超长序列场景下的大规模工具调用强化学习训练成为可能。评估表明，AgentMath在AIME24、AIME25和HMMT25等数学竞赛基准测试中达到最先进性能。具体而言，AgentMath-30B-A3B分别取得90.6%、86.4%和73.8%的准确率，超越OpenAI-o3-mini与Claude-Opus-4.0-Thinking，并与OpenAI-o3、Gemini-2.5-Pro及DeepSeek-R1-671B-0528保持竞争力。这些结果验证了我们方法的有效性，为构建可扩展数学推理智能体开辟了道路。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the computational inefficiency and accuracy limitations of large reasoning models in complex mathematical tasks, this paper introduces AgentMath, an agent framework that integrates language models' reasoning with code interpreters' computational precision. The method features three innovations: an automated conversion of natural language chain-of-thought into structured tool-augmented trajectories for high-quality SFT data, a novel agentic reinforcement learning paradigm enabling dynamic interleaving of natural language generation with real-time code execution to learn tool-use strategies, and an efficient training system with techniques like asynchronous rollout scheduling for 4-5x speedup. Experimental results show state-of-the-art performance on benchmarks including AIME24, AIME25, and HMMT25, with AgentMath-30B-A3B achieving accuracies of 90.6%, 86.4%, and 73.8%, surpassing models like OpenAI-o3-mini and Claude-Opus-4.0-Thinking while remaining competitive with top-tier models.
本研究针对大型推理模型在复杂数学问题中计算效率低和准确性不足的问题，提出了AgentMath框架，将语言模型的推理能力与代码解释器的计算精度相结合。方法包含三项创新：自动将自然语言思维链转化为结构化工具增强轨迹以生成高质量监督微调数据；一种新型智能体强化学习范式，动态交织自然语言生成与实时代码执行，使模型能通过多轮交互反馈自主学习最优工具使用策略；以及一个高效训练系统，采用异步推出调度等技术实现4-5倍加速。实验结果表明，在AIME24、AIME25和HMMT25等数学竞赛基准上，AgentMath-30B-A3B分别达到90.6%、86.4%和73.8%的准确率，超越了OpenAI-o3-mini和Claude-Opus-4.0-Thinking等模型，并与顶尖模型保持竞争力。
Temporal Representations for Exploration: Learning Complex Exploratory Behavior without Extrinsic Rewards
Authors: Faisal Mohamed, Catherine Ji, Benjamin Eysenbach, Glen Berseth
First: 2026-03-02T15:55:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T15:55:27+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Effective exploration in reinforcement learning requires not only tracking where an agent has been, but also understanding how the agent perceives and represents the world. To learn powerful representations, an agent should actively explore states that contribute to its knowledge of the environment. Temporal representations can capture the information necessary to solve a wide range of potential tasks while avoiding the computational cost associated with full state reconstruction. In this paper, we propose an exploration method that leverages temporal contrastive representations to guide exploration, prioritizing states with unpredictable future outcomes. We demonstrate that such representations can enable the learning of complex exploratory x in locomotion, manipulation, and embodied-AI tasks, revealing capabilities and behaviors that traditionally require extrinsic rewards. Unlike approaches that rely on explicit distance learning or episodic memory mechanisms (e.g., quasimetric-based methods), our method builds directly on temporal similarities, yielding a simpler yet effective strategy for exploration.
中文标题/摘要
标题：时序表征探索：无需外部奖励学习复杂探索行为
强化学习中的有效探索不仅需要追踪智能体的历史轨迹，还需理解其对环境的感知与表征方式。为学习强表征能力，智能体应主动探索能增进环境认知的状态。时序表征能捕获解决广泛潜在任务所需的信息，同时避免完整状态重建的计算开销。本文提出一种利用时序对比表征引导探索的方法，优先选择未来结果难以预测的状态。实验表明，此类表征能在运动控制、操作任务及具身AI中实现复杂探索行为的学习，揭示传统依赖外部奖励才能展现的能力。与依赖显式距离学习或情景记忆机制（如拟度量方法）的方法不同，本方法直接基于时序相似性构建，形成更简洁高效的探索策略。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the need for effective exploration in reinforcement learning that goes beyond tracking visited states to learning how an agent represents the world, aiming to acquire representations useful for a broad range of tasks without the cost of full state reconstruction. The method introduces an exploration strategy that uses temporal contrastive representations to prioritize states with unpredictable future outcomes, leveraging temporal similarities rather than explicit distance metrics or episodic memory. Experimental results show this approach enables learning complex exploratory behaviors in locomotion, manipulation, and embodied-AI tasks without extrinsic rewards, demonstrating capabilities typically requiring reward signals and offering a simpler yet effective alternative to methods like quasimetric-based techniques.
本文的动机是强化学习中需要超越简单追踪访问状态的有效探索，以学习智能体如何表征世界，旨在获取适用于广泛任务且无需完整状态重建成本的表示。该方法提出了一种利用时序对比表示的探索策略，优先考虑未来结果不可预测的状态，基于时序相似性而非显式距离度量或情景记忆。实验结果表明，该方法能够在没有外部奖励的情况下，在运动、操作和具身人工智能任务中学习复杂的探索行为，展示了通常需要奖励信号才能实现的能力，并为类度量方法等提供了更简单有效的替代方案。
CharacterFlywheel: Scaling Iterative Improvement of Engaging and Steerable LLMs in Production
Authors: Yixin Nie, Lin Guan, Zhongyao Ma, Anchit Gupta, Yipin Zhou, Xiao Li, Zhengping Zhou, Raymond Zeng, Gelin Zhou, Shigan Chu, Ajay Thampi, Wancen Mu, Nathan Shuster, Ketong Wang, Lin Chen, Jason Brewer, Derek Hao Hu, Alexander McCauley, Jason Weston, Sem Park, Na Zhang, Kevin Tang
First: 2026-03-02T15:27:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T15:27:31+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This report presents CharacterFlywheel, an iterative flywheel process for improving large language models (LLMs) in production social chat applications across Instagram, WhatsApp, and Messenger. Starting from LLaMA 3.1, we refined models across 15 generations using data from both internal and external real-user traffic. Through continuous deployments from July 2024 to April 2025, we conducted controlled 7-day A/B tests showing consistent engagement improvements: 7 of 8 newly deployed models demonstrated positive lift over the baseline, with the strongest performers achieving up to 8.8% improvement in engagement breadth and 19.4% in engagement depth. We also observed substantial gains in steerability, with instruction following increasing from 59.2% to 84.8% and instruction violations decreasing from 26.6% to 5.8%. We detail the CharacterFlywheel process which integrates data curation, reward modeling to estimate and interpolate the landscape of engagement metrics, supervised fine-tuning (SFT), reinforcement learning (RL), and both offline and online evaluation to ensure reliable progress at each optimization step. We also discuss our methods for overfitting prevention and navigating production dynamics at scale. These contributions advance the scientific rigor and understanding of LLMs in social applications serving millions of users.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CharacterFlywheel：规模化迭代优化生产环境中引人入胜且可操控的大语言模型
本报告介绍了CharacterFlywheel，一种用于在Instagram、WhatsApp和Messenger等生产环境社交聊天应用中迭代优化大语言模型（LLM）的飞轮流程。基于LLaMA 3.1，我们利用内部和外部真实用户流量数据，历经15代模型精炼。通过2024年7月至2025年4月的持续部署，我们进行了为期7天的对照A/B测试，结果显示参与度持续提升：8个新部署模型中有7个较基线表现正向提升，最优模型在参与广度上提升达8.8%，参与深度提升达19.4%。同时，模型可操控性显著增强：指令遵循率从59.2%提升至84.8%，指令违规率从26.6%降至5.8%。我们详细阐述了整合数据筛选、奖励建模（用于评估和插值参与度指标）、监督微调（SFT）、强化学习（RL）以及离线和在线评估的CharacterFlywheel流程，确保每个优化步骤的可靠进展。我们还讨论了预防过拟合及应对大规模生产动态的方法。这些成果提升了服务数百万用户的社交应用中LLM研究的科学严谨性与认知水平。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind CharacterFlywheel is to systematically enhance the engagement and steerability of large language models (LLMs) in real-world social chat applications across platforms like Instagram, WhatsApp, and Messenger. The method involves an iterative flywheel process starting from LLaMA 3.1, refining models over 15 generations using real-user data, and integrating data curation, reward modeling for engagement metrics, supervised fine-tuning, reinforcement learning, and rigorous offline and online evaluation to prevent overfitting and manage production dynamics. The main experimental results from controlled A/B tests from July 2024 to April 2025 show consistent improvements: 7 out of 8 newly deployed models achieved positive engagement lift, with top performers reaching up to 8.8% improvement in engagement breadth and 19.4% in depth, alongside substantial steerability gains where instruction following increased from 59.2% to 84.8% and violations decreased from 26.6% to 5.8%.
CharacterFlywheel 的动机在于系统性地提升大型语言模型（LLMs）在 Instagram、WhatsApp 和 Messenger 等真实社交聊天应用中的参与度和可操控性。该方法采用了一种迭代飞轮流程，从 LLaMA 3.1 出发，利用内部和外部真实用户数据对模型进行了 15 代优化，并整合了数据整理、用于评估和插值参与度指标的奖励建模、监督微调、强化学习以及严格的离线和在线评估，以防止过拟合并应对大规模生产动态。2024年7月至2025年4月期间的受控A/B测试主要实验结果显示：在8个新部署的模型中，有7个实现了相对于基线的正向提升，表现最佳的模型在参与广度上提升了8.8%，在参与深度上提升了19.4%；同时，可操控性也获得显著改善，指令遵循率从59.2%提高到84.8%，指令违规率从26.6%降至5.8%。
Sample-efficient and Scalable Exploration in Continuous-Time RL
Authors: Klemens Iten, Lenart Treven, Bhavya Sukhija, Florian Dörfler, Andreas Krause
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-10-28T14:54:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T15:08:43+00:00
Comments: 28 pages, 8 figures, 6 tables. Published as a conference paper at ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning algorithms are typically designed for discrete-time dynamics, even though the underlying real-world control systems are often continuous in time. In this paper, we study the problem of continuous-time reinforcement learning, where the unknown system dynamics are represented using nonlinear ordinary differential equations (ODEs). We leverage probabilistic models, such as Gaussian processes and Bayesian neural networks, to learn an uncertainty-aware model of the underlying ODE. Our algorithm, COMBRL, greedily maximizes a weighted sum of the extrinsic reward and model epistemic uncertainty. This yields a scalable and sample-efficient approach to continuous-time model-based RL. We show that COMBRL achieves sublinear regret in the reward-driven setting, and in the unsupervised RL setting (i.e., without extrinsic rewards), we provide a sample complexity bound. In our experiments, we evaluate COMBRL in both standard and unsupervised RL settings and demonstrate that it scales better, is more sample-efficient than prior methods, and outperforms baselines across several deep RL tasks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：连续时间强化学习中的高效样本与可扩展探索
强化学习算法通常针对离散时间动态设计，而现实世界的底层控制系统往往是连续时间的。本文研究连续时间强化学习问题，其中未知系统动态通过非线性常微分方程（ODE）表示。我们利用高斯过程和贝叶斯神经网络等概率模型，学习具有不确定性感知的底层ODE模型。所提出的COMBRL算法通过贪婪最大化外部奖励与模型认知不确定性的加权和，实现了可扩展且样本高效的连续时间基于模型的强化学习方法。我们证明COMBRL在奖励驱动场景下能实现次线性遗憾，在无监督强化学习场景（即无外部奖励）中提供了样本复杂度界限。实验部分在标准和无监督强化学习场景中评估COMBRL，结果表明该方法比现有方法具有更好的可扩展性、更高的样本效率，并在多项深度强化学习任务中超越基线模型。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the gap between discrete-time RL algorithms and the continuous-time nature of real-world control systems, this paper introduces COMBRL, a model-based RL method for environments governed by nonlinear ODEs. The method employs probabilistic models like Gaussian processes to learn an uncertainty-aware dynamics model and greedily optimizes a combination of extrinsic reward and model uncertainty. Experimental results demonstrate that COMBRL achieves sublinear regret, provides sample complexity bounds in unsupervised settings, and outperforms prior methods in scalability and sample efficiency across several deep RL tasks.
针对离散时间强化学习算法与现实世界连续时间控制系统的差异，本文提出了COMBRL，一种用于非线性常微分方程环境下的基于模型的强化学习方法。该方法采用高斯过程等概率模型来学习具有不确定性感知的动态模型，并贪婪地优化外部奖励与模型不确定性的加权组合。实验结果表明，COMBRL实现了次线性遗憾，在无监督设置中提供了样本复杂度界限，并在多个深度强化学习任务中展现出优于先前方法的可扩展性和样本效率。
Stable Asynchrony: Variance-Controlled Off-Policy RL for LLMs
Authors: Luke J. Huang, Zhuoyang Zhang, Qinghao Hu, Shang Yang, Song Han
First: 2026-02-19T18:40:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T14:57:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Asynchronous reinforcement learning has become increasingly central to scaling LLM post-training, delivering major throughput gains by decoupling rollout generation from policy updates. However, widely used policy-gradient objectives such as REINFORCE and GRPO suffer under high asynchrony: stale rollouts produce heavy-tailed importance weights, so a small number of trajectories dominate updates and the policy-gradient estimator becomes markedly higher variance. Through systematic analysis on math, reasoning, and tool-use benchmarks, we find that this increasing variance is reliably predicted by collapsing effective sample size (ESS), which prior stabilization methods largely fail to address. Motivated by this diagnosis, we introduce $\textbf{V}$ariance $\textbf{C}$ontrolled $\textbf{P}$olicy $\textbf{O}$ptimization ($\textbf{VCPO}$), a method that (i) dynamically scales the learning rate with ESS to dampen unreliable updates and (ii) applies a closed-form minimum-variance baseline for off-policy settings, without a critic model and adding minimal overhead. Empirically, across math and general reasoning benchmarks, this enables robustly stable asynchronous training compared to previous stabilization and algorithmic methods, even in highly off-policy regimes (128 steps off-policy). In a long-horizon, tool-use task, VCPO matches synchronous performance while delivering a 2.5$\times$ speedup in training time. Code is available at: https://github.com/mit-han-lab/vcpo
中文标题/摘要
标题：稳定异步：面向大语言模型的方差控制离策略强化学习
异步强化学习在大语言模型后训练规模化中日益重要，通过解耦轨迹生成与策略更新显著提升训练吞吐量。然而，REINFORCE、GRPO等广泛使用的策略梯度目标在高异步环境下存在缺陷：过时轨迹产生重尾重要性权重，导致少量轨迹主导更新，策略梯度估计器方差显著增大。通过对数学、推理和工具使用基准的系统分析，我们发现有效样本量（ESS）的衰减可可靠预测方差增长，而现有稳定方法大多未能解决此问题。基于此诊断，我们提出方差控制策略优化（VCPO）方法：（1）根据ESS动态缩放学习率以抑制不可靠更新；（2）为离策略场景应用闭式最小方差基线，无需评论家模型且开销极小。实验表明，在数学与通用推理基准上，相比先前的稳定方法与算法，VCPO能在高度离策略场景（128步离策略）下实现鲁棒的稳定异步训练。在长时程工具使用任务中，VCPO在保持同步训练性能的同时，将训练速度提升2.5倍。代码已开源：https://github.com/mit-han-lab/vcpo
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the challenge that high asynchrony in reinforcement learning for large language models leads to high variance in policy-gradient estimators due to stale rollouts, which prior stabilization methods fail to address. The method proposed, Variance Controlled Policy Optimization (VCPO), dynamically scales the learning rate based on effective sample size and applies a minimum-variance baseline for off-policy settings without a critic model. Experimental results on math, reasoning, and tool-use benchmarks show that VCPO enables stable asynchronous training even under high off-policy conditions, matching synchronous performance while achieving a 2.5× speedup in training time for a tool-use task.
本文的动机在于，大型语言模型强化学习中的高异步性会导致策略梯度估计器因过时数据而产生高方差，而现有稳定方法未能解决此问题。提出的方法称为方差控制策略优化（VCPO），它根据有效样本量动态调整学习率，并应用一种无需评论家模型的最小方差基线来处理离策略场景。在数学、推理和工具使用基准测试中的实验结果表明，VCPO能在高度离策略条件下实现稳定的异步训练，在工具使用任务中匹配同步训练性能的同时，将训练时间加速了2.5倍。
CoVe: Training Interactive Tool-Use Agents via Constraint-Guided Verification
Authors: Jinpeng Chen, Cheng Gong, Hanbo Li, Ziru Liu, Zichen Tian, Xinyu Fu, Shi Wu, Chenyang Zhang, Wu Zhang, Suiyun Zhang, Dandan Tu, Rui Liu
First: 2026-03-02T14:56:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T14:56:35+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Developing multi-turn interactive tool-use agents is challenging because real-world user needs are often complex and ambiguous, yet agents must execute deterministic actions to satisfy them. To address this gap, we introduce \textbf{CoVe} (\textbf{Co}nstraint-\textbf{Ve}rification), a post-training data synthesis framework designed for training interactive tool-use agents while ensuring both data complexity and correctness. CoVe begins by defining explicit task constraints, which serve a dual role: they guide the generation of complex trajectories and act as deterministic verifiers for assessing trajectory quality. This enables the creation of high-quality training trajectories for supervised fine-tuning (SFT) and the derivation of accurate reward signals for reinforcement learning (RL). Our evaluation on the challenging $τ^2$-bench benchmark demonstrates the effectiveness of the framework. Notably, our compact \textbf{CoVe-4B} model achieves success rates of 43.0\% and 59.4\% in the Airline and Retail domains, respectively; its overall performance significantly outperforms strong baselines of similar scale and remains competitive with models up to $17\times$ its size. These results indicate that CoVe provides an effective and efficient pathway for synthesizing training data for state-of-the-art interactive tool-use agents. To support future research, we open-source our code, trained model, and the full set of 12K high-quality trajectories used for training.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CoVe：基于约束引导验证的交互式工具使用智能体训练方法
开发多轮交互式工具使用智能体具有挑战性，因为真实场景中的用户需求通常复杂且模糊，而智能体必须执行确定性操作以满足需求。为弥合这一差距，我们提出 **CoVe**（约束验证），一种专为训练交互式工具使用智能体设计的后训练数据合成框架，确保数据复杂性与正确性。CoVe 首先定义明确的任务约束，这些约束具有双重作用：引导生成复杂轨迹，并作为确定性验证器评估轨迹质量。该方法能生成用于监督微调的高质量训练轨迹，并为强化学习提供精确奖励信号。在挑战性基准 $τ^2$-bench 上的评估验证了框架有效性：紧凑的 **CoVe-4B** 模型在航空和零售领域分别达到 43.0% 和 59.4% 的成功率，整体性能显著超越同规模基线模型，并与规模达其 17 倍的模型保持竞争力。结果表明，CoVe 为前沿交互式工具使用智能体提供了一种高效训练数据合成路径。为支持后续研究，我们开源了代码、训练模型及用于训练的 12K 条高质量完整轨迹集。

Efficient RLVR Training via Weighted Mutual Information Data Selection
Authors: Xinyu Zhou, Boyu Zhu, Haotian Zhang, Huiming Wang, Zhijiang Guo
First: 2026-03-02T14:25:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T14:25:07+00:00
Comments: 15 Pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) plays a central role in improving the reasoning and alignment of large language models, yet its efficiency critically depends on how training data are selected. Existing online selection strategies predominantly rely on difficulty-based heuristics, favouring datapoints with intermediate success rates, implicitly equating difficulty with informativeness and neglecting epistemic uncertainty arising from limited evidence. We introduce InSight, an INformation-guided data SamplInG metHod for RL Training, grounded in a weighted mutual information objective. By modeling data outcomes with Bayesian latent success rates, we show that expected uncertainty reduction decomposes into complementary difficulty- and evidence-dependent components, revealing a fundamental limitation of difficulty-only selection. Leveraging this observation, InSight constructs a stable acquisition score based on the mean belief of datapoints' success rather than noisy sampled outcomes, and naturally extends to multi-rollout settings common in reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR). Extensive experiments demonstrate that InSight consistently achieves state-of-the-art performance and improves training efficiency, including a +1.41 average gain on Planning & Mathmatics benchmarks, +1.01 improvement on general reasoning, and up to ~2.2x acceleration, with negligible additional computational overhead.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于加权互信息数据选择的高效RLVR训练方法
强化学习在提升大语言模型的推理与对齐能力中发挥核心作用，但其效率关键取决于训练数据的选择策略。现有在线选择方法主要依赖基于难度的启发式规则，偏好中等成功率的样本，隐含地将难度等同于信息量，却忽视了有限证据导致的认识不确定性。本文提出InSight——一种基于加权互信息目标的强化训练信息引导采样方法。通过贝叶斯潜在成功率建模数据结果，我们证明预期不确定性降低可分解为难度相关与证据相关的互补成分，从而揭示纯难度选择策略的根本局限。基于此发现，InSight构建了以数据点成功率的均值置信（而非噪声采样结果）为核心的稳定获取分数，并可自然扩展至可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）常见的多轮次场景。大量实验表明：InSight持续取得最先进性能并提升训练效率，在规划与数学基准上平均提升+1.41，通用推理任务提升+1.01，加速比最高达约2.2倍，且额外计算开销可忽略。

This paper addresses the inefficiency of existing difficulty-based data selection methods in reinforcement learning for language models, which overlook epistemic uncertainty. The authors propose InSight, a method that uses a weighted mutual information objective to model data outcomes with Bayesian latent success rates, decomposing uncertainty reduction into difficulty- and evidence-dependent components and constructing a stable acquisition score based on mean belief. Experimental results show that InSight achieves state-of-the-art performance, with average gains of +1.41 on Planning & Mathematics benchmarks and +1.01 on general reasoning, along with up to ~2.2x training acceleration and minimal computational overhead.
本文针对强化学习中现有基于难度的数据选择方法效率低下、忽略认知不确定性的问题，提出了一种名为InSight的方法。该方法基于加权互信息目标，通过贝叶斯潜在成功率建模数据结果，将不确定性减少分解为难度和证据依赖的组成部分，并基于平均信念构建稳定的获取分数。实验结果表明，InSight在规划和数学基准上平均提升1.41分，在一般推理上提升1.01分，训练速度最高加速约2.2倍，且计算开销可忽略不计，实现了最先进的性能。
SEAR: Sample Efficient Action Chunking Reinforcement Learning
Authors: C. F. Maximilian Nagy, Onur Celik, Emiliyan Gospodinov, Florian Seligmann, Weiran Liao, Aryan Kaushik, Gerhard Neumann
First: 2026-03-02T14:11:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T14:11:53+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Action chunking can improve exploration and value estimation in long horizon reinforcement learning, but makes learning substantially harder since the critic must evaluate action sequences rather than single actions, greatly increasing approximation and data efficiency challenges. As a result, existing action chunking methods, primarily designed for the offline and offline-to-online settings, have not achieved strong performance in purely online reinforcement learning. We introduce SEAR, an off policy online reinforcement learning algorithm for action chunking. It exploits the temporal structure of action chunks and operates with a receding horizon, effectively combining the benefits of small and large chunk sizes. SEAR outperforms state of the art online reinforcement learning methods on Metaworld, training with chunk sizes up to 20.
中文标题/摘要

动作分块可提升长时程强化学习中的探索与价值估计能力，但由于需评估动作序列而非单一动作，大幅增加了近似误差与数据效率的挑战，使学习难度显著上升。现有动作分块方法主要针对离线及离线转在线场景，在纯在线强化学习中尚未取得优异性能。本文提出SEAR——一种面向动作分块的离线策略在线强化学习算法。该算法利用动作分块的时间结构，采用滑动时域机制运行，有效融合了不同分块尺寸的优势。在Metaworld环境中，SEAR以最高达20的分块尺寸进行训练，其性能超越了当前最先进的在线强化学习方法。

It introduces SEAR, an off-policy online algorithm that leverages the temporal structure of action chunks with a receding horizon approach, effectively balancing the benefits of small and large chunk sizes. Experimental results on the Metaworld benchmark demonstrate that SEAR outperforms state-of-the-art online reinforcement learning methods, successfully training with chunk sizes as large as 20.
本文针对动作分块（将动作分组为序列以改善长视野强化学习中的探索和价值估计）在纯在线设置中应用困难的问题，现有方法因近似误差增加和数据效率低下而表现不佳。研究提出了SEAR，一种采用滚动时域策略的离策略在线算法，利用动作块的时间结构，有效结合了不同分块大小的优势。在Metaworld基准测试上的实验结果表明，SEAR优于当前最先进的在线强化学习方法，并能成功训练分块大小高达20的任务。
SPIRAL: Self-Play on Zero-Sum Games Incentivizes Reasoning via Multi-Agent Multi-Turn Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Bo Liu, Leon Guertler, Simon Yu, Zichen Liu, Penghui Qi, Daniel Balcells, Mickel Liu, Cheston Tan, Weiyan Shi, Min Lin, Wee Sun Lee, Natasha Jaques
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-06-30T17:58:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T14:09:28+00:00
Comments: Accepted at ICLR 2026. Code: https://github.com/spiral-rl/spiral
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Recent advances in reinforcement learning have shown that language models can develop sophisticated reasoning through training on tasks with verifiable rewards, but these approaches depend on human-curated problem-answer pairs and domain-specific reward engineering. We introduce SPIRAL, a self-play framework where models learn by playing multi-turn, zero-sum games against continuously improving versions of themselves, generating an automatic curriculum of stronger opponents, and eliminating the need for human supervision. To enable this self-play training at scale, we implement a fully online, multi-turn, multi-agent reinforcement learning system for LLMs and propose role-conditioned advantage estimation (RAE) to stabilize multi-agent training. SPIRAL produces reasoning capabilities that transfer broadly, improving performance by up to 10% across a suite of 8 reasoning benchmarks on 4 different models spanning Qwen and Llama model families, outperforming supervised fine-tuning on 25,000 expert game trajectories. Multi-game training (TicTacToe, Kuhn Poker, Simple Negotiation) yields the strongest results, with improvements observed across both base and instruction-tuned models. Analysis of chain-of-thought traces reveals that games develop distinct cognitive patterns that transfer to improve reasoning performance, with different games developing complementary strengths. Even models which have already been trained on reasoning tasks using RLVR, like DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-7B, still benefit from our approach. These results demonstrate that zero-sum games naturally develop transferable reasoning capabilities across diverse model architectures and training stages, highlighting a promising direction for autonomous reasoning development. Our code can be found in https://github.com/spiral-rl/spiral.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SPIRAL：基于零和博弈自我对弈通过多智能体多轮强化学习激励推理能力
近期强化学习进展表明，语言模型可通过可验证奖励任务训练发展复杂推理能力，但这些方法依赖人工标注的问题-答案对及领域特定的奖励工程。我们提出SPIRAL，一种自我对弈框架：模型通过不断与自我改进版本进行多轮零和博弈学习，自动生成更强对手的课程，无需人工监督。为实现规模化自我对弈训练，我们构建了面向大语言模型的完全在线、多轮、多智能体强化学习系统，并提出角色条件优势估计（RAE）以稳定多智能体训练。SPIRAL产生的推理能力具备广泛迁移性，在涵盖Qwen和Llama系列的4个不同模型、8项推理基准测试中性能提升最高达10%，优于基于25,000条专家博弈轨迹的监督微调。多游戏训练（井字棋、库恩扑克、简单谈判）效果最佳，在基础模型和指令微调模型中均观察到改进。思维链轨迹分析显示，博弈发展出可迁移至推理任务的独特认知模式，不同游戏形成互补优势。即使已通过RLVR进行推理训练的模型（如DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-7B）仍能受益于本方法。这些结果表明，零和博弈能自然发展出跨模型架构与训练阶段的可迁移推理能力，为自主推理发展指明新方向。代码详见https://github.com/spiral-rl/spiral。

The method employs multi-turn, zero-sum games where models train against progressively stronger versions of themselves, using a fully online multi-agent system and role-conditioned advantage estimation to stabilize training. Optimistic Task Inference for Behavior Foundation Models
Authors: Thomas Rupf, Marco Bagatella, Marin Vlastelica, Andreas Krause
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-10-23T06:36:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T14:03:42+00:00
Comments: ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Behavior Foundation Models (BFMs) are capable of retrieving high-performing policy for any reward function specified directly at test-time, commonly referred to as zero-shot reinforcement learning (RL). While this is a very efficient process in terms of compute, it can be less so in terms of data: as a standard assumption, BFMs require computing rewards over a non-negligible inference dataset, assuming either access to a functional form of rewards, or significant labeling efforts. To alleviate these limitations, we tackle the problem of task inference purely through interaction with the environment at test-time. We propose OpTI-BFM, an optimistic decision criterion that directly models uncertainty over reward functions and guides BFMs in data collection for task inference. Formally, we provide a regret bound for well-trained BFMs through a direct connection to upper-confidence algorithms for linear bandits. Empirically, we evaluate OpTI-BFM on established zero-shot benchmarks, and observe that it enables successor-features-based BFMs to identify and optimize an unseen reward function in a handful of episodes with minimal compute overhead. Code is available at https://github.com/ThomasRupf/opti-bfm.
中文标题/摘要
标题：行为基础模型的乐观任务推断
行为基础模型（BFMs）能够为测试时直接指定的任何奖励函数检索高性能策略，通常称为零样本强化学习（RL）。虽然这一过程在计算上非常高效，但在数据方面可能效率较低：根据标准假设，BFMs需要在不可忽略的推断数据集上计算奖励，这要求要么能获取奖励的函数形式，要么进行大量标注工作。为缓解这些限制，我们通过测试时与环境的纯交互来解决任务推断问题。我们提出OpTI-BFM，这是一种乐观决策准则，直接对奖励函数的不确定性进行建模，并指导BFMs为任务推断收集数据。形式上，我们通过与线性赌博机上置信界算法的直接关联，为训练良好的BFMs提供了遗憾界。实证上，我们在成熟的零样本基准上评估OpTI-BFM，观察到它使基于后继特征的BFMs能够在少量回合中以最小计算开销识别并优化未见过的奖励函数。代码发布于https://github.com/ThomasRupf/opti-bfm。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the data inefficiency of Behavior Foundation Models (BFMs) in zero-shot reinforcement learning, which typically require extensive reward computation or labeling at test time. To overcome this, the authors propose OpTI-BFM, an optimistic decision criterion that models reward uncertainty and guides BFMs to interact with the environment for task inference, drawing a theoretical connection to linear bandit algorithms with a regret bound. Experimental results on zero-shot benchmarks show that OpTI-BFM enables successor-features-based BFMs to identify and optimize unseen reward functions within a few episodes with minimal computational overhead.
本文针对行为基础模型在零样本强化学习中通常需要大量奖励计算或标注导致数据效率低下的问题，提出了一种乐观决策准则OpTI-BFM，通过建模奖励函数的不确定性来引导模型在测试时与环境交互进行任务推断，并建立了与线性赌博机算法的理论联系，提供了遗憾界。在零样本基准测试上的实验结果表明，OpTI-BFM使基于后继特征的行为基础模型能够在少量回合内以最小计算开销识别并优化未见过的奖励函数。
FIRE: Frobenius-Isometry Reinitialization for Balancing the Stability-Plasticity Tradeoff
Authors: Isaac Han, Sangyeon Park, Seungwon Oh, Donghu Kim, Hojoon Lee, Kyung-Joong Kim
Venue: ICLR oral
First: 2026-02-08T16:17:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T13:58:28+00:00
Comments: ICLR'26 (oral)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Deep neural networks trained on nonstationary data must balance stability (i.e., retaining prior knowledge) and plasticity (i.e., adapting to new tasks). Standard reinitialization methods, which reinitialize weights toward their original values, are widely used but difficult to tune: conservative reinitializations fail to restore plasticity, while aggressive ones erase useful knowledge. We propose FIRE, a principled reinitialization method that explicitly balances the stability-plasticity tradeoff. FIRE quantifies stability through Squared Frobenius Error (SFE), measuring proximity to past weights, and plasticity through Deviation from Isometry (DfI), reflecting weight isotropy. The reinitialization point is obtained by solving a constrained optimization problem, minimizing SFE subject to DfI being zero, which is efficiently approximated by Newton-Schulz iteration. FIRE is evaluated on continual visual learning (CIFAR-10 with ResNet-18), language modeling (OpenWebText with GPT-0.1B), and reinforcement learning (HumanoidBench with SAC and Atari games with DQN). Across all domains, FIRE consistently outperforms both naive training without intervention and standard reinitialization methods, demonstrating effective balancing of the stability-plasticity tradeoff.
中文标题/摘要
标题：FIRE：基于Frobenius等距重初始化的稳定性-可塑性权衡平衡方法
在非平稳数据上训练的深度神经网络需平衡稳定性（保留先验知识）与可塑性（适应新任务）。标准重初始化方法通过将权重向原始值重置被广泛使用，但难以调优：保守重置无法恢复可塑性，激进重置则会消除有用知识。本文提出FIRE——一种显式平衡稳定性-可塑性权衡的原理性重初始化方法。FIRE通过平方Frobenius误差量化稳定性（衡量与历史权重的接近程度），通过等距偏差量化可塑性（反映权重各向同性）。重初始化点通过求解约束优化问题获得：在等距偏差为零的约束下最小化平方Frobenius误差，该问题可通过牛顿-舒尔茨迭代高效近似。FIRE在持续视觉学习、语言建模和强化学习三大领域进行评估，均显著优于无干预的朴素训练及标准重初始化方法，有效实现了稳定性-可塑性的平衡。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of balancing stability and plasticity in deep neural networks trained on nonstationary data, where standard reinitialization methods are difficult to tune effectively. The authors propose FIRE, a method that quantifies stability via Squared Frobenius Error and plasticity via Deviation from Isometry, then solves a constrained optimization problem to find a reinitialization point that minimizes stability loss while ensuring plasticity. Experimental results across continual visual learning, language modeling, and reinforcement learning tasks show that FIRE consistently outperforms both naive training and standard reinitialization methods, effectively balancing the tradeoff.
本文针对在非平稳数据上训练的深度神经网络中平衡稳定性与可塑性的挑战，提出FIRE方法，该方法通过Frobenius误差量化稳定性，通过等距偏差量化可塑性，并通过求解约束优化问题获得重初始化点。在持续视觉学习、语言建模和强化学习任务上的实验表明，FIRE一致优于无干预的朴素训练和标准重初始化方法，有效平衡了稳定性与可塑性之间的权衡。
A Survey for Deep Reinforcement Learning Based Network Intrusion Detection
Authors: Wanrong Yang, Alberto Acuto, Yihang Zhou, Dominik Wojtczak
First: 2024-09-25T13:39:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T13:54:11+00:00
Comments: 17 pages, 7 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Cyber-attacks are becoming increasingly sophisticated and frequent, highlighting the importance of network intrusion detection systems. This paper explores the potential and challenges of using deep reinforcement learning (DRL) in network intrusion detection. It begins by introducing key DRL concepts and frameworks, such as deep Q-networks and actor-critic algorithms, and reviews recent research utilizing DRL for intrusion detection. The study evaluates challenges related to model training efficiency, detection of minority and unknown class attacks, feature selection, and handling unbalanced datasets. The performance of DRL models is comprehensively analyzed, showing that while DRL holds promise, many recent technologies remain underexplored. Some DRL models achieve state-of-the-art results on public datasets, occasionally outperforming traditional deep learning methods. The paper concludes with recommendations for enhancing DRL deployment and testing in real-world network scenarios, with a focus on Internet of Things intrusion detection. It discusses recent DRL architectures and suggests future policy functions for DRL-based intrusion detection. Finally, the paper proposes integrating DRL with generative methods to further improve performance, addressing current gaps and supporting more robust and adaptive network intrusion detection systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于深度强化学习的网络入侵检测研究综述
网络攻击日益复杂频繁，凸显了网络入侵检测系统的重要性。本文探讨了深度强化学习在网络入侵检测中的应用潜力与挑战。首先介绍了深度Q网络、行动者-评论家算法等核心DRL概念与框架，综述了近期利用DRL进行入侵检测的研究进展。研究评估了模型训练效率、少数类与未知类攻击检测、特征选择及不平衡数据集处理等挑战，并对DRL模型的性能进行全面分析。结果表明，虽然DRL前景广阔，但许多新兴技术仍待深入探索。部分DRL模型在公开数据集上取得领先成果，偶尔优于传统深度学习方法。本文最后提出增强DRL在实际网络场景中部署与测试的建议，重点关注物联网入侵检测领域，讨论了近期DRL架构，并提出基于DRL的入侵检测未来策略函数设计方向。最终建议将DRL与生成式方法结合以提升性能，弥补当前研究空白，构建更鲁棒、自适应的网络入侵检测系统。
