CAIMAN: Causal Action Influence Detection for Sample-efficient Loco-manipulation
Authors: Yuanchen Yuan, Jin Cheng, Núria Armengol Urpí, Stelian Coros
First: 2025-02-02T16:16:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T13:47:02+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Enabling legged robots to perform non-prehensile loco-manipulation is crucial for enhancing their versatility. Learning behaviors such as whole-body object pushing often requires sophisticated planning strategies or extensive task-specific reward shaping, especially in unstructured environments. In this work, we present CAIMAN, a practical reinforcement learning framework that encourages the agent to gain control over other entities in the environment. CAIMAN leverages causal action influence as an intrinsic motivation objective, allowing legged robots to efficiently acquire object pushing skills even under sparse task rewards. We employ a hierarchical control strategy, combining a low-level locomotion module with a high-level policy that generates task-relevant velocity commands and is trained to maximize the intrinsic reward. To estimate causal action influence, we learn the dynamics of the environment by integrating a kinematic prior with data collected during training. We empirically demonstrate CAIMAN's superior sample efficiency and adaptability to diverse scenarios in simulation, as well as its successful transfer to real-world systems without further fine-tuning. A video demo is available at https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=dNyvT04Cqaw.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CAIMAN：面向高效样本学习的移动操作因果动作影响检测
使足式机器人能够执行非抓取式移动操作对其功能拓展至关重要。学习全身物体推动等行为通常需要复杂的规划策略或大量任务特定奖励设计，尤其在非结构化环境中。本研究提出CAIMAN——一种实用的强化学习框架，通过鼓励智能体获取对环境实体的控制能力，利用因果动作影响作为内在激励目标，使足式机器人即使在稀疏任务奖励下也能高效掌握物体推动技能。我们采用分层控制策略，将底层运动模块与高层策略相结合：高层策略生成任务相关速度指令，并通过最大化内在奖励进行训练。为估计因果动作影响，我们通过整合运动学先验与训练期间收集的数据来学习环境动力学。实验证明CAIMAN在仿真环境中具有卓越的样本效率与多场景适应性，并能无需微调直接迁移至真实系统。演示视频详见：https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=dNyvT04Cqaw。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for CAIMAN is to enable legged robots to perform non-prehensile loco-manipulation, such as object pushing, more efficiently without relying on complex planning or extensive reward engineering. The method introduces a reinforcement learning framework that uses causal action influence as an intrinsic motivation objective, combined with a hierarchical control strategy: a low-level locomotion module and a high-level policy trained to maximize this intrinsic reward by learning environment dynamics with a kinematic prior. Experimental results show that CAIMAN achieves superior sample efficiency and adaptability in simulation, and successfully transfers to real-world robots without additional fine-tuning.
CAIMAN 的研究动机是让足式机器人能够更高效地执行非抓取式移动操作（如物体推动），而无需依赖复杂的规划或大量的奖励设计。该方法提出了一种强化学习框架，利用因果行动影响作为内在激励目标，并结合分层控制策略：一个底层运动模块和一个高层策略，该策略通过结合运动学先验学习环境动态来最大化内在奖励。实验结果表明，CAIMAN 在仿真中表现出卓越的样本效率和适应性，并能成功迁移到真实机器人系统而无需进一步微调。
SWE-MiniSandbox: Container-Free Reinforcement Learning for Building Software Engineering Agents
Authors: Danlong Yuan, Wei Wu, Zhengren Wang, Xueliang Zhao, Huishuai Zhang, Dongyan Zhao
Venue: ICML
First: 2026-02-11T02:33:04+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T13:00:09+00:00
Comments: ICML under review
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) has become a key paradigm for training software engineering (SWE) agents, but existing pipelines typically rely on per-task containers for isolation. At scale, pre-built container images incur substantial storage overhead, slow environment setup, and require container-management privileges. We propose SWE-MiniSandbox, a lightweight, container-free method that enables scalable RL training of SWE agents without sacrificing isolation. Instead of relying on per-instance containers, SWE-MiniSandbox executes each task in an isolated workspace backed by kernel-level mechanisms, substantially reducing system overhead. It leverages lightweight environment pre-caching techniques to eliminate the need for bulky container images. As a result, our approach lowers disk usage to approximately 5\% of that required by container-based pipelines and reduces environment preparation time to about 25\% of the container baseline. Empirical results demonstrate that SWE-MiniSandbox achieves evaluation performance comparable to standard container-based pipelines. By removing the dependency on heavy container infrastructure, SWE-MiniSandbox offers a practical and accessible foundation for scaling RL-based SWE agents, particularly in resource-constrained research environments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SWE-MiniSandbox：面向软件工程智能体构建的无容器强化学习方法
强化学习已成为训练软件工程智能体的关键范式，但现有流程通常依赖按任务配置的容器实现隔离。大规模场景中，预构建容器镜像会带来显著的存储开销、拖慢环境部署速度，且需要容器管理权限。本文提出SWE-MiniSandbox——一种轻量级无容器方法，可在保持隔离性的前提下实现软件工程智能体的可扩展强化学习训练。该方法摒弃按实例配置容器的传统方式，转而通过内核级机制在隔离工作空间中执行任务，显著降低系统开销。其采用轻量化环境预缓存技术，无需臃肿的容器镜像。实验表明：本方案将磁盘占用降至容器基准方案的约5%，环境准备时间缩短至容器基准的约25%，且评估性能与标准容器流程相当。通过摆脱对重型容器基础设施的依赖，SWE-MiniSandbox为基于强化学习的软件工程智能体规模化训练提供了实用化基础架构，尤其适用于资源受限的研究环境。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the substantial storage overhead, slow setup, and privilege requirements of container-based pipelines for training software engineering agents with reinforcement learning, this paper introduces SWE-MiniSandbox, a container-free method that uses kernel-level isolation and lightweight environment pre-caching to create isolated workspaces. The method significantly reduces system resource demands, lowering disk usage to about 5% and cutting environment preparation time to roughly 25% of container-based baselines. 针对基于容器的软件工程智能体强化学习训练流程存在存储开销大、环境准备慢且需要管理权限的问题，本文提出了SWE-MiniSandbox这一无容器方法，其利用内核级隔离机制和轻量级环境预缓存技术，在隔离的工作空间中执行任务。该方法大幅降低了系统资源消耗，将磁盘占用降至容器方案的约5%，并将环境准备时间缩短至基线的大约25%。实验结果表明，该方法的评估性能与标准容器流程相当，从而为在资源受限的研究环境中规模化训练基于强化学习的软件工程智能体提供了实用且易于实施的基础。
Co-Evolutionary Multi-Modal Alignment via Structured Adversarial Evolution
Authors: Guoxin Shi, Haoyu Wang, Zaihui Yang, Yuxing Wang, Yongzhe Chang
First: 2026-03-02T12:10:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T12:10:46+00:00
Comments: Preprint
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Adversarial behavior plays a central role in aligning large language models with human values. However, existing alignment methods largely rely on static adversarial settings, which fundamentally limit robustness, particularly in multimodal settings with a larger attack surface. In this work, we move beyond static adversarial supervision and introduce co-evolutionary alignment with evolving attacks, instantiated by CEMMA (Co-Evolutionary Multi-Modal Alignment), an automated and adaptive framework for multimodal safety alignment. We introduce an Evolutionary Attacker that decomposes adversarial prompts into method templates and harmful intents. By employing genetic operators, including mutation, crossover, and differential evolution, it enables simple seed attacks to inherit the structural efficacy of sophisticated jailbreaks. The Adaptive Defender is iteratively updated on the synthesized hard negatives, forming a closed-loop process that adapts alignment to evolving attacks. Experiments show that the Evolutionary Attacker substantially increases red-teaming jailbreak attack success rate (ASR), while the Adaptive Defender improves robustness and generalization across benchmarks with higher data efficiency, without inducing excessive benign refusal, and remains compatible with inference-time defenses such as AdaShield.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于结构化对抗进化的协同进化多模态对齐方法
对抗行为在使大语言模型与人类价值观对齐方面起着核心作用。然而，现有对齐方法主要依赖静态对抗设置，这从根本上限制了鲁棒性，尤其在攻击面更大的多模态场景中。本研究突破静态对抗监督的局限，提出通过进化攻击实现协同进化对齐，具体体现为CEMMA（协同进化多模态对齐）框架——一个自动化、自适应的多模态安全对齐框架。我们设计了进化攻击器，将对抗性提示分解为方法模板和恶意意图。通过采用包括突变、交叉和差分进化在内的遗传算子，使简单种子攻击能够继承复杂越狱攻击的结构有效性。自适应防御器在合成的困难负例上迭代更新，形成闭环流程，使对齐能力适应持续演化的攻击。实验表明，进化攻击器显著提升了红队越狱攻击成功率，而自适应防御器以更高数据效率提升了跨基准测试的鲁棒性与泛化能力，且未引发过度良性拒绝，同时保持与AdaShield等推理时防御机制的兼容性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of static adversarial settings in aligning multimodal models, which restrict robustness against evolving attacks, this paper introduces CEMMA, a co-evolutionary alignment framework. The method employs an Evolutionary Attacker that decomposes adversarial prompts into templates and intents, using genetic operators to evolve seed attacks into sophisticated jailbreaks, and an Adaptive Defender iteratively trained on these hard negatives. Experimental results demonstrate that the attacker significantly boosts jailbreak attack success rates, while the defender enhances robustness and generalization across benchmarks with high data efficiency, without excessive benign refusal, and remains compatible with inference-time defenses.
本文针对静态对抗设置在多模态模型对齐中鲁棒性不足的问题，提出了CEMMA这一协同进化对齐框架。方法上，通过进化攻击器将对抗提示分解为模板和意图，利用遗传算子使简单种子攻击继承复杂越狱的结构有效性，并由自适应防御器在合成的困难负例上迭代更新。实验结果表明，进化攻击器大幅提升了越狱攻击成功率，而自适应防御器则增强了跨基准的鲁棒性和泛化能力，具有更高的数据效率，且不会导致过度良性拒绝，并与推理时防御保持兼容。
Combinatorial Bandit Bayesian Optimization for Tensor Outputs
Authors: Jingru Huang, Haijie Xu, Jie Guo, Manrui Jiang, Chen Zhang
First: 2026-01-31T10:16:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T12:10:27+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Bayesian optimization (BO) has been widely used to optimize expensive and black-box functions across various domains. However, existing BO methods have not addressed tensor-output functions. To fill this gap, we propose a novel tensor-output BO framework. Specifically, we first introduce a tensor-output Gaussian process (TOGP) with two classes of tensor-output kernels as a surrogate model of the tensor-output function, which can effectively capture the structural dependencies within the tensor. Based on it, we develop an upper confidence bound (UCB) acquisition function to select query points. Furthermore, we introduce a more practical and challenging problem setting, termed combinatorial bandit Bayesian optimization (CBBO), where only a subset of the tensor outputs can be selected to contribute to the objective. To tackle this, we propose a tensor-output CBBO method, which extends TOGP to handle partially observed tensor outputs, and accordingly design a novel combinatorial multi-arm bandit-UCB2 (CMAB-UCB2) criterion to sequentially select both the query points and the output subset. We establish theoretical regret bounds for both methods, guaranteeing sublinear regret. Extensive experiments on synthetic and real-world datasets demonstrate the superiority of our methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向张量输出的组合赌博机贝叶斯优化
贝叶斯优化（BO）已被广泛应用于优化各领域中的昂贵黑箱函数。然而，现有BO方法尚未处理张量输出函数。为填补这一空白，我们提出了一种新颖的张量输出BO框架。具体而言，我们首先引入一种张量输出高斯过程（TOGP），其配备两类张量输出核作为张量输出函数的代理模型，能有效捕捉张量内部的结构依赖性。基于此，我们开发了一种上置信界（UCB）采集函数以选择查询点。此外，我们引入了一个更实用且富挑战性的问题设置，称为组合赌博机贝叶斯优化（CBBO），其中仅能选择张量输出的子集来贡献于目标函数。为此，我们提出了一种张量输出CBBO方法，该方法将TOGP扩展至处理部分观测的张量输出，并相应设计了一种新颖的组合多臂赌博机-UCB2（CMAB-UCB2）准则，以顺序选择查询点与输出子集。我们为两种方法建立了理论遗憾界，保证了次线性遗憾。在合成与真实数据集上的大量实验证明了我们方法的优越性。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the gap in Bayesian optimization (BO) for tensor-output functions, which existing methods have not handled. The proposed method introduces a tensor-output Gaussian process (TOGP) with specialized kernels to model structural dependencies in tensors, and an upper confidence bound acquisition function for query selection. For a more challenging combinatorial bandit BO setting where only a subset of tensor outputs contributes to the objective, the authors extend TOGP to handle partial observations and design a combinatorial multi-arm bandit-UCB2 criterion to select both query points and output subsets. Experimental results on synthetic and real-world datasets show the superiority of the methods, supported by theoretical regret bounds guaranteeing sublinear regret.
本研究的动机是解决现有贝叶斯优化方法未处理的张量输出函数优化问题。所提出的方法引入了具有专门核函数的张量输出高斯过程作为代理模型，以捕捉张量内部的结构依赖性，并采用上置信界采集函数选择查询点。针对更实际且具有挑战性的组合赌博机贝叶斯优化设置，即仅部分张量输出对目标有贡献，作者扩展了张量输出高斯过程以处理部分观测数据，并设计了一种组合多臂赌博机-UCB2准则来同时选择查询点和输出子集。在合成和真实数据集上的大量实验证明了该方法的优越性，理论遗憾界分析保证了次线性遗憾。
Self-Harmony: Learning to Harmonize Self-Supervision and Self-Play in Test-Time Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Ru Wang, Wei Huang, Qi Cao, Yusuke Iwasawa, Yutaka Matsuo, Jiaxian Guo
Venue: ICLR 2026 Poster
First: 2025-11-03T03:34:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T12:08:56+00:00
Comments: Accepted at the 14th International Conference on Learning Representations (ICLR 2026), Poster
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Test-time reinforcement learning (TTRL) offers a label-free paradigm for adapting models using only synthetic signals at inference, but its success hinges on constructing reliable learning signals. Standard approaches such as majority voting often collapse to spurious yet popular answers. We introduce Self-Harmony, a framework built on a simple intuition: the correct answer should remain stable across both an original question and its paraphrase. Self-Harmony operationalizes this by employing a single model in two complementary roles: a Solver to produce answers and a Reframer to rephrase the input. Based on this, we further propose a pseudo-label method: instead of majority voting, it aggregates answer frequencies across these original and reframed views using the harmonic mean. This is a process that naturally selects for solutions stable under reframing, thereby avoiding the common trap of favoring view-dependent, spurious answers. Crucially, this requires no human supervision or auxiliary models. Across diverse reasoning benchmarks, Self-Harmony achieves state-of-the-art results at the label-free test-time setting, ranking first in 28 of 30 settings across multiple methods. Beyond accuracy, it demonstrates unprecedented robustness, with zero training failures in all experiments, underscoring its stability and reliability.
中文标题/摘要
标题：自和谐：在测试时强化学习中协调自监督与自博弈
测试时强化学习（TTRL）提供了一种无需标注的范式，仅通过推理时的合成信号来适配模型，但其成功依赖于构建可靠的学习信号。多数投票等标准方法常会坍缩至虚假但流行的答案。我们提出“自和谐”框架，其基于一个简单直觉：正确答案应在原始问题及其转述版本中保持稳定。该框架通过让单一模型承担两个互补角色来实现这一理念：求解器生成答案，重构器重述输入。基于此，我们进一步提出一种伪标签方法：放弃多数投票，转而使用调和平均数聚合原始视角与重构视角下的答案频率。这一过程能自然筛选出在重构下保持稳定的解，从而避免偏向视角依赖型虚假答案的常见陷阱。关键的是，该方法无需人工监督或辅助模型。在多样化推理基准测试中，自和谐在无标注测试时设定下取得了最先进的成果，在跨多种方法的30个设定中，有28项位列第一。除准确性外，它还展现出前所未有的鲁棒性——所有实验均未出现训练失败，彰显了其稳定性与可靠性。

The paper introduces Self-Harmony, a test-time reinforcement learning framework motivated by the need to avoid spurious answers that arise from standard methods like majority voting, which often favor popular but incorrect solutions. The method employs a single model in dual roles—as a Solver to generate answers and a Reframer to rephrase inputs—and aggregates answer frequencies using the harmonic mean across original and reframed views, selecting solutions stable under paraphrasing without human supervision. Experimental results show state-of-the-art performance on diverse reasoning benchmarks, achieving top rankings in 28 out of 30 label-free test-time settings and demonstrating robust stability with zero training failures across all experiments.
本文提出了Self-Harmony框架，其动机是解决测试时强化学习中多数投票等标准方法易产生虚假流行答案的问题。该方法让单一模型扮演双重角色：求解器生成答案，重构器改写输入，并通过调和平均聚合原始与改写视图下的答案频率，从而选择在改写下保持稳定的解，无需人工监督或辅助模型。实验结果表明，在多种推理基准测试中，该框架在无标签测试时设置下取得了最先进的性能，在30个设置中的28个排名第一，且在所有实验中均未出现训练失败，展现了卓越的稳健性和可靠性。
Structured Diversity Control: A Dual-Level Framework for Group-Aware Multi-Agent Coordination
Authors: Shuocun Yang, Huawen Hu, Xuan Liu, Yincheng Yao, Enze Shi, Shu Zhang
First: 2025-06-23T13:54:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T12:00:09+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Controlling the behavioral diversity is a pivotal challenge in multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL), particularly in complex collaborative scenarios. While existing methods attempt to regulate behavioral diversity by directly differentiating across all agents, they lack deep characterization and learning of multi-agent composition structures. This limitation leads to suboptimal performance or coordination failures when facing more complex or challenging tasks. To bridge this gap, we introduce Structured Diversity Control (SDC), a framework that redefines the system-wide diversity metric as a weighted combination of intra-group diversity, which is minimized for cohesion and inter-group diversity, which is maximized for specialization. The trade-off is governed by a pre-set Diversity Structure Factor (DSF), allowing for fine-grained, group-aware control over the collective strategy. Our method directly constrains the policy architecture without altering reward functions. This structural definition of diversity enables SDC to deliver substantial performance gains across various experiments, including increasing average rewards by up to 47.1\% in multi-target pursuit and reducing episode lengths by 12.82\% in complex neutralization scenarios. The proposed method offers a novel analytical perspective on the problem of cooperation in group-aware multi-agent systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：结构化多样性控制：面向群体感知的多智能体协调双层级框架
在多智能体强化学习（MARL）中，控制行为多样性是一个关键挑战，尤其在复杂协作场景下。现有方法试图通过直接区分所有智能体来调节行为多样性，但缺乏对多智能体组合结构的深度表征与学习，导致面对更复杂或更具挑战性的任务时性能欠佳或协调失败。为弥补这一不足，我们提出了结构化多样性控制（SDC）框架，将系统级多样性指标重新定义为组内多样性（为增强内聚力而最小化）与组间多样性（为促进专业化而最大化）的加权组合，其权衡由预设的多样性结构因子（DSF）调控，实现对集体策略的细粒度、群体感知控制。该方法直接约束策略架构而无需修改奖励函数。这种结构化的多样性定义使SDC在多项实验中取得显著性能提升：在多目标追捕任务中平均奖励最高提升47.1%，在复杂中和场景中回合长度减少12.82%。所提方法为群体感知多智能体系统的协作问题提供了新的分析视角。

本文针对多智能体强化学习（MARL）中复杂协作任务的行为多样性控制挑战，指出现有方法因缺乏对多智能体组成结构的深入刻画而导致协调性能不佳。为此，作者提出了结构化多样性控制（SDC）框架，该系统将整体多样性重新定义为组内多样性（最小化以增强凝聚力）和组间多样性（最大化以促进专业化）的加权组合，并通过预设的多样性结构因子（DSF）进行细粒度控制，且无需修改奖励函数。实验结果表明，SDC在多目标追捕任务中平均奖励提升高达47.1%，在复杂中和场景中回合长度减少12.82%，为群体感知的多智能体协作问题提供了新的分析视角。
Hyperparameter Trajectory Inference with Conditional Lagrangian Optimal Transport
Authors: Harry Amad, Mihaela van der Schaar
First: 2026-03-02T11:55:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T11:55:02+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Neural networks (NNs) often have critical behavioural trade-offs that are set at design time with hyperparameters-such as reward weights in reinforcement learning or quantile targets in regression. Post-deployment, however, user preferences can evolve, making initial settings undesirable, necessitating potentially expensive retraining. To circumvent this, we introduce the task of Hyperparameter Trajectory Inference (HTI): to learn, from observed data, how a NN's conditional output distribution changes with its hyperparameters, and construct a surrogate model that approximates the NN at unobserved hyperparameter settings. HTI requires extending existing trajectory inference approaches to incorporate conditions, exacerbating the challenge of ensuring inferred paths are feasible. We propose an approach based on conditional Lagrangian optimal transport, jointly learning the Lagrangian function governing hyperparameter-induced dynamics along with the associated optimal transport maps and geodesics between observed marginals, which form the surrogate model. We incorporate inductive biases based on the manifold hypothesis and least-action principles into the learned Lagrangian, improving surrogate model feasibility. We empirically demonstrate that our approach reconstructs NN outputs across various hyperparameter spectra better than other alternatives.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于条件拉格朗日最优传输的超参数轨迹推断
神经网络（NNs）常在设计时通过超参数（如强化学习中的奖励权重或回归中的分位数目标）设定关键行为权衡。然而，部署后用户偏好可能变化，导致初始设置不再适用，需进行可能昂贵的重新训练。为规避此问题，我们提出超参数轨迹推断（HTI）任务：从观测数据中学习NN的条件输出分布如何随超参数变化，并构建一个在未观测超参数设置下近似NN的代理模型。HTI需扩展现有轨迹推断方法以纳入条件，这加剧了确保推断路径可行的挑战。我们提出一种基于条件拉格朗日最优传输的方法，联合学习控制超参数诱导动态的拉格朗日函数，以及观测边缘分布间的最优传输映射和测地线（构成代理模型）。我们将基于流形假设和最小作用原理的归纳偏置融入学习的拉格朗日函数中，提升代理模型的可行性。实验表明，我们的方法在多种超参数谱上重建NN输出的效果优于其他替代方案。

The paper is motivated by the need to adapt neural networks post-deployment when user preferences evolve, making initial hyperparameter settings suboptimal and retraining costly. The method introduces Hyperparameter Trajectory Inference (HTI), which uses conditional Lagrangian optimal transport to learn how a neural network's output distribution changes with hyperparameters, jointly learning a Lagrangian function and optimal transport maps to construct a surrogate model that approximates the network at unobserved settings, incorporating inductive biases from the manifold hypothesis and least-action principles for feasibility. Quark Medical Alignment: A Holistic Multi-Dimensional Alignment and Collaborative Optimization Paradigm
Authors: Tianxiang Xu, Jiayi Liu, Yixuan Tong, Jialu Xu, Yunqing Wei, Kaiwen Feng, PanPan Hou, Kangping Yin, Jiyuan Hu, Hao Zhou, Zhenxin Ma, Jian Xu, Guanjun Jiang
First: 2026-02-12T07:26:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T11:30:55+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While reinforcement learning for large language model alignment has progressed rapidly in recent years, transferring these paradigms to high-stakes medical question answering reveals a fundamental paradigm mismatch. Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback relies on preference annotations that are prohibitively expensive and often fail to reflect the absolute correctness of medical facts. Reinforcement Learning from Verifiable Rewards lacks effective automatic verifiers and struggles to handle complex clinical contexts. Meanwhile, medical alignment requires the simultaneous optimization of correctness, safety, and compliance, yet multi-objective heterogeneous reward signals are prone to scale mismatch and optimization conflicts. To address these challenges, we propose a robust medical alignment paradigm. We first construct a holistic multi-dimensional medical alignment matrix that decomposes alignment objectives into four categories: fundamental capabilities, expert knowledge, online feedback, and format specifications. Within each category, we establish a closed loop of where observable metrics inform attributable diagnosis, which in turn drives optimizable rewards, thereby providing fine-grained, high-resolution supervision signals for subsequent iterative optimization. To resolve gradient domination and optimization instability problem caused by heterogeneous signals, we further propose a unified optimization mechanism. This mechanism employs Reference-Frozen Normalization to align reward scales and implements a Tri-Factor Adaptive Dynamic Weighting strategy to achieve collaborative optimization that is weakness-oriented, risk-prioritized, and redundancy-reducing. Experimental results demonstrate the effectiveness of our proposed paradigm in real-world medical scenario evaluations, establishing a new paradigm for complex alignment in vertical domains.
中文标题/摘要
标题：夸克医疗对齐：一种整体多维对齐与协同优化范式
尽管近年来大语言模型对齐的强化学习进展迅速，但将这些范式迁移至高风险医疗问答领域时，却暴露出根本性的范式失配问题。基于人类反馈的强化学习依赖成本极高且难以反映医疗事实绝对正确性的偏好标注；基于可验证奖励的强化学习则缺乏有效的自动验证器，难以处理复杂临床情境。同时，医疗对齐需同步优化正确性、安全性与合规性，但多目标异质奖励信号易出现尺度失配与优化冲突。为应对这些挑战，我们提出一种鲁棒的医疗对齐范式：首先构建整体多维医疗对齐矩阵，将对齐目标解构为基础能力、专家知识、在线反馈与格式规范四类；在每类中建立可观测指标驱动归因诊断、进而生成可优化奖励的闭环，为后续迭代优化提供细粒度高分辨率监督信号。针对异质信号导致的梯度主导与优化失稳问题，进一步提出统一优化机制：采用参考冻结归一化实现奖励尺度对齐，并通过三因子自适应动态加权策略实现面向短板、风险优先、冗余削减的协同优化。实验结果表明，该范式在真实医疗场景评估中具有显著有效性，为垂直领域的复杂对齐问题建立了新范式。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work stems from the inadequacy of existing reinforcement learning alignment methods, such as RLHF and RL from verifiable rewards, for high-stakes medical question answering due to high annotation costs, lack of automatic verifiers, and the need to simultaneously optimize multiple heterogeneous objectives like correctness, safety, and compliance. To address this, the authors propose a holistic medical alignment paradigm that constructs a multi-dimensional alignment matrix decomposing objectives into four categories—fundamental capabilities, expert knowledge, online feedback, and format specifications—and establishes a closed loop where observable metrics inform attributable diagnosis to drive optimizable rewards, providing fine-grained supervision. They further introduce a unified optimization mechanism using Reference-Frozen Normalization to align reward scales and a Tri-Factor Adaptive Dynamic Weighting strategy for collaborative, weakness-oriented optimization. Experimental results validate the paradigm's effectiveness in real-world medical scenarios, establishing a new approach for complex vertical domain alignment.
本研究的动机在于现有强化学习对齐方法（如基于人类反馈的强化学习和基于可验证奖励的强化学习）难以适用于高风险医疗问答场景，因其标注成本高昂、缺乏有效自动验证器，且需同时优化正确性、安全性和合规性等多维异构目标。为此，作者提出了一种整体医疗对齐范式，构建了一个多维对齐矩阵，将目标分解为基本能力、专家知识、在线反馈和格式规范四类，并建立闭环系统，使可观测指标驱动可归因诊断以生成可优化奖励，从而提供细粒度监督信号。为进一步解决异构信号导致的梯度主导和优化不稳定问题，他们提出统一优化机制，采用参考冻结归一化对齐奖励尺度，并实施三因子自适应动态加权策略以实现以弱点为导向、风险优先且减少冗余的协同优化。实验结果表明，该范式在真实医疗场景评估中有效，为垂直领域的复杂对齐建立了新范式。
Look Back to Reason Forward: Revisitable Memory for Long-Context LLM Agents
Authors: Yaorui Shi, Yuxin Chen, Siyuan Wang, Sihang Li, Hengxing Cai, Qi Gu, Xiang Wang, An Zhang
First: 2025-09-27T01:36:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T11:19:01+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models face challenges in long-context question answering, where key evidence of a query may be dispersed across millions of tokens. Existing works equip large language models with a memory buffer that is dynamically updated via a linear document scan, also known as the "memorize while reading" methods. While this approach scales efficiently, it suffers from pruning of latent evidence, information loss through overwriting, and sparse reinforcement learning signals. To tackle these challenges, we present ReMemR1, which integrates the mechanism of memory retrieval into the memory update process, enabling the agent to selectively callback historical memories for non-linear reasoning. To further strengthen training, we propose a multi-level reward design, which combines final-answer rewards with dense, step-level signals that guide effective memory use. Together, these contributions mitigate information degradation, improve supervision, and support complex multi-hop reasoning. Extensive experiments demonstrate that ReMemR1 significantly outperforms state-of-the-art baselines on long-context question answering while incurring negligible computational overhead, validating its ability to trade marginal cost for robust long-context reasoning.
中文标题/摘要

Experimental results show that ReMemR1 significantly outperforms state-of-the-art baselines on long-context QA tasks with minimal computational overhead, demonstrating robust reasoning capabilities.

Rethinking Policy Diversity in Ensemble Policy Gradient in Large-Scale Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Naoki Shitanda, Motoki Omura, Tatsuya Harada, Takayuki Osa
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-03-02T11:06:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T11:06:40+00:00
Comments: In ICLR 2026. Website at https://naoki04.github.io/paper-cpo/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Scaling reinforcement learning to tens of thousands of parallel environments requires overcoming the limited exploration capacity of a single policy. Ensemble-based policy gradient methods, which employ multiple policies to collect diverse samples, have recently been proposed to promote exploration. However, merely broadening the exploration space does not always enhance learning capability, since excessive exploration can reduce exploration quality or compromise training stability. In this work, we theoretically analyze the impact of inter-policy diversity on learning efficiency in policy ensembles, and propose Coupled Policy Optimization which regulates diversity through KL constraints between policies. The proposed method enables effective exploration and outperforms strong baselines such as SAPG, PBT, and PPO across multiple tasks, including challenging dexterous manipulation, in terms of both sample efficiency and final performance. Furthermore, analysis of policy diversity and effective sample size during training reveals that follower policies naturally distribute around the leader, demonstrating the emergence of structured and efficient exploratory behavior. Our results indicate that diverse exploration under appropriate regulation is key to achieving stable and sample-efficient learning in ensemble policy gradient methods. Project page at https://naoki04.github.io/paper-cpo/ .
中文标题/摘要
标题：大规模强化学习中集成策略梯度方法策略多样性的再思考
将强化学习扩展到数万个并行环境需要克服单一策略探索能力有限的问题。近期提出的基于集成的策略梯度方法通过使用多个策略收集多样化样本以促进探索。然而，单纯扩大探索空间并不总能提升学习能力，因为过度探索可能降低探索质量或损害训练稳定性。本文从理论上分析了策略间多样性对集成策略学习效率的影响，并提出通过策略间KL约束调控多样性的耦合策略优化方法。该方法在多个任务（包括具有挑战性的灵巧操作任务）中实现了有效探索，并在样本效率和最终性能上超越了SAPG、PBT、PPO等强基线。训练过程中对策略多样性和有效样本量的分析表明，跟随策略会自然围绕主导策略分布，展现出结构化高效探索行为的涌现。研究结果表明，在适当调控下的多样化探索是实现集成策略梯度方法稳定且样本高效学习的关键。项目页面：https://naoki04.github.io/paper-cpo/
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the limited exploration capacity of single policies in large-scale reinforcement learning by using policy ensembles, while recognizing that uncontrolled diversity can harm learning efficiency and stability. The method, Coupled Policy Optimization, theoretically analyzes the role of inter-policy diversity and regulates it by imposing KL divergence constraints between policies to balance exploration and training quality. Experimental results on tasks including dexterous manipulation show that the approach outperforms strong baselines like SAPG, PBT, and PPO in both sample efficiency and final performance, with analysis revealing that follower policies naturally cluster around a leader, leading to structured and effective exploratory behavior.
本研究的动机是通过策略集成解决大规模强化学习中单一策略探索能力有限的问题，同时认识到不受控制的多样性可能损害学习效率和稳定性。所提出的方法称为耦合策略优化，它从理论上分析了策略间多样性的作用，并通过在策略间施加KL散度约束来调节多样性，以平衡探索与训练质量。在包括灵巧操作在内的多个任务上的实验结果表明，该方法在样本效率和最终性能上均优于SAPG、PBT和PPO等强基线，分析显示跟随策略会自然地围绕主导策略分布，从而形成结构化且高效的探索行为。
Flow-Factory: A Unified Framework for Reinforcement Learning in Flow-Matching Models
Authors: Bowen Ping, Chengyou Jia, Minnan Luo, Hangwei Qian, Ivor Tsang
First: 2026-02-13T02:21:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T10:54:54+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement learning has emerged as a promising paradigm for aligning diffusion and flow-matching models with human preferences, yet practitioners face fragmented codebases, model-specific implementations, and engineering complexity. We introduce Flow-Factory, a unified framework that decouples algorithms, models, and rewards through through a modular, registry-based architecture. This design enables seamless integration of new algorithms and architectures, as demonstrated by our support for GRPO, DiffusionNFT, and AWM across Flux, Qwen-Image, and WAN video models. By minimizing implementation overhead, Flow-Factory empowers researchers to rapidly prototype and scale future innovations with ease. Flow-Factory provides production-ready memory optimization, flexible multi-reward training, and seamless distributed training support. The codebase is available at https://github.com/X-GenGroup/Flow-Factory.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Flow-Factory：流匹配模型中强化学习的统一框架
强化学习已成为将扩散模型和流匹配模型与人类偏好对齐的重要范式，但实践者面临代码库碎片化、模型特定实现和工程复杂性等挑战。本文提出Flow-Factory，这是一个通过模块化、基于注册表的架构将算法、模型和奖励机制解耦的统一框架。该设计支持新算法与架构的无缝集成，例如我们在Flux、Qwen-Image和WAN视频模型中实现了对GRPO、DiffusionNFT和AWM的支持。通过最小化实现开销，Flow-Factory使研究人员能够快速原型化并轻松扩展未来创新。该框架提供生产级内存优化、灵活的多奖励训练机制和无缝分布式训练支持。代码库已开源：https://github.com/X-GenGroup/Flow-Factory。

RL for Reasoning by Adaptively Revealing Rationales
Authors: Mohammad Hossein Amani, Aryo Lotfi, Nicolas Mario Baldwin, Samy Bengio, Mehrdad Farajtabar, Emmanuel Abbe, Robert West
First: 2025-06-22T17:46:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T10:46:54+00:00
Comments: 22 pages, 11 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Learning in the combinatorially large output space of sequence generation problems is challenging as providing expert demonstrations scales poorly with sequence length, and RL struggles with sparse rewards. Between dense demonstrations in supervised training and no demonstrations in reinforcement learning lies an underexplored regime: partial supervision. We ask whether some classes of sequence learning problems become efficiently learnable by exploiting this gap. We address this by introducing adaptive backtracking (AdaBack), a per-sample curriculum learning algorithm that reveals a partial prefix of the target output. The supervision length is adjusted dynamically for each sample based on the model's past reward signal, allowing it to incrementally learn to complete reasoning chains by conditioning on correct partial solutions. We investigate this intermediate regime between SFT and RL and argue that per-sample curriculum learning is more than a trade-off between efficiency and generality--it can succeed in tasks with long sequences of latent dependencies where SFT and RL both fail to generalize. Using a synthetic task with latent parity constraints, we show that AdaBack reliably solves problems that are otherwise intractable. On three mathematical reasoning benchmarks, DeepScaleR, MATH, and GSM8k, we find that AdaBack enables models to solve problems that RL alone cannot, acquiring new reasoning capabilities through incremental exposure to partial solutions.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过自适应揭示推理链的强化学习
在序列生成问题的组合爆炸输出空间中进行学习具有挑战性，因为专家演示的提供随序列长度增加而难以扩展，且强化学习面临稀疏奖励问题。在监督训练的密集演示与强化学习的无演示之间，存在一个尚未充分探索的中间区域：部分监督。我们探讨是否某些序列学习问题能通过利用这一间隙实现高效学习。为此，我们提出自适应回溯算法（AdaBack），一种基于样本的课程学习方法，它逐步揭示目标输出的部分前缀。监督长度根据模型历史奖励信号动态调整，使其能够通过基于正确部分解的条件化，逐步学习完成推理链。我们研究了监督微调与强化学习之间的这一中间机制，并论证基于样本的课程学习不仅是效率与泛化性的权衡——它能在具有长程隐式依赖的任务中取得成功，而监督微调与强化学习均无法泛化。通过在隐式奇偶约束的合成任务中验证，AdaBack可稳定解决原本棘手的问题。在DeepScaleR、MATH和GSM8k三个数学推理基准测试中，AdaBack使模型能够解决仅用强化学习无法攻克的问题，通过逐步接触部分解获得新的推理能力。

The paper is motivated by the challenge of learning in large output spaces for sequence generation, where supervised fine-tuning (SFT) requires extensive demonstrations and reinforcement learning (RL) suffers from sparse rewards, prompting exploration of a partial supervision regime. The method introduces adaptive backtracking (AdaBack), a per-sample curriculum learning algorithm that dynamically reveals partial prefixes of target outputs based on past reward signals, enabling incremental learning by conditioning on correct partial solutions. Experimental results demonstrate that AdaBack reliably solves synthetic tasks with latent parity constraints and, on mathematical reasoning benchmarks like DeepScaleR, MATH, and GSM8k, enables models to acquire new reasoning capabilities and solve problems that RL alone cannot, outperforming both SFT and RL in tasks with long sequences of latent dependencies.

TopoCurate:Modeling Interaction Topology for Tool-Use Agent Training
Authors: Jinluan Yang, Yuxin Liu, Zhengyu Chen, Chengcheng Han, Yueqing Sun, Qi Gu, Hui Su, Xunliang Cai, Fei Wu, Kun Kuang
First: 2026-03-02T10:38:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T10:38:54+00:00
Comments: Under Review
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Training tool-use agents typically relies on outcome-based filtering: Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) on successful trajectories and Reinforcement Learning (RL) on pass-rate-selected tasks. However, this paradigm ignores interaction dynamics: successful trajectories may lack error recovery or exhibit redundancy, while pass rates fail to distinguish structurally informative tasks from trivial ones. We propose \textbf{TopoCurate}, an interaction-aware framework that projects multi-trial rollouts from the same task into a unified semantic quotient topology. By merging equivalent action-observation states, this projection transforms scattered linear trajectories into a structured manifold that explicitly captures how tool invocations and environmental responses drive the divergence between effective strategies and failure modes. Leveraging this representation, we introduce a dual-selection mechanism: for SFT, we prioritize trajectories demonstrating reflective recovery, semantic efficiency, and strategic diversity to mitigate covariate shift and mode collapse; for RL, we select tasks with high error branch ratios and strategic heterogeneity, maximizing gradient Signal-to-Noise Ratio to address vanishing signals in sparse-reward settings. Evaluations on BFCLv3 and Tau2 Bench show that TopoCurate achieves consistent gains of 4.2\% (SFT) and 6.9\% (RL) over state-of-the-art baselines. We will release the code and data soon for further investigations.
中文标题/摘要
标题：TopoCurate：为工具使用智能体训练建模交互拓扑
训练工具使用智能体通常依赖基于结果的筛选：对成功轨迹进行监督微调（SFT），对通过率筛选的任务进行强化学习（RL）。然而，该范式忽略了交互动态：成功轨迹可能缺乏错误恢复或存在冗余，而通过率无法区分具有结构信息量的任务与简单任务。我们提出\textbf{TopoCurate}，一种交互感知框架，将同一任务的多轮试验轨迹投影到统一的语义商拓扑中。通过合并等效的动作-观察状态，该投影将分散的线性轨迹转化为结构化流形，明确捕捉工具调用与环境响应如何驱动有效策略与失败模式之间的分岔。基于此表示，我们引入双重选择机制：对于SFT，优先选择展现反思性恢复、语义效率与策略多样性的轨迹，以缓解协变量偏移与模式坍塌；对于RL，选择具有高错误分支比与策略异质性的任务，最大化梯度信噪比，以应对稀疏奖励设置中的信号消失问题。在BFCLv3与Tau2 Bench上的评估表明，TopoCurate相比最先进基线在SFT和RL上分别实现4.2%与6.9%的稳定提升。我们将很快发布代码与数据以供进一步研究。

The paper introduces TopoCurate, a framework motivated by the limitations of outcome-based training for tool-use agents, which overlooks interaction dynamics such as error recovery and task structural complexity. The method projects multi-trial rollouts into a semantic quotient topology to merge equivalent states, creating a structured manifold that captures strategic divergence, and employs a dual-selection mechanism to prioritize trajectories with reflective recovery and tasks with high error branch ratios for supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning, respectively. Experimental results on BFCLv3 and Tau2 Bench demonstrate consistent performance gains of 4.2% for SFT and 6.9% for RL over state-of-the-art baselines.

Search Multilayer Perceptron-Based Fusion for Efficient and Accurate Siamese Tracking
Authors: Tianqi Shen, Huakao Lin, Ning An
First: 2026-03-02T10:30:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T10:30:54+00:00
Comments: 23 pages, 12 figures, 7 tables. This work was completed in 2024 and accepted for publication in IEEE TCDS (2026)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Siamese visual trackers have recently advanced through increasingly sophisticated fusion mechanisms built on convolutional or Transformer architectures. However, both struggle to deliver pixel-level interactions efficiently on resource-constrained hardware, leading to a persistent accuracy-efficiency imbalance. Motivated by this limitation, we redesign the Siamese neck with a simple yet effective Multilayer Perception (MLP)-based fusion module that enables pixel-level interaction with minimal structural overhead. Nevertheless, naively stacking MLP blocks introduces a new challenge: computational cost can scale quadratically with channel width. To overcome this, we construct a hierarchical search space of carefully designed MLP modules and introduce a customized relaxation strategy that enables differentiable neural architecture search (DNAS) to decouple channel-width optimization from other architectural choices. This targeted decoupling automatically balances channel width and depth, yielding a low-complexity architecture. The resulting tracker achieves state-of-the-art accuracy-efficiency trade-offs. It ranks among the top performers on four general-purpose and three aerial tracking benchmarks, while maintaining real-time performance on both resource-constrained Graphics Processing Units (GPUs) and Neural Processing Units (NPUs).
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于多层感知机融合的高效精准孪生跟踪搜索方法
近年来，基于卷积或Transformer架构的复杂融合机制推动了孪生视觉跟踪器的发展，但两者在资源受限硬件上均难以高效实现像素级交互，导致精度与效率持续失衡。针对这一局限，我们采用简单有效的多层感知机（MLP）融合模块重新设计孪生网络颈部，以最小结构开销实现像素级交互。然而，简单堆叠MLP模块会引发新问题：计算成本随通道宽度呈二次方增长。为此，我们构建了精心设计的MLP模块层级搜索空间，并引入定制化松弛策略，使可微分神经架构搜索（DNAS）能够将通道宽度优化与其他架构选择解耦。这种定向解耦自动平衡通道宽度与深度，生成低复杂度架构。所得跟踪器实现了最优的精度-效率权衡，在四项通用基准和三项航空跟踪基准中位列前茅，同时在资源受限的图形处理器（GPU）和神经处理器（NPU）上保持实时性能。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the accuracy-efficiency imbalance in Siamese trackers due to inefficient pixel-level interactions in convolutional or Transformer-based fusion, this paper redesigns the tracker's neck with a simple Multilayer Perceptron (MLP)-based fusion module for effective pixel-level interaction with low overhead. To address the quadratic computational cost increase from stacking MLP blocks, the method constructs a hierarchical search space of MLP modules and employs a customized relaxation strategy for differentiable neural architecture search, decoupling channel-width optimization to automatically balance width and depth for a low-complexity architecture. Experimental results show that the resulting tracker achieves state-of-the-art accuracy-efficiency trade-offs, ranking top on four general-purpose and three aerial tracking benchmarks while maintaining real-time performance on resource-constrained GPUs and NPUs.

Cross-modal Identity Mapping: Minimizing Information Loss in Modality Conversion via Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Haonan Jia, Shichao Dong, Xin Dong, Zenghui Sun, Jin Wang, Jinsong Lan, Xiaoyong Zhu, Bo Zheng, Kaifu Zhang
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2026-03-02T10:24:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T10:24:41+00:00
Comments: Accepted by CVPR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Vision-Language Models (LVLMs) often omit or misrepresent critical visual content in generated image captions. Minimizing such information loss will force LVLMs to focus on image details to generate precise descriptions. However, measuring information loss during modality conversion is inherently challenging due to the modal gap between visual content and text output. In this paper, we argue that the quality of an image caption is positively correlated with the similarity between images retrieved via text search using that caption. Based on this insight, we further propose Cross-modal Identity Mapping (CIM), a reinforcement learning framework that enhances image captioning without requiring additional annotations. Specifically, the method quantitatively evaluates the information loss from two perspectives: Gallery Representation Consistency and Query-gallery Image Relevance. Supervised under these metrics, LVLM minimizes information loss and aims to achieve identity mapping from images to captions. The experimental results demonstrate the superior performance of our method in image captioning, even when compared with Supervised Fine-Tuning. Particularly, on the COCO-LN500 benchmark, CIM achieves a 20% improvement in relation reasoning on Qwen2.5-VL-7B.The code will be released when the paper is accepted.
中文标题/摘要
标题：跨模态身份映射：通过强化学习最小化模态转换中的信息损失
大型视觉语言模型在生成图像描述时常常忽略或误传关键视觉内容。最小化此类信息损失将迫使模型聚焦于图像细节以生成精确描述。然而，由于视觉内容与文本输出之间的模态鸿沟，衡量模态转换过程中的信息损失本质上是困难的。本文提出，图像描述的质量与通过该描述进行文本检索所获图像的相似度呈正相关。基于此洞见，我们进一步提出跨模态身份映射——一种无需额外标注即可增强图像描述能力的强化学习框架。该方法从图库表示一致性和查询-图库图像相关性两个角度定量评估信息损失。在这些指标监督下，大型视觉语言模型通过最小化信息损失，致力于实现从图像到描述的恒等映射。实验结果表明，即使在有监督微调对比下，本方法在图像描述任务中仍表现出优越性能。特别是在COCO-LN500基准测试中，跨模态身份映射在Qwen2.5-VL-7B模型上实现了关系推理能力20%的提升。代码将在论文录用后开源。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the problem of information loss in image captioning by Large Vision-Language Models (LVLMs), where critical visual details are often omitted or misrepresented in generated text. The core motivation is to minimize this loss by forcing the model to focus on precise image details, but measuring such loss is challenging due to the modal gap. The proposed method, Cross-modal Identity Mapping (CIM), uses a reinforcement learning framework that quantitatively evaluates information loss from two perspectives: Gallery Representation Consistency and Query-gallery Image Relevance, based on the insight that caption quality correlates with the similarity of images retrieved via text search. Without needing extra annotations, CIM supervises the LVLM to achieve identity mapping from images to captions. Experimental results show superior performance in image captioning, even compared to Supervised Fine-Tuning, with a notable 20% improvement in relation reasoning on the COCO-LN500 benchmark using the Qwen2.5-VL-7B model.
本文针对大型视觉语言模型（LVLMs）在图像描述生成中存在的信息丢失问题展开研究，该问题常导致关键视觉细节在生成的文本中被忽略或错误表达。其核心动机是通过迫使模型关注精确的图像细节来最小化这种信息损失，但由于模态差异，测量这种损失具有挑战性。基于图像描述质量与通过文本搜索检索到的图像相似度正相关的洞见，提出的方法——跨模态身份映射（CIM）——采用强化学习框架，从图库表示一致性和查询-图库图像相关性两个角度定量评估信息损失。该方法无需额外标注，通过监督LVLM实现从图像到描述的恒等映射。实验结果表明，即使在有监督微调的对比下，该方法在图像描述任务上也表现出优越性能，特别是在COCO-LN500基准测试中，使用Qwen2.5-VL-7B模型在关系推理方面实现了20%的提升。
MVR: Multi-view Video Reward Shaping for Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Lirui Luo, Guoxi Zhang, Hongming Xu, Yaodong Yang, Cong Fang, Qing Li
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-03-02T10:24:04+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T10:24:04+00:00
Comments: ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reward design is of great importance for solving complex tasks with reinforcement learning. Recent studies have explored using image-text similarity produced by vision-language models (VLMs) to augment rewards of a task with visual feedback. A common practice linearly adds VLM scores to task or success rewards without explicit shaping, potentially altering the optimal policy. Moreover, such approaches, often relying on single static images, struggle with tasks whose desired behavior involves complex, dynamic motions spanning multiple visually different states. Furthermore, single viewpoints can occlude critical aspects of an agent's behavior. To address these issues, this paper presents Multi-View Video Reward Shaping (MVR), a framework that models the relevance of states regarding the target task using videos captured from multiple viewpoints. MVR leverages video-text similarity from a frozen pre-trained VLM to learn a state relevance function that mitigates the bias towards specific static poses inherent in image-based methods. Additionally, we introduce a state-dependent reward shaping formulation that integrates task-specific rewards and VLM-based guidance, automatically reducing the influence of VLM guidance once the desired motion pattern is achieved. We confirm the efficacy of the proposed framework with extensive experiments on challenging humanoid locomotion tasks from HumanoidBench and manipulation tasks from MetaWorld, verifying the design choices through ablation studies.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MVR：面向强化学习的多视角视频奖励塑形方法
奖励设计对于利用强化学习解决复杂任务至关重要。近期研究探索使用视觉语言模型（VLM）生成的图像-文本相似度，通过视觉反馈增强任务奖励。常见做法是将VLM评分与任务或成功奖励线性叠加，缺乏显式塑形，可能改变最优策略。此外，这类方法通常依赖单张静态图像，难以处理期望行为涉及跨越多个视觉差异状态的复杂动态运动的任务。单一视角还可能遮挡智能体行为的关键方面。为解决这些问题，本文提出多视角视频奖励塑形（MVR）框架，利用多视角拍摄的视频建模状态与目标任务的相关性。MVR通过冻结预训练VLM提取视频-文本相似度，学习状态相关性函数，以缓解基于图像方法对特定静态姿态的固有偏差。同时，我们提出状态依赖的奖励塑形公式，整合任务特定奖励与VLM引导，在达成期望运动模式后自动减弱VLM引导的影响。通过在HumanoidBench的复杂人形运动任务和MetaWorld的操作任务上进行大量实验，并通过消融研究验证设计选择，我们证实了所提框架的有效性。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses limitations in using vision-language models (VLMs) for reward shaping in reinforcement learning, where existing methods that linearly add single-image VLM scores to task rewards can alter the optimal policy and fail to capture dynamic, multi-state behaviors or handle viewpoint occlusion. The proposed Multi-View Video Reward Shaping (MVR) framework models state relevance to the target task using videos from multiple viewpoints, leveraging video-text similarity from a frozen VLM to learn a relevance function that reduces bias toward static poses, and introduces a state-dependent shaping formulation that integrates task rewards with VLM guidance while automatically reducing that guidance once desired motion is achieved. Experimental results on challenging humanoid locomotion tasks from HumanoidBench and manipulation tasks from MetaWorld demonstrate the framework's efficacy, with ablation studies validating the design choices.
本文针对强化学习中利用视觉语言模型进行奖励塑造的局限性提出改进，现有方法通常将单张静态图像的VLM分数线性叠加到任务奖励上，这可能会改变最优策略，且难以捕捉涉及多个视觉状态、动态复杂的行为，也无法处理视角遮挡问题。为此，论文提出了多视角视频奖励塑造框架，该框架利用从多个视角拍摄的视频，通过冻结预训练VLM的视频-文本相似度来学习状态与目标任务的相关性函数，从而减少基于图像方法对特定静态姿势的偏差，并引入一种状态依赖的奖励塑造公式，将任务特定奖励与VLM引导相结合，在达到期望运动模式后自动减弱VLM引导的影响。在HumanoidBench的人形机器人运动任务和MetaWorld的操作任务上的大量实验验证了该框架的有效性，消融研究也证实了其设计选择的合理性。
Chain-of-Context Learning: Dynamic Constraint Understanding for Multi-Task VRPs
Authors: Shuangchun Gui, Suyu Liu, Xuehe Wang, Zhiguang Cao
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-03-02T09:57:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T09:57:15+00:00
Comments: This paper is accepted by ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multi-task Vehicle Routing Problems (VRPs) aim to minimize routing costs while satisfying diverse constraints. Existing solvers typically adopt a unified reinforcement learning (RL) framework to learn generalizable patterns across tasks. However, they often overlook the constraint and node dynamics during the decision process, making the model fail to accurately react to the current context. To address this limitation, we propose Chain-of-Context Learning (CCL), a novel framework that progressively captures the evolving context to guide fine-grained node adaptation. Specifically, CCL constructs step-wise contextual information via a Relevance-Guided Context Reformulation (RGCR) module, which adaptively prioritizes salient constraints. This context then guides node updates through a Trajectory-Shared Node Re-embedding (TSNR) module, which aggregates shared node features from all trajectories' contexts and uses them to update inputs for the next step. By modeling evolving preferences of the RL agent, CCL captures step-by-step dependencies in sequential decision-making. We evaluate CCL on 48 diverse VRP variants, including 16 in-distribution and 32 out-of-distribution (with unseen constraints) tasks. Experimental results show that CCL performs favorably against the state-of-the-art baselines, achieving the best performance on all in-distribution tasks and the majority of out-of-distribution tasks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：上下文链式学习：面向多任务车辆路径问题的动态约束理解
多任务车辆路径问题旨在满足多样化约束的同时最小化路径成本。现有求解器通常采用统一的强化学习框架来学习跨任务的可泛化模式，但往往忽略决策过程中的约束与节点动态，导致模型难以准确响应当前上下文。为克服这一局限，本文提出上下文链式学习框架，通过渐进捕捉演化上下文以指导细粒度节点适配。具体而言，该框架通过相关性引导的上下文重构模块构建逐步的上下文信息，自适应地突出关键约束；随后通过轨迹共享的节点重嵌入模块，聚合所有轨迹上下文中的共享节点特征，并用于更新下一步的输入。通过建模强化学习代理的演化偏好，该框架捕获了序列决策中的逐步依赖关系。我们在48种不同的车辆路径问题变体上评估该框架，包括16个分布内任务和32个分布外任务。实验结果表明，该框架在全部分布内任务和大多数分布外任务上均优于现有先进基线方法。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge in multi-task Vehicle Routing Problems (VRPs) where existing reinforcement learning solvers often fail to adapt to dynamic constraints and node states during decision-making. The authors propose Chain-of-Context Learning (CCL), a framework that progressively captures evolving context through a Relevance-Guided Context Reformulation module to prioritize salient constraints, and a Trajectory-Shared Node Re-embedding module to update node features using aggregated trajectory information. Evaluated on 48 VRP variants, including in-distribution and out-of-distribution tasks with unseen constraints, CCL outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, achieving top performance on all in-distribution tasks and most out-of-distribution tasks.
本文针对多任务车辆路径问题中现有强化学习求解器在决策过程中难以适应动态约束和节点状态的问题，提出了链式上下文学习框架。该方法通过相关性引导的上下文重构模块逐步捕获演化上下文以优先处理关键约束，并利用轨迹共享节点重嵌入模块聚合轨迹信息来更新节点特征。在48个车辆路径问题变体上的实验表明，包括16个分布内任务和32个具有未见约束的分布外任务，该框架优于现有最先进基线，在所有分布内任务和大多数分布外任务上取得了最佳性能。
Relaxed Triangle Inequality for Kullback-Leibler Divergence Between Multivariate Gaussian Distributions
Authors: Shiji Xiao, Yufeng Zhang, Chubo Liu, Yan Ding, Keqin Li, Kenli Li
First: 2026-01-31T09:28:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T09:43:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The Kullback-Leibler (KL) divergence is not a proper distance metric and does not satisfy the triangle inequality, posing theoretical challenges in certain practical applications. Existing work has demonstrated that KL divergence between multivariate Gaussian distributions follows a relaxed triangle inequality. Given any three multivariate Gaussian distributions $\mathcal{N}_1, \mathcal{N}_2$, and $\mathcal{N}_3$, if $KL(\mathcal{N}_1, \mathcal{N}_2)\leq ε_1$ and $KL(\mathcal{N}_2, \mathcal{N}_3)\leq ε_2$, then $KL(\mathcal{N}_1, \mathcal{N}_3)< 3ε_1+3ε_2+2\sqrt{ε_1ε_2}+o(ε_1)+o(ε_2)$. However, the supremum of $KL(\mathcal{N}_1, \mathcal{N}_3)$ is still unknown. In this paper, we investigate the relaxed triangle inequality for the KL divergence between multivariate Gaussian distributions and give the supremum of $KL(\mathcal{N}_1, \mathcal{N}_3)$ as well as the conditions when the supremum can be attained. When $ε_1$ and $ε_2$ are small, the supremum is $ε_1+ε_2+2\sqrt{ε_1ε_2}+o(ε_1)+o(ε_2)$. Finally, we demonstrate several applications of our results in out-of-distribution detection with flow-based generative models and safe reinforcement learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：多元高斯分布间Kullback-Leibler散度的松弛三角不等式
Kullback-Leibler（KL）散度并非严格的距离度量，不满足三角不等式，这为某些实际应用带来理论挑战。现有研究表明，多元高斯分布间的KL散度遵循一种松弛的三角不等式：给定任意三个多元高斯分布$\mathcal{N}_1$、$\mathcal{N}_2$和$\mathcal{N}_3$，若$KL(\mathcal{N}_1, \mathcal{N}_2)\leq ε_1$且$KL(\mathcal{N}_2, \mathcal{N}_3)\leq ε_2$，则$KL(\mathcal{N}_1, \mathcal{N}_3)< 3ε_1+3ε_2+2\sqrt{ε_1ε_2}+o(ε_1)+o(ε_2)$，但其上确界仍未知。本文系统研究了多元高斯分布间KL散度的松弛三角不等式，给出了$KL(\mathcal{N}_1, \mathcal{N}_3)$的上确界及其可达条件：当$ε_1$和$ε_2$较小时，上确界为$ε_1+ε_2+2\sqrt{ε_1ε_2}+o(ε_1)+o(ε_2)$。最后，我们展示了该结论在基于流的生成模型分布外检测与安全强化学习中的若干应用。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the theoretical challenges posed by the Kullback-Leibler (KL) divergence not satisfying the triangle inequality, this paper investigates a relaxed triangle inequality for KL divergence between multivariate Gaussian distributions. The method involves deriving the supremum of the KL divergence between two distributions given bounds on their divergences from a common third distribution, and establishing the conditions under which this supremum is attained. The main experimental results show that for small divergence bounds, the supremum is ε₁ + ε₂ + 2√(ε₁ε₂) plus higher-order terms, and the findings are demonstrated in applications such as out-of-distribution detection with flow-based models and safe reinforcement learning.
本文的动机是Kullback-Leibler（KL）散度不满足三角不等式，这给某些实际应用带来了理论挑战。研究方法针对多元高斯分布之间的KL散度，探讨其松弛三角不等式，给出了在给定两个散度边界条件下，第三个散度的上确界及其可达条件。主要实验结果表明，当散度边界较小时，上确界为ε₁ + ε₂ + 2√(ε₁ε₂)加上高阶项，并将该结果应用于基于流的生成模型的分布外检测和安全强化学习等领域。
PAPN: Proximity Attention Encoder and Pointer Network Decoder for Parcel Pickup Route Prediction
Authors: Hansi Denis, Ali Anwar, Ngoc-Quang Luong, Siegfried Mercelis
First: 2025-04-30T08:24:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T09:17:32+00:00
Comments: 10 pages, 2 figures, 2 tables, WCTR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Optimization of the last-mile delivery and first-mile pickup of parcels is integral to the logistics optimization pipeline as it entails both cost and resource efficiency and a heightened service quality. Such optimization requires accurate route and time prediction systems to adapt to different scenarios in advance. This work tackles the first building block, namely route prediction. The novel Proximity Attention (PA) mechanism is coupled to a Pointer Network (PN) decoder to leverage the underlying connections between the different visitable pickup positions at each timestep of the parcel pickup process. This local attention is coupled with global context computing via a multi-head attention transformer encoder. Both attentions are then mixed for complete and comprehensive modeling of the problems. PA is also used in the decoding process to skew predictions towards the locations with the highest visit likeliness, thus using inter-connectivity of nodes for next-location prediction. This method is trained, validated and tested on a large industry-level dataset of real-world, last-mile delivery and first-mile pickup named LaDE (2024). This approach outperforms all state-of-the-art supervised methods in terms of most metrics used for benchmarking on this dataset while still being competitive with the best-performing reinforcement learning framework named DRL4Route (2023).
中文标题/摘要
标题：PAPN：基于邻近注意力编码器与指针网络解码器的包裹取件路径预测
包裹的末端配送与首程取件优化是物流优化流程的核心环节，关乎成本与资源效率及服务质量的提升。此类优化需依赖精准的路径与时间预测系统以提前适应不同场景。本研究聚焦于基础模块——路径预测，创新性地将邻近注意力机制与指针网络解码器结合，以利用包裹取件过程中各时间步可访问取件点间的潜在关联。该局部注意力通过多头注意力变换器编码器与全局上下文计算耦合，二者混合后实现对问题的完整建模。邻近注意力亦用于解码过程，使预测偏向访问概率最高的位置，从而利用节点间的互连性进行下一位置预测。该方法在名为LaDE（2024）的大规模工业级真实末端配送与首程取件数据集上完成训练、验证与测试，在多数评估指标上超越所有现有监督学习方法，并与性能最优的强化学习框架DRL4Route（2023）保持竞争力。

This paper addresses the need for accurate route prediction in last-mile delivery and first-mile pickup to optimize logistics efficiency and service quality. The authors propose a novel model combining a Proximity Attention (PA) mechanism with a Pointer Network (PN) decoder, where PA captures local connections between pickup locations at each timestep and is integrated with a transformer encoder for global context. 本文针对最后一公里配送和首公里取件的路线预测需求，旨在优化物流效率和提升服务质量。作者提出了一种新颖模型，将邻近注意力机制与指针网络解码器相结合，其中邻近注意力捕捉每个时间步取件位置间的局部关联，并与Transformer编码器集成以获取全局上下文。在行业级LaDE数据集上的实验结果表明，该方法在多数评估指标上优于现有监督学习方法，并与领先的强化学习框架DRL4Route保持竞争力。
ToolRLA: Fine-Grained Reward Decomposition for Tool-Integrated Reinforcement Learning Alignment in Domain-Specific Agents
Authors: Pengbo Liu
First: 2026-03-02T08:52:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T08:52:14+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Tool-integrated reasoning agents interleaving natural language deliberation with external API calls show promise for complex multi-step tasks. However, aligning such agents for high-stakes domain-specific deployment is challenging, as existing reinforcement learning uses coarse binary rewards (success/failure) that insufficiently guide nuanced tool invocation in production. We present ToolRLA, a three-stage post-training pipeline (Supervised Fine-Tuning, Group Relative Policy Optimization, Direct Preference Optimization) for domain-specific tool-integrated agents. Its core is a fine-grained reward function with multiplicative correctness decomposition, evaluating tool invocation across four dimensions: format validity, tool selection correctness, invocation efficiency, and domain constraint compliance. Multiplicative composition prioritizes correct tool selection (a prerequisite for meaningful parameter evaluation), while a large negative compliance penalty (λ=10) ensures regulatory adherence. Deployed on a real-world financial advisory copilot (80+ advisors, 1,200+ daily queries, 15+ heterogeneous APIs), ToolRLA achieves 47% higher end-to-end task completion (62% to 91%), 63% lower tool invocation error (38% to 14%), 93% lower regulatory violation (12% to 0.8%), and sub-2-second latency after three months. Ablation studies confirm fine-grained reward decomposition contributes 7 percentage points over coarse additive rewards; generalizability is validated on ToolBench and API-Bank.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ToolRLA：面向领域专用智能体的工具集成强化学习对齐中的细粒度奖励分解方法
工具集成推理智能体通过自然语言推演与外部API调用的交替执行，在复杂多步骤任务中展现出潜力。然而，为高风险领域专用场景对齐此类智能体面临挑战：现有强化学习采用粗粒度的二元奖励（成功/失败），难以在生产环境中细致引导工具调用。本文提出ToolRLA——面向领域专用工具集成智能体的三阶段后训练流程（监督微调、分组相对策略优化、直接偏好优化），其核心是通过乘法式正确性分解构建的细粒度奖励函数，从四个维度评估工具调用：格式有效性、工具选择正确性、调用效率、领域约束合规性。乘法组合优先保证工具选择正确性（参数评估的前提条件），同时通过大幅合规惩罚系数（λ=10）确保监管遵从。在实际金融顾问协理系统（80+顾问、1200+日查询量、15+异构API）部署后，ToolRLA使端到端任务完成率提升47%（62%→91%），工具调用错误率降低63%（38%→14%），违规率下降93%（12%→0.8%），并在三个月后实现亚2秒延迟。消融实验证实细粒度奖励分解较粗粒度加法奖励提升7个百分点；在ToolBench与API-Bank上的测试验证了方法的泛化能力。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of aligning tool-integrated reasoning agents for high-stakes domain-specific tasks, where coarse binary rewards in reinforcement learning fail to guide nuanced tool invocation. It introduces ToolRLA, a three-stage post-training pipeline featuring a fine-grained reward function that multiplicatively decomposes correctness into four dimensions: format validity, tool selection, invocation efficiency, and domain constraint compliance, with a heavy penalty for regulatory violations to prioritize adherence. In deployment on a financial advisory copilot, the method significantly improved end-to-end task completion by 47%, reduced tool invocation errors by 63%, cut regulatory violations by 93%, and maintained sub-2-second latency, with ablation studies showing a 7-percentage-point gain from fine-grained rewards and validation on benchmarks confirming generalizability.
本文针对高风险领域特定任务中工具集成推理智能体的对齐挑战，指出传统强化学习使用的粗粒度二元奖励无法有效指导细粒度工具调用。提出了ToolRLA方法，这是一个包含三阶段的后训练流程，其核心是一个细粒度奖励函数，通过乘法分解将正确性评估为四个维度：格式有效性、工具选择正确性、调用效率和领域约束合规性，并设置高额违规惩罚以确保合规优先。在实际金融顾问助手的部署中，该方法将端到端任务完成率提升47%，工具调用错误降低63%，违规率减少93%，并保持亚2秒延迟，消融实验证实细粒度奖励分解相比粗粒度加法奖励带来7个百分点的提升，且在通用基准上验证了泛化能力。
Towards Efficient Large Language Reasoning Models via Extreme-Ratio Chain-of-Thought Compression
Authors: Yuntian Tang, Bohan Jia, Wenxuan Huang, Lianyue Zhang, Jiao Xie, Wenxi Li, Rongrong Ji, Shaohui Lin
First: 2026-02-09T06:57:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T08:47:20+00:00
Comments: 15 pages, 7 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Chain-of-Thought (CoT) reasoning successfully enhances the reasoning capabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs), yet it incurs substantial computational overhead for inference. Existing CoT compression methods often suffer from a critical loss of logical fidelity at high compression ratios, resulting in significant performance degradation. To achieve high-fidelity, fast reasoning, we propose a novel EXTreme-RAtio Chain-of-Thought Compression framework, termed Extra-CoT, which aggressively reduces the token budget while preserving answer accuracy. To generate reliable, high-fidelity supervision, we first train a dedicated semantically-preserved compressor on mathematical CoT data with fine-grained annotations. An LLM is then fine-tuned on these compressed pairs via a mixed-ratio supervised fine-tuning (SFT), teaching it to follow a spectrum of compression budgets and providing a stable initialization for reinforcement learning (RL). We further propose Constrained and Hierarchical Ratio Policy Optimization (CHRPO) to explicitly incentivize question-solving ability under lower budgets by a hierarchical reward. Experiments on three mathematical reasoning benchmarks show the superiority of Extra-CoT. For example, on MATH-500 using Qwen3-1.7B, Extra-CoT achieves over 73\% token reduction with an accuracy improvement of 0.6\%, significantly outperforming state-of-the-art (SOTA) methods. Our source codes have been released at https://github.com/Mwie1024/Extra-CoT.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向高效大语言推理模型的极端比例思维链压缩方法
思维链推理虽成功增强了大语言模型的推理能力，但其推理过程会产生巨大的计算开销。现有思维链压缩方法在高压缩比下常出现逻辑保真度的严重损失，导致性能显著下降。为实现高保真度的快速推理，我们提出了一种新颖的极端比例思维链压缩框架（简称Extra-CoT），该框架在保持答案准确性的同时大幅降低令牌预算。为生成可靠的高保真度监督信号，我们首先在具有细粒度标注的数学思维链数据上训练专用的语义保持压缩器，随后通过混合比例监督微调在大语言模型上对这些压缩对进行微调，使其能适应不同压缩预算，并为强化学习提供稳定初始化。我们进一步提出约束分层比例策略优化，通过分层奖励机制显式激励模型在更低预算下保持解题能力。在三个数学推理基准测试上的实验证明了Extra-CoT的优越性。例如，在Qwen3-1.7B模型上使用MATH-500数据集时，Extra-CoT实现了超过73%的令牌缩减，同时准确率提升0.6%，显著优于现有最优方法。源代码已发布于https://github.com/Mwie1024/Extra-CoT。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the substantial computational overhead incurred by Chain-of-Thought (CoT) reasoning in Large Language Models (LLMs), as existing compression methods often lose logical fidelity at high ratios, degrading performance. The proposed method, Extra-CoT, is a framework for extreme-ratio CoT compression that first trains a dedicated compressor to generate high-fidelity supervision from annotated mathematical CoT data, then fine-tunes an LLM via mixed-ratio supervised fine-tuning, and further applies a novel reinforcement learning approach called Constrained and Hierarchical Ratio Policy Optimization (CHRPO) to explicitly incentivize question-solving under low token budgets. Main experimental results on three mathematical reasoning benchmarks demonstrate its superiority; for instance, on MATH-500 using Qwen3-1.7B, it achieves over 73% token reduction with a 0.6% accuracy improvement, significantly outperforming state-of-the-art methods.
本研究的动机是解决大语言模型中思维链推理带来的巨大计算开销，因为现有压缩方法在高压缩比下常损失逻辑保真度，导致性能下降。所提出的方法Extra-CoT是一个极端比率思维链压缩框架，首先训练一个专用压缩器，从带细粒度标注的数学思维链数据中生成高保真监督信号，然后通过混合比率监督微调对大语言模型进行微调，并进一步应用一种称为约束分层比率策略优化的新型强化学习方法，以明确激励在低令牌预算下的问题解决能力。在三个数学推理基准上的主要实验结果表明了其优越性；例如，在MATH-500数据集上使用Qwen3-1.7B模型，实现了超过73%的令牌减少和0.6%的准确率提升，显著优于现有最先进方法。
CARE: Towards Clinical Accountability in Multi-Modal Medical Reasoning with an Evidence-Grounded Agentic Framework
Authors: Yuexi Du, Jinglu Wang, Shujie Liu, Nicha C. Dvornek, Yan Lu
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-03-02T08:38:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T08:38:37+00:00
Comments: Accepted by ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large visual language models (VLMs) have shown strong multi-modal medical reasoning ability, but most operate as end-to-end black boxes, diverging from clinicians' evidence-based, staged workflows and hindering clinical accountability. Complementarily, expert visual grounding models can accurately localize regions of interest (ROIs), providing explicit, reliable evidence that improves both reasoning accuracy and trust. In this paper, we introduce CARE, advancing Clinical Accountability in multi-modal medical Reasoning with an Evidence-grounded agentic framework. Unlike existing approaches that couple grounding and reasoning within a single generalist model, CARE decomposes the task into coordinated sub-modules to reduce shortcut learning and hallucination: a compact VLM proposes relevant medical entities; an expert entity-referring segmentation model produces pixel-level ROI evidence; and a grounded VLM reasons over the full image augmented by ROI hints. The VLMs are optimized with reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards to align answers with supporting evidence. Furthermore, a VLM coordinator plans tool invocation and reviews evidence-answer consistency, providing agentic control and final verification. Evaluated on standard medical VQA benchmarks, our CARE-Flow (coordinator-free) improves average accuracy by 10.9% over the same size (10B) state-of-the-art (SOTA). With dynamic planning and answer review, our CARE-Coord yields a further gain, outperforming the heavily pre-trained SOTA by 5.2%. Our experiments demonstrate that an agentic framework that emulates clinical workflows, incorporating decoupled specialized models and explicit evidence, yields more accurate and accountable medical AI.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CARE：基于证据驱动的智能体框架实现多模态医学推理的临床可问责性
大型视觉语言模型（VLM）已展现出强大的多模态医学推理能力，但多数模型作为端到端黑箱运行，与临床医生基于证据的分阶段工作流程相悖，且阻碍了临床可问责性。互补地，专家级视觉定位模型能精准定位感兴趣区域（ROI），提供显式可靠的证据，从而提升推理准确性与可信度。本文提出CARE框架，通过证据驱动的智能体架构推进多模态医学推理的临床可问责性。与现有将定位与推理耦合于单一通用模型的方法不同，CARE将任务分解为协同子模块以减少捷径学习与幻觉：紧凑型VLM提出相关医学实体；专家级实体参照分割模型生成像素级ROI证据；基于证据的VLM结合ROI提示对完整图像进行推理。VLM通过可验证奖励的强化学习进行优化，确保答案与支持证据对齐。此外，VLM协调器规划工具调用并核查证据-答案一致性，提供智能体控制与最终验证。在标准医学VQA基准测试中，CARE-Flow（无协调器版本）相比同规模（100亿参数）的先进模型平均准确率提升10.9%；而具备动态规划与答案审查的CARE-Coord进一步获得增益，以5.2%的优势超越经过大量预训练的先进模型。实验表明，模拟临床工作流程、融合解耦专用模型与显式证据的智能体框架能产生更精准且可问责的医学人工智能。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to align AI with clinicians' evidence-based workflows and improve accountability in medical reasoning, this paper introduces CARE, an agentic framework that decomposes multi-modal medical question-answering into specialized, coordinated modules to reduce hallucinations. The method employs a compact VLM to propose medical entities, an expert segmentation model to produce pixel-level region-of-interest evidence, and a grounded VLM to reason over the image augmented with this evidence, with reinforcement learning used to align answers with supporting evidence and a coordinator module for dynamic planning and verification. Experimental results on medical VQA benchmarks show that the coordinator-free version (CARE-Flow) improves average accuracy by 10.9% over a same-size state-of-the-art model, and the full framework (CARE-Coord) further outperforms a heavily pre-trained SOTA by 5.2%, demonstrating that emulating clinical workflows with explicit evidence yields more accurate and accountable AI.
本文的动机是使人工智能与临床医生基于证据的工作流程保持一致，并提高医学推理的可问责性，为此提出了CARE框架，该框架将多模态医学问答分解为专门化、协同的模块以减少幻觉。方法上，它使用紧凑的视觉语言模型提出医学实体，由专家分割模型生成像素级的感兴趣区域证据，再由一个基于证据的视觉语言模型结合图像和证据进行推理，并通过强化学习使答案与证据对齐，同时引入协调器模块进行动态规划和验证。在标准医学视觉问答基准上的实验结果表明，无协调器版本（CARE-Flow）的平均准确率比同等规模的最先进模型提高了10.9%，而完整框架（CARE-Coord）进一步超越了经过大量预训练的SOTA模型5.2%，证明通过模拟临床工作流程并引入显式证据，能产生更准确且可问责的医学人工智能。
Inverse Reinforcement Learning with Dynamic Reward Scaling for LLM Alignment
Authors: Ruoxi Cheng, Haoxuan Ma, Weixin Wang, Ranjie Duan, Jiexi Liu, Xiaoshuang Jia, Simeng Qin, Xiaochun Cao, Yang Liu, Xiaojun Jia
First: 2025-03-23T16:40:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T08:36:34+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Alignment is vital for safely deploying large language models (LLMs). Existing techniques are either reward-based (training a reward model on preference pairs and optimizing with reinforcement learning) or reward-free (directly fine-tuning on ranked outputs). Recent research shows that well-tuned reward-based pipelines remain the most robust, and single-response demonstrations can outperform pairwise preference data. However, there still exist two key challenges: (1) imbalanced safety datasets that overrepresent common hazards while neglecting long-tail threats; and (2) static reward models that ignore task difficulty, limiting optimization efficiency and attainable gains. To address these limitations, we propose DR-IRL, which Dynamically adjusts Rewards through Inverse Reinforcement Learning. We first train category-specific reward models using a balanced safety dataset of seven harmful categories as demonstration via IRL. Then we enhance Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) by introducing dynamic reward scaling: adjusting rewards by task difficulty, data-level hardness by text encoder cosine similarity, and model-level responsiveness by reward gaps. Extensive experiments across various benchmarks and LLMs demonstrate that DR-IRL outperforms all baseline methods in safety alignment while maintaining usefulness.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于动态奖励缩放的反向强化学习用于大语言模型对齐
对齐对于安全部署大语言模型至关重要。现有技术分为基于奖励的方法（通过偏好对训练奖励模型，并用强化学习优化）和无奖励方法（直接对排序输出进行微调）。近期研究表明，调优良好的基于奖励流程仍是最稳健的，且单响应演示可优于成对偏好数据。但仍存在两大挑战：（1）安全数据集不平衡，过度代表常见风险而忽略长尾威胁；（2）静态奖励模型忽略任务难度，限制了优化效率和可获收益。为解决这些局限，我们提出DR-IRL，通过反向强化学习动态调整奖励。首先利用包含七类有害类别的平衡安全数据集作为演示，通过IRL训练特定类别奖励模型。随后通过引入动态奖励缩放增强组相对策略优化：依据任务难度、基于文本编码器余弦相似度的数据级难度，以及基于奖励差距的模型级响应度来调整奖励。跨多种基准和大语言模型的广泛实验表明，DR-IRL在保持实用性的同时，其安全对齐性能优于所有基线方法。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses two key challenges in aligning large language models (LLMs): imbalanced safety datasets that overlook long-tail threats and static reward models that ignore task difficulty, which limit optimization efficiency. The proposed method, DR-IRL, dynamically adjusts rewards through inverse reinforcement learning by first training category-specific reward models on a balanced safety dataset across seven harmful categories and then enhancing Group Relative Policy Optimization with dynamic scaling based on task difficulty, data-level hardness via text encoder similarity, and model-level responsiveness via reward gaps. Experimental results across various benchmarks and LLMs show that DR-IRL outperforms baseline methods in safety alignment while preserving model usefulness.
本文针对大语言模型对齐中的两个关键挑战：忽视长尾威胁的不平衡安全数据集，以及忽略任务难度从而限制优化效率的静态奖励模型。提出的方法DR-IRL通过逆强化学习动态调整奖励，首先使用涵盖七种有害类别的平衡安全数据集训练类别特定奖励模型，然后通过基于任务难度、文本编码器相似度的数据级硬度和奖励差距的模型级响应性进行动态缩放，增强了组相对策略优化。在各种基准测试和大语言模型上的实验结果表明，DR-IRL在保持模型实用性的同时，在安全对齐方面优于所有基线方法。
Beyond Length Scaling: Synergizing Breadth and Depth for Generative Reward Models
Authors: Qiyuan Zhang, Yufei Wang, Tianhe Wu, Can Xu, Qingfeng Sun, Kai Zheng, Xue Liu, Chen Ma
First: 2026-03-02T07:54:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T07:54:29+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Recent advancements in Generative Reward Models (GRMs) have demonstrated that scaling the length of Chain-of-Thought (CoT) reasoning considerably enhances the reliability of evaluation. However, current works predominantly rely on unstructured length scaling, ignoring the divergent efficacy of different reasoning mechanisms: Breadth-CoT (B-CoT, i.e., multi-dimensional principle coverage) and Depth-CoT (D-CoT, i.e., substantive judgment soundness). To address this, we introduce Mix-GRM, a framework that reconfigures raw rationales into structured B-CoT and D-CoT through a modular synthesis pipeline, subsequently employing Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) and Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) to internalize and optimize these mechanisms. Comprehensive experiments demonstrate that Mix-GRM establishes a new state-of-the-art across five benchmarks, surpassing leading open-source RMs by an average of 8.2\%. Our results reveal a clear divergence in reasoning: B-CoT benefits subjective preference tasks, whereas D-CoT excels in objective correctness tasks. Consequently, misaligning the reasoning mechanism with the task directly degrades performance. Furthermore, we demonstrate that RLVR acts as a switching amplifier, inducing an emergent polarization where the model spontaneously allocates its reasoning style to match task demands. The synthesized data and models are released at \href{https://huggingface.co/collections/DonJoey/mix-grm}{Hugging Face}, and the code is released at \href{https://github.com/Don-Joey/Mix-GRM}{Github}.
中文标题/摘要
标题：超越长度扩展：融合广度与深度以优化生成式奖励模型
近期生成式奖励模型（GRM）的研究表明，扩展思维链（CoT）推理长度能显著提升评估可靠性。然而，现有工作主要依赖非结构化的长度扩展，忽视了不同推理机制（广度思维链B-CoT，即多维原则覆盖；深度思维链D-CoT，即实质性判断稳健性）的效能差异。为此，我们提出Mix-GRM框架：通过模块化合成流程将原始理据重构为结构化B-CoT与D-CoT，并采用监督微调（SFT）及可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）实现机制内化与优化。综合实验表明，Mix-GRM在五项基准测试中均达到最优性能，平均超越主流开源奖励模型8.2%。研究揭示推理机制存在明确分化：B-CoT利于主观偏好任务，D-CoT擅长客观正确性任务，机制与任务错配将直接导致性能下降。此外，RLVR可作为切换放大器，引发模型自发分配推理风格以适应任务需求的极化现象。合成数据与模型发布于Hugging Face平台，代码发布于Github仓库。

The paper is motivated by the observation that current Generative Reward Models (GRMs) scale reasoning length in an unstructured way, overlooking the distinct benefits of breadth-oriented (B-CoT) and depth-oriented (D-CoT) reasoning mechanisms. To address this, the authors propose Mix-GRM, a framework that restructures raw rationales into structured B-CoT and D-CoT via a modular pipeline, then uses Supervised Fine-Tuning and Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards to internalize and optimize these reasoning styles. Experimental results on five benchmarks show that Mix-GRM achieves a new state-of-the-art, outperforming leading open-source reward models by an average of 8.2%, and reveals that B-CoT is more effective for subjective preference tasks while D-CoT excels in objective correctness tasks, with misalignment degrading performance; furthermore, the reinforcement learning component acts as a switching amplifier, enabling the model to spontaneously polarize its reasoning style to match task demands.

Adversarial Query Synthesis via Bayesian Optimization
Authors: Jeffrey Tao, Yimeng Zeng, Haydn Thomas Jones, Natalie Maus, Osbert Bastani, Jacob R. Gardner, Ryan Marcus
First: 2026-03-02T07:50:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T07:50:46+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Benchmark workloads are extremely important to the database management research community, especially as more machine learning components are integrated into database systems. Here, we propose a Bayesian optimization technique to automatically search for difficult benchmark queries, significantly reducing the amount of manual effort usually required. In preliminary experiments, we show that our approach can generate queries with more than double the optimization headroom compared to existing benchmarks.

LFPO: Likelihood-Free Policy Optimization for Masked Diffusion Models
Authors: Chenxing Wei, Jiazhen Kang, Hong Wang, Jianqing Zhang, Hao Jiang, Xiaolong Xu, Ningyuan Sun, Ying He, F. Richard Yu, Yao Shu, Bo Jiang
First: 2026-03-02T07:42:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T07:42:55+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has achieved remarkable success in improving autoregressive models, especially in domains requiring correctness like mathematical reasoning and code generation. However, directly applying such paradigms to Diffusion Large Language Models (dLLMs) is fundamentally hindered by the intractability of exact likelihood computation, which forces existing methods to rely on high-variance approximations. To bridge this gap, we propose Likelihood-Free Policy Optimization (LFPO), a native framework that maps the concept of vector field flow matching to the discrete token space. Specifically, LFPO formulates alignment as geometric velocity rectification, which directly optimizes denoising logits via contrastive updates. This design effectively bypasses the errors inherent in likelihood approximation, yielding the precise gradient estimation. Furthermore, LFPO enforce consistency by predicting final solutions from intermediate steps, effectively straightening the probability flow to enable high-quality generation with significantly fewer iterations. Extensive experiments demonstrate that LFPO not only outperforms state-of-the-art baselines on code and reasoning benchmarks but also accelerates inference by approximately 20% through reduced diffusion steps.
中文标题/摘要
标题：LFPO：基于掩码扩散模型的免似然策略优化
可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）在提升自回归模型性能方面取得了显著成就，尤其在数学推理与代码生成等需要严格正确性的领域。然而，由于精确似然计算难以处理，现有方法被迫依赖高方差近似，这从根本上阻碍了将该范式直接应用于扩散大语言模型（dLLM）。为弥合这一差距，我们提出免似然策略优化（LFPO），这是一个将向量场流匹配概念映射到离散词元空间的原生框架。具体而言，LFPO将对齐问题构建为几何速度校正，通过对比更新直接优化去噪逻辑值。该设计有效规避了似然近似固有的误差，实现了精确的梯度估计。此外，LFPO通过从中间步骤预测最终解来强化一致性，有效拉直概率流，从而以显著更少的迭代次数实现高质量生成。大量实验表明，LFPO不仅在代码与推理基准测试中超越现有先进基线，还通过减少扩散步骤将推理速度提升约20%。
