The motivation for this work stems from the challenge of applying Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) to Diffusion Large Language Models (dLLMs), as exact likelihood computation is intractable, forcing existing methods to rely on high-variance approximations. To address this, the authors propose Likelihood-Free Policy Optimization (LFPO), a native framework that maps vector field flow matching to discrete token space by formulating alignment as geometric velocity rectification, which directly optimizes denoising logits via contrastive updates to bypass likelihood approximation errors. Experimental results show that LFPO outperforms state-of-the-art baselines on code and reasoning benchmarks while accelerating inference by approximately 20% through reduced diffusion steps, thanks to its consistency enforcement that straightens the probability flow.
本研究的动机源于将可验证奖励的强化学习应用于扩散大语言模型时面临的挑战，因为精确似然计算难以处理，迫使现有方法依赖高方差近似。为此，作者提出了无似然策略优化方法，这是一个将向量场流匹配映射到离散令牌空间的本土框架，通过将对齐表述为几何速度校正，直接通过对比更新优化去噪逻辑值，从而绕过似然近似误差。实验结果表明，该方法在代码和推理基准测试中优于现有先进基线，同时通过减少扩散步骤将推理速度提升了约20%，这得益于其通过一致性预测拉直概率流的设计。
State-Action Inpainting Diffuser for Continuous Control with Delay
Authors: Dongqi Han, Wei Wang, Enze Zhang, Dongsheng Li
First: 2026-03-02T07:28:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T07:28:27+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Signal delay poses a fundamental challenge in continuous control and reinforcement learning (RL) by introducing a temporal gap between interaction and perception. Current solutions have largely evolved along two distinct paradigms: model-free approaches which utilize state augmentation to preserve Markovian properties, and model-based methods which focus on inferring latent beliefs via dynamics modeling. In this paper, we bridge these perspectives by introducing State-Action Inpainting Diffuser (SAID), a framework that integrates the inductive bias of dynamics learning with the direct decision-making capability of policy optimization. By formulating the problem as a joint sequence inpainting task, SAID implicitly captures environmental dynamics while directly generating consistent plans, effectively operating at the intersection of model-based and model-free paradigms. Crucially, this generative formulation allows SAID to be seamlessly applied to both online and offline RL. Extensive experiments on delayed continuous control benchmarks demonstrate that SAID achieves state-of-the-art and robust performance. Our study suggests a new methodology to advance the field of RL with delay.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向延迟连续控制的状态-动作修复扩散模型
信号延迟在交互与感知间引入时间差，对连续控制与强化学习构成根本性挑战。现有解决方案主要沿两种范式发展：一是采用状态增强保持马尔可夫性的无模型方法，二是通过动力学建模推断潜在信念的基于模型方法。本文通过提出状态-动作修复扩散模型（SAID）融合这两种视角，该框架将动力学学习的归纳偏置与策略优化的直接决策能力相结合。通过将问题构建为联合序列修复任务，SAID在直接生成一致性规划的同时隐式捕捉环境动态，有效运行于基于模型与无模型范式的交叉领域。关键的是，这种生成式框架使SAID能无缝应用于在线与离线强化学习。在延迟连续控制基准测试中的大量实验表明，SAID实现了最先进且鲁棒的性能。本研究为推进延迟强化学习领域提出了新的方法论。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of signal delay in continuous control and reinforcement learning, which disrupts the alignment between interaction and perception. The authors propose the State-Action Inpainting Diffuser (SAID), a framework that bridges model-based and model-free paradigms by formulating delayed control as a joint sequence inpainting task, thereby integrating dynamics learning with direct policy optimization. Experimental results on delayed continuous control benchmarks show that SAID achieves state-of-the-art and robust performance, offering a unified approach applicable to both online and offline RL settings.
本文针对连续控制和强化学习中信号延迟导致交互与感知错位的挑战，提出了状态-动作修复扩散模型（SAID）。该方法通过将延迟控制问题构建为联合序列修复任务，融合了基于模型和无模型范式的优势，在隐式学习环境动态的同时直接生成一致的行动计划。在延迟连续控制基准测试上的实验表明，SAID实现了最先进且稳健的性能，为在线和离线强化学习提供了一种统一的新方法。
Model Predictive Adversarial Imitation Learning for Planning from Observation
Authors: Tyler Han, Yanda Bao, Bhaumik Mehta, Gabriel Guo, Anubhav Vishwakarma, Emily Kang, Sanghun Jung, Rosario Scalise, Jason Zhou, Bryan Xu, Byron Boots
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-07-29T06:52:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T07:07:08+00:00
Comments: Accepted at ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Human demonstration data is often ambiguous and incomplete, motivating imitation learning approaches that also exhibit reliable planning behavior. A common paradigm to perform planning-from-demonstration involves learning a reward function via Inverse Reinforcement Learning (IRL) then deploying this reward via Model Predictive Control (MPC). Towards unifying these methods, we derive a replacement of the policy in IRL with a planning-based agent. With connections to Adversarial Imitation Learning, this formulation enables end-to-end interactive learning of planners from observation-only demonstrations. In addition to benefits in interpretability, complexity, and safety, we study and observe significant improvements on sample efficiency, out-of-distribution generalization, and robustness. The study includes evaluations in both simulated control benchmarks and real-world navigation experiments using few-to-single observation-only demonstrations.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于模型预测对抗模仿学习的观察规划方法
人类示范数据常存在模糊性与不完整性，这推动了兼具可靠规划行为的模仿学习方法的发展。当前基于示范的规划范式通常通过逆强化学习学习奖励函数，再借助模型预测控制实施该奖励机制。为整合这些方法，本研究提出用基于规划的智能体替代逆强化学习中的策略模块。通过与对抗模仿学习的理论关联，该框架实现了从纯观察示范到规划器的端到端交互式学习。除在可解释性、复杂度和安全性方面的优势外，研究还观察到该方法在样本效率、分布外泛化及鲁棒性上的显著提升。实验涵盖模拟控制基准测试和仅使用少量至单次纯观察示范的真实导航场景验证。

The paper addresses the challenge of learning from ambiguous and incomplete human demonstrations by unifying inverse reinforcement learning (IRL) with planning, motivated by the need for reliable planning behavior in imitation learning. The method replaces the policy in IRL with a planning-based agent, integrating adversarial imitation learning to enable end-to-end interactive learning from observation-only demonstrations. Experimental results in simulated control benchmarks and real-world navigation show significant improvements in sample efficiency, out-of-distribution generalization, and robustness, using few-to-single demonstrations.
该论文针对人类演示数据模糊和不完整的问题，旨在通过统一逆强化学习与规划来提升模仿学习中的可靠规划能力。方法上，它将逆强化学习中的策略替换为基于规划的智能体，结合对抗模仿学习实现从纯观察演示的端到端交互学习。在模拟控制基准和真实世界导航实验中的评估表明，该方法使用极少甚至单次演示，显著提高了样本效率、分布外泛化能力和鲁棒性。
GAC: Stabilizing Asynchronous RL Training for LLMs via Gradient Alignment Control
Authors: Haofeng Xu, Junwei Su, Yukun Tian, Lansong Diao, Zhengping Qian, Chuan Wu
First: 2026-03-02T06:19:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T06:19:43+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Asynchronous execution is essential for scaling reinforcement learning (RL) to modern large model workloads, including large language models and AI agents, but it can fundamentally alter RL optimization behavior. While prior work on asynchronous RL focuses on training throughput and distributional correction, we show that naively applying asynchrony to policy-gradient updates can induce qualitatively different training dynamics and lead to severe training instability. Through systematic empirical and theoretical analysis, we identify a key signature of this instability: asynchronous training exhibits persistently high cosine similarity between consecutive policy gradients, in contrast to the near-orthogonal updates observed under synchronized training. This stale-aligned gradient effect amplifies correlated updates and increases the risk of overshooting and divergence. Motivated by this observation, we propose GRADIENT ALIGNMENT CONTROL(GAC), a simple dynamics-aware stabilization method that regulates asynchronous RL progress along stale-aligned directions via gradient projection. We establish convergence guarantees under bounded staleness and demonstrate empirically that GAC recovers stable, on-policy training dynamics and matches synchronized baselines even at high staleness.
中文标题/摘要
标题：GAC：通过梯度对齐控制稳定大型语言模型的异步强化学习训练
异步执行对于将强化学习扩展到现代大规模模型工作负载（包括大型语言模型和AI智能体）至关重要，但它可能从根本上改变强化学习的优化行为。尽管先前关于异步强化学习的研究主要关注训练吞吐量和分布校正，但我们发现，将异步机制简单应用于策略梯度更新可能导致训练动态发生质变，并引发严重的训练不稳定性。通过系统的实证与理论分析，我们识别出这种不稳定性的关键特征：异步训练中连续策略梯度间持续保持较高的余弦相似度，而同步训练下则观察到近乎正交的更新。这种陈旧对齐梯度效应放大了相关更新，增加了过冲和发散的风险。基于此观察，我们提出了梯度对齐控制（GAC），这是一种简单的动态感知稳定方法，通过梯度投影调节沿陈旧对齐方向的异步强化学习进程。我们在有界陈旧性条件下建立了收敛保证，并通过实验证明，即使在高陈旧性情况下，GAC也能恢复稳定的同策略训练动态，并匹配同步基准性能。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work stems from the need to scale reinforcement learning (RL) for large language models and AI agents via asynchronous execution, which, while boosting throughput, can induce severe training instability. The method proposed, Gradient Alignment Control (GAC), addresses this by identifying that asynchronous policy-gradient updates lead to persistently high cosine similarity between consecutive gradients—a stale-aligned gradient effect—and stabilizes training via a dynamics-aware gradient projection technique that regulates progress along these aligned directions. Experimental results demonstrate that GAC recovers stable, on-policy training dynamics, matches the performance of synchronized baselines even under high staleness conditions, and is supported by convergence guarantees under bounded staleness.
本研究的动机在于通过异步执行来扩展强化学习（RL）以适用于大语言模型和AI智能体等大规模工作负载，但异步操作可能导致严重的训练不稳定问题。所提出的方法——梯度对齐控制（GAC）——通过分析发现异步策略梯度更新会导致连续梯度间持续保持高余弦相似性（即陈旧对齐梯度效应），并采用一种动态感知的梯度投影技术来调控沿这些对齐方向的训练进程，从而稳定训练。实验结果表明，GAC能够恢复稳定的同策略训练动态，即使在高陈旧度条件下也能达到与同步基线相当的性能，并且在有界陈旧度下具有收敛保证。
SpotAgent: Grounding Visual Geo-localization in Large Vision-Language Models through Agentic Reasoning
Authors: Furong Jia, Ling Dai, Wenjin Deng, Fan Zhang, Chen Hu, Daxin Jiang, Yu Liu
First: 2026-02-10T06:57:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T06:18:27+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Vision-Language Models (LVLMs) have demonstrated strong reasoning capabilities in geo-localization, yet they often struggle in real-world scenarios where visual cues are sparse, long-tailed, and highly ambiguous. Previous approaches, bound by internal knowledge, often fail to provide verifiable results, yielding confident but ungrounded predictions when faced with confounded evidence. To address these challenges, we propose SpotAgent, a framework that formalizes geo-localization into an agentic reasoning process that leverages expert-level reasoning to synergize visual interpretation with tool-assisted verification. SpotAgent actively explores and verifies visual cues by leveraging external tools (e.g., web search, maps) through a ReAct diagram. We introduce a 3-stage post-training pipeline starting with a Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) stage for basic alignment, followed by an Agentic Cold Start phase utilizing high-quality trajectories synthesized via a Multi-Agent framework, aiming to instill tool-calling expertise. Subsequently, the model's reasoning capabilities are refined through Reinforcement Learning. We propose a Spatially-Aware Dynamic Filtering strategy to enhance the efficiency of the RL stage by prioritizing learnable samples based on spatial difficulty. Extensive experiments on standard benchmarks demonstrate that SpotAgent achieves state-of-the-art performance, effectively mitigating hallucinations while delivering precise and verifiable geo-localization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SpotAgent：通过智能体推理将视觉地理定位能力植入大型视觉语言模型
大型视觉语言模型在视觉地理定位任务中展现出强大的推理能力，但在视觉线索稀疏、长尾分布且高度模糊的真实场景中仍面临挑战。现有方法受限于内部知识库，常因证据混淆而产生自信但缺乏依据的预测，且难以提供可验证结果。为此，我们提出SpotAgent框架，将地理定位形式化为智能体推理过程，通过专家级推理实现视觉解析与工具辅助验证的协同。该框架借助ReAct决策图，利用外部工具（如网络搜索、地图服务）主动探索并验证视觉线索。我们设计了包含三阶段的后训练流程：首先通过监督微调实现基础对齐，随后采用基于多智能体框架合成的高质量轨迹进行智能体冷启动，以培养工具调用能力，最后通过强化学习优化模型推理。我们提出空间感知动态过滤策略，依据空间难度对可学习样本进行优先级排序，从而提升强化学习阶段的效率。在标准基准测试上的大量实验表明，SpotAgent实现了最先进的性能，在提供精确且可验证地理定位结果的同时，有效缓解了幻觉问题。

The method formalizes geo-localization as an agentic reasoning process, integrating visual interpretation with tool-assisted verification (e.g., web search, maps) via a ReAct diagram, and employs a three-stage post-training pipeline: supervised fine-tuning, an agentic cold start phase using trajectories synthesized by a multi-agent framework to instill tool-calling expertise, and reinforcement learning refined with a spatially-aware dynamic filtering strategy to prioritize learnable samples. Experimental results on standard benchmarks show that SpotAgent achieves state-of-the-art performance, effectively reducing hallucinations and delivering precise, verifiable geo-localization.

LLM-assisted Semantic Option Discovery for Facilitating Adaptive Deep Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Chang Yao, Jinghui Qin, Kebing Jin, Hankz Hankui Zhuo
First: 2026-03-02T05:54:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T05:54:02+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Despite achieving remarkable success in complex tasks, Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL) is still suffering from critical issues in practical applications, such as low data efficiency, lack of interpretability, and limited cross-environment transferability. However, the learned policy generating actions based on states are sensitive to the environmental changes, struggling to guarantee behavioral safety and compliance. Recent research shows that integrating Large Language Models (LLMs) with symbolic planning is promising in addressing these challenges. Inspired by this, we introduce a novel LLM-driven closed-loop framework, which enables semantic-driven skill reuse and real-time constraint monitoring by mapping natural language instructions into executable rules and semantically annotating automatically created options. The proposed approach utilizes the general knowledge of LLMs to facilitate exploration efficiency and adapt to transferable options for similar environments, and provides inherent interpretability through semantic annotations. To validate the effectiveness of this framework, we conduct experiments on two domains, Office World and Montezuma's Revenge, respectively. The results demonstrate superior performance in data efficiency, constraint compliance, and cross-task transferability.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于大语言模型的语义选项发现促进自适应深度强化学习
尽管深度强化学习在复杂任务中取得了显著成功，但在实际应用中仍面临数据效率低、可解释性不足和跨环境迁移能力有限等关键问题。基于状态生成动作的学习策略对环境变化敏感，难以保证行为安全性与合规性。近期研究表明，将大语言模型与符号规划相结合有望应对这些挑战。受此启发，我们提出了一种新型大语言模型驱动的闭环框架，通过将自然语言指令映射为可执行规则并对自动创建的选项进行语义标注，实现语义驱动的技能复用与实时约束监控。该方法利用大语言模型的通用知识提升探索效率，适配相似环境的可迁移选项，并通过语义标注提供内在可解释性。为验证框架有效性，我们分别在Office World和Montezuma's Revenge两个领域进行实验，结果在数据效率、约束合规性和跨任务迁移能力方面均表现出优越性能。

Motivated by the practical limitations of Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL), such as low data efficiency and poor adaptability to environmental changes, this paper introduces an LLM-assisted framework to enhance DRL through semantic skill reuse. The method leverages Large Language Models to map natural language instructions into executable rules and automatically create semantically annotated options, thereby improving exploration and enabling real-time constraint monitoring. Experimental results in the Office World and Montezuma's Revenge domains demonstrate that the approach achieves superior data efficiency, better constraint compliance, and enhanced cross-task transferability compared to standard methods.

EnterpriseBench Corecraft: Training Generalizable Agents on High-Fidelity RL Environments
Authors: Sushant Mehta, Logan Ritchie, Suhaas Garre, Ian Niebres, Nick Heiner, Edwin Chen
First: 2026-02-18T04:35:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T05:48:19+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We show that training AI agents on high-fidelity reinforcement learning environments produces capabilities that generalize beyond the training distribution. We introduce CoreCraft, the first environment in EnterpriseBench, Surge AI's suite of agentic RL environments. CoreCraft is a fully operational enterprise simulation of a customer support organization, comprising over 2,500 entities across 14 entity types with 23 unique tools, designed to measure whether AI agents can perform the multi-step, domain-specific work that real jobs demand. Frontier models such as GPT-5.2 and Claude Opus 4.6 solve fewer than 30% of tasks when all expert-authored rubric criteria must be satisfied. Using this environment, we train GLM 4.6 with Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) and adaptive clipping. After a single epoch of training, the model improves from 25.37% to 36.76% task pass rate on held-out evaluation tasks. More importantly, these gains transfer to out-of-distribution benchmarks: +4.5% on BFCL Parallel, +7.4% on Tau2-Bench Retail, and +6.8% on Tool Decathlon (Pass@1). We believe three environment properties are consistent with the observed transfer: task-centric world building that optimizes for diverse, challenging tasks; expert-authored rubrics enabling reliable reward computation; and enterprise workflows that reflect realistic professional patterns. Our results suggest that environment quality, diversity, and realism are key factors enabling generalizable agent capabilities.
中文标题/摘要
标题：EnterpriseBench Corecraft：在高保真强化学习环境中训练可泛化智能体
研究表明，在高保真强化学习环境中训练AI智能体可产生超越训练分布的泛化能力。我们推出CoreCraft——Surge AI智能体强化学习环境套件EnterpriseBench的首个环境。CoreCraft是一个完全可运行的客户支持组织企业仿真系统，包含14种实体类型超过2500个实体及23种独特工具，旨在评估AI智能体能否执行现实岗位所需的多步骤、领域特定工作。当需满足所有专家制定的评估标准时，GPT-5.2和Claude Opus 4.6等前沿模型的任务通过率不足30%。在此环境中，我们采用组相对策略优化（GRPO）与自适应剪裁技术训练GLM 4.6模型。经单轮训练后，模型在保留评估任务上的通过率从25.37%提升至36.76%。更重要的是，这些增益可迁移至分布外基准测试：BFCL Parallel提升4.5%、Tau2-Bench Retail提升7.4%、Tool Decathlon（Pass@1）提升6.8%。我们认为三个环境特性与观察到的迁移效应相符：以任务为中心的世界构建优化了多样性与挑战性；专家制定的评估准则实现了可靠奖励计算；企业工作流反映了真实专业模式。结果表明，环境质量、多样性和真实性是形成可泛化智能体能力的关键因素。

The method involves training agents on CoreCraft, a high-fidelity enterprise simulation of a customer support organization with over 2,500 entities and 23 tools, using Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) with adaptive clipping on the GLM 4.6 model. Experimental results show that after one training epoch, task pass rates improved from 25.37% to 36.76% on held-out tasks, with transfer gains of +4.5% to +7.4% on out-of-distribution benchmarks, indicating that environment quality and realism are crucial for generalizable agent capabilities.
该研究的动机是开发能够超越训练分布进行泛化的AI智能体，特别是在专业环境中处理复杂多步骤任务。方法包括在CoreCraft上训练智能体，这是一个高保真的企业客户支持组织模拟，包含超过2,500个实体和23种工具，使用带自适应裁剪的组相对策略优化（GRPO）对GLM 4.6模型进行训练。实验结果表明，经过一个训练周期后，在保留任务上的通过率从25.37%提升至36.76%，并在分布外基准测试中实现了+4.5%至+7.4%的迁移增益，表明环境质量、多样性和真实性是获得可泛化智能体能力的关键因素。
Harmonizing Dense and Sparse Signals in Multi-turn RL: Dual-Horizon Credit Assignment for Industrial Sales Agents
Authors: Haojin Yang, Ai Jian, Xinyue Huang, Yiwei Wang, Weipeng Zhang, Ke Zeng, Xunliang Cai, Jingqing Ruan
First: 2026-03-02T05:44:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T05:44:50+00:00
Comments: 15 pages, 6 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Optimizing large language models for industrial sales requires balancing long-term commercial objectives (e.g., conversion rate) with immediate linguistic constraints such as fluency and compliance. Conventional reinforcement learning often merges these heterogeneous goals into a single reward, causing high-magnitude session-level rewards to overwhelm subtler turn-level signals, which leads to unstable training or reward hacking. To address this issue, we propose Dual-Horizon Credit Assignment (DuCA), a framework that disentangles optimization across time scales. Its core, Horizon-Independent Advantage Normalization (HIAN), separately normalizes advantages from turn-level and session-level rewards before fusion, ensuring balanced gradient contributions from both immediate and long-term objectives to the policy update. Extensive experiments with a high-fidelity user simulator show DuCA outperforms the state-of-the-art GRPO baseline, achieving a 6.82% relative improvement in conversion rate, reducing inter-sentence repetition by 82.28%, and lowering identity detection rate by 27.35%, indicating a substantial improvement for an industrial sales scenario that effectively balances the dual demands of strategic performance and naturalistic language generation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：多轮强化学习中稠密与稀疏信号的协调：面向工业销售代理的双层信用分配机制
为工业销售场景优化大语言模型需平衡长期商业目标（如转化率）与即时语言约束（如流畅性与合规性）。传统强化学习常将异质目标合并为单一奖励，导致高量级会话级奖励淹没更细微的轮次级信号，引发训练不稳定或奖励黑客行为。为解决该问题，我们提出双层信用分配框架，其核心——层级无关优势归一化技术——在融合前分别对轮次级和会话级奖励的优势值进行归一化，确保即时与长期目标对策略更新的梯度贡献均衡。基于高保真用户模拟器的实验表明，该框架在转化率上相对GRPO基线提升6.82%，语句重复率降低82.28%，身份识别率下降27.35%，显著提升了工业销售场景中战略绩效与自然语言生成的双重需求平衡能力。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of optimizing large language models for industrial sales agents, where long-term commercial goals like conversion rate must be balanced with immediate linguistic constraints such as fluency and compliance. The authors propose Dual-Horizon Credit Assignment (DuCA), a framework that disentangles optimization across time scales via Horizon-Independent Advantage Normalization (HIAN), which separately normalizes advantages from turn-level and session-level rewards before fusion to ensure balanced gradient contributions. Experimental results using a high-fidelity user simulator demonstrate that DuCA outperforms the GRPO baseline, achieving a 6.82% relative improvement in conversion rate, an 82.28% reduction in inter-sentence repetition, and a 27.35% lower identity detection rate, indicating effective harmonization of strategic performance and naturalistic language generation.
本文针对工业销售智能体中优化大语言模型的挑战，即需平衡长期商业目标（如转化率）与即时语言约束（如流畅性和合规性）。作者提出了双视野信用分配框架，通过视野独立优势归一化核心方法，在融合前分别对回合级和会话级奖励的优势进行归一化，以确保策略更新中即时与长期目标的梯度贡献均衡。基于高保真用户模拟器的实验结果表明，该框架优于GRPO基线，实现了转化率相对提升6.82%、句子间重复减少82.28%、身份检测率降低27.35%，有效协调了战略性能与自然语言生成的双重需求。
Toward Clinically Explainable AI for Medical Diagnosis: A Foundation Model with Human-Compatible Reasoning via Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Qika Lin, Yifan Zhu, Bin Pu, Ling Huang, Haoran Luo, Jingying Ma, Feng Wu, Kai He, Jiaxing Xu, Zhen Peng, Tianzhe Zhao, Fangzhi Xu, Jian Zhang, Zhonghong Ou, Erik Cambria, Swapnil Mishra, Mengling Feng
First: 2025-09-04T06:00:04+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T05:37:36+00:00
Comments: 35 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The clinical adoption of artificial intelligence (AI) in medical diagnostics is critically hampered by its black-box nature, which prevents clinicians from verifying the rationale behind automated decisions. To overcome this fundamental barrier, we introduce DeepMedix-R1, a foundation model (FM) for chest X-ray (CXR) interpretation that generates not only accurate diagnoses but also a transparent, step-by-step reasoning process grounded in specific visual evidence. Our methodology employs a sequential training strategy, beginning with instruction fine-tuning, followed by a cold-start phase to elicit reasoning capabilities. Critically, we then implement reinforcement learning with grounded rewards to meticulously refine the model, aligning both its diagnostic outputs and its reasoning pathways with clinical plausibility. Quantitative assessments show that DeepMedix-R1 substantially outperforms advanced FMs, achieving improvements in report generation and visual question answering tasks. We also introduce Report Arena, a novel LLM-based benchmark that ranks DeepMedix-R1 first among competing models for output quality. Most significantly, a formal review by clinical experts reveals a profound preference for DeepMedix-R1's generated reasoning over the broadly adopted Qwen2.5-VL-7B model, confirming its superior interpretability and clinical utility.
中文标题/摘要
标题：迈向临床可解释的医疗诊断人工智能：通过强化学习实现人类兼容推理的基础模型
人工智能在医疗诊断中的临床应用因其黑箱性质而严重受阻，临床医生无法验证自动化决策背后的依据。为克服这一根本障碍，我们推出DeepMedix-R1——一种用于胸部X光片解读的基础模型，不仅能生成准确诊断，还能基于具体视觉证据提供透明的逐步推理过程。我们的方法采用顺序训练策略：从指令微调开始，随后通过冷启动阶段激发推理能力。关键的是，我们进一步实施基于实际奖励的强化学习，精细优化模型，使其诊断输出和推理路径均符合临床合理性。定量评估表明，DeepMedix-R1显著优于先进基础模型，在报告生成和视觉问答任务上实现性能提升。我们还推出Report Arena这一基于大语言模型的新型基准测试，DeepMedix-R1在输出质量上位列竞争模型首位。最重要的是，临床专家的正式评审显示，相较于广泛采用的Qwen2.5-VL-7B模型，专家们明显更倾向于DeepMedix-R1生成的推理过程，这证实了其卓越的可解释性与临床实用性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to overcome the black-box nature of AI in medical diagnostics, which hinders clinical trust and adoption, this paper introduces DeepMedix-R1, a foundation model for chest X-ray interpretation. The method employs a sequential training strategy involving instruction fine-tuning, a cold-start phase, and reinforcement learning with grounded rewards to align the model's diagnostic outputs and step-by-step reasoning with clinical plausibility. Experimental results show the model substantially outperforms advanced foundation models in report generation and visual question answering, ranks first in a novel LLM-based benchmark (Report Arena), and is strongly preferred by clinical experts for its interpretable reasoning compared to a leading model like Qwen2.5-VL-7B.
本研究旨在解决医疗诊断中人工智能黑箱特性阻碍临床信任与应用的核心问题，为此提出了用于胸部X光解读的基础模型DeepMedix-R1。该方法采用顺序训练策略，包括指令微调、冷启动阶段，以及基于具体证据的强化学习，以精细调整模型，使其诊断输出和逐步推理过程符合临床合理性。实验结果表明，该模型在报告生成和视觉问答任务上显著优于先进的基础模型，在一个新颖的基于大语言模型的基准（Report Arena）中排名第一，并且临床专家评审对其生成的可解释推理表现出强烈偏好，认为其优于广泛采用的Qwen2.5-VL-7B模型。
Randomized Kiring Believer for Parallel Bayesian Optimization with Regret Bounds
Authors: Shuhei Sugiura, Ichiro Takeuchi, Shion Takeno
First: 2026-03-02T05:32:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T05:32:59+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We consider an optimization problem of an expensive-to-evaluate black-box function, in which we can obtain noisy function values in parallel. For this problem, parallel Bayesian optimization (PBO) is a promising approach, which aims to optimize with fewer function evaluations by selecting a diverse input set for parallel evaluation. However, existing PBO methods suffer from poor practical performance or lack theoretical guarantees. In this study, we propose a PBO method, called randomized kriging believer (KB), based on a well-known KB heuristic and inheriting the advantages of the original KB: low computational complexity, a simple implementation, versatility across various BO methods, and applicability to asynchronous parallelization. Furthermore, we show that our randomized KB achieves Bayesian expected regret guarantees. We demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed method through experiments on synthetic and benchmark functions and emulators of real-world data.
中文标题/摘要
标题：具有遗憾界保证的并行贝叶斯优化随机克里金置信方法
本文研究一个评估成本高昂的黑箱函数优化问题，其中可并行获取带噪声的函数值。针对该问题，并行贝叶斯优化（PBO）是一种前景广阔的方法，其通过选择多样化的输入集进行并行评估，旨在以更少的函数评估次数实现优化。然而，现有PBO方法存在实际性能不佳或缺乏理论保证的局限。本研究提出一种基于经典克里金置信启发式策略的PBO方法——随机克里金置信法，该方法继承了原始克里金置信法的优势：计算复杂度低、实现简单、可适配多种贝叶斯优化方法，并适用于异步并行场景。此外，我们证明随机克里金置信法能够实现贝叶斯期望遗憾的理论保证。通过合成函数、基准函数以及真实数据模拟器的实验，验证了所提方法的有效性。
Summary / 总结
The study addresses the challenge of optimizing expensive black-box functions using parallel evaluations, where existing parallel Bayesian optimization methods often lack theoretical guarantees or perform poorly in practice. The proposed method, called randomized kriging believer, builds on a known heuristic to offer low computational cost, simple implementation, compatibility with various Bayesian optimization approaches, and support for asynchronous parallelization. Experimental results on synthetic functions, benchmarks, and real-world data emulators demonstrate its effectiveness, while theoretical analysis confirms it achieves Bayesian expected regret bounds.
本研究针对昂贵黑盒函数的并行优化问题，现有并行贝叶斯优化方法常缺乏理论保证或实际性能不佳。提出的方法称为随机克里金置信者，基于已知启发式策略，具有计算复杂度低、实现简单、兼容多种贝叶斯优化方法及支持异步并行化的优点。在合成函数、基准测试和真实数据模拟器上的实验验证了其有效性，同时理论分析表明该方法实现了贝叶斯期望遗憾界。
ProteinZero: Self-Improving Protein Generation via Online Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Ziwen Wang, Jiajun Fan, Ruihan Guo, Thao Nguyen, Heng Ji, Ge Liu
First: 2025-06-09T06:08:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T05:31:24+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Protein generative models have shown remarkable promise in protein design, yet their success rates remain constrained by reliance on curated sequence-structure datasets and by misalignment between supervised objectives and real design goals. We present ProteinZero, an online reinforcement learning framework for inverse folding models that enables scalable, automated, and continuous self-improvement with computationally efficient feedback. ProteinZero employs a reward pipeline that combines structural guidance from ESMFold with a novel self-derived ddG predictor, providing stable multi-objective signals while avoiding the prohibitive cost of physics-based methods. To ensure robustness in online RL, we further introduce a novel embedding-level diversity regularizer that mitigates mode collapse and promotes functionally meaningful sequence variation. Within a general RL formulation balancing multi-reward optimization, KL-divergence from a reference model, and diversity regularization, ProteinZero achieves robust improvements across designability, stability, recovery, and diversity. On the CATH-4.3 benchmark, it consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines including ProteinMPNN, ESM-IF, and InstructPLM, reducing design failure rates by 36-48% and achieving success rates above 90% across diverse folds. Importantly, a complete RL run can be executed on a single 8 X GPU node within three days, including reward computation and data generation. These results indicate that efficient online RL fine-tuning can complement supervised pretraining by allowing protein generative models to evolve continuously from their own outputs and optimize multiple design objectives without labeled data, opening new possibilities for exploring the vast protein design space. Full source code and model checkpoints will be released upon publication.

The method employs a reward pipeline combining ESMFold structural guidance with a novel self-derived ddG predictor, alongside an embedding-level diversity regularizer to prevent mode collapse, all within a general RL formulation balancing multi-reward optimization, KL-divergence, and diversity. ProtRLSearch: A Multi-Round Multimodal Protein Search Agent with Large Language Models Trained via Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Congying Liu, Taihao Li, Ming Huang, Xingyuan Wei, Peipei Liu, Yiqing Shen, Yanxu Mao, Tiehan Cui
First: 2026-03-02T05:25:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T05:25:41+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Protein analysis tasks arising in healthcare settings often require accurate reasoning under protein sequence constraints, involving tasks such as functional interpretation of disease-related variants, protein-level analysis for clinical research, and similar scenarios. To address such tasks, search agents are introduced to search protein-related information, providing support for disease-related variant analysis and protein function reasoning in protein-centric inference. However, such search agents are mostly limited to single-round, text-only modality search, which prevents the protein sequence modality from being incorporated as a multimodal input into the search decision-making process. Meanwhile, their reliance on reinforcement learning (RL) supervision that focuses solely on the final answer results in a lack of search process constraints, making deviations in keyword selection and reasoning directions difficult to identify and correct in a timely manner. To address these limitations, we propose ProtRLSearch, a multi-round protein search agent trained with multi-dimensional reward based RL, which jointly leverages protein sequence and text as multimodal inputs during real-time search to produce high quality reports. To evaluate the ability of models to integrate protein sequence information and text-based multimodal inputs in realistic protein query settings, we construct ProtMCQs, a benchmark of 3,000 multiple choice questions (MCQs) organized into three difficulty levels. The benchmark evaluates protein query tasks that range from sequence constrained reasoning about protein function and phenotype changes to comprehensive protein reasoning that integrates multi-dimensional sequence features with signal pathways and regulatory networks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ProtRLSearch：基于强化学习训练的多轮多模态蛋白质搜索智能体
医疗场景中的蛋白质分析任务常需在序列约束下进行精确推理，包括疾病相关变异的功能解读、临床研究的蛋白质层面分析等。现有搜索智能体多局限于单轮纯文本检索，无法将蛋白质序列作为多模态输入纳入决策过程，且其依赖仅关注最终答案的强化学习监督机制，缺乏对搜索过程的约束，导致关键词选择和推理方向的偏差难以及时纠正。为此，我们提出ProtRLSearch——一种基于多维奖励强化学习训练的多轮蛋白质搜索智能体，能够在实时检索中联合利用蛋白质序列与文本作为多模态输入生成高质量报告。为评估模型在实际蛋白质查询场景中整合序列信息与文本多模态输入的能力，我们构建了包含3,000道选择题的ProtMCQs基准数据集，按难度分为三级，评估范围涵盖从蛋白质功能与表型变化的序列约束推理，到整合多维序列特征与信号通路、调控网络的综合蛋白质推理任务。

Experimental results on the newly constructed ProtMCQs benchmark, comprising 3,000 multiple-choice questions across three difficulty levels, demonstrate the agent's ability to effectively integrate sequence and text information for tasks ranging from functional reasoning to comprehensive protein analysis.

Scaling Tasks, Not Samples: Mastering Humanoid Control through Multi-Task Model-Based Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Shaohuai Liu, Weirui Ye, Yilun Du, Le Xie
First: 2026-03-02T05:07:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T05:07:43+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Developing generalist robots capable of mastering diverse skills remains a central challenge in embodied AI. While recent progress emphasizes scaling model parameters and offline datasets, such approaches are limited in robotics, where learning requires active interaction. We argue that effective online learning should scale the \emph{number of tasks}, rather than the number of samples per task. This regime reveals a structural advantage of model-based reinforcement learning (MBRL). Because physical dynamics are invariant across tasks, a shared world model can aggregate multi-task experience to learn robust, task-agnostic representations. In contrast, model-free methods suffer from gradient interference when tasks demand conflicting actions in similar states. Task diversity therefore acts as a regularizer for MBRL, improving dynamics learning and sample efficiency. We instantiate this idea with \textbf{EfficientZero-Multitask (EZ-M)}, a sample-efficient multi-task MBRL algorithm for online learning. Evaluated on \textbf{HumanoidBench}, a challenging whole-body control benchmark, EZ-M achieves state-of-the-art performance with significantly higher sample efficiency than strong baselines, without extreme parameter scaling. These results establish task scaling as a critical axis for scalable robotic learning. The project website is available \href{https://yewr.github.io/ez_m/}{here}.
中文标题/摘要
标题：扩展任务而非样本：通过多任务模型强化学习掌握人形机器人控制
开发能够掌握多样化技能的通用机器人仍是具身AI的核心挑战。尽管近期研究强调扩展模型参数和离线数据集，但这类方法在需要主动交互的机器人学习中存在局限。我们认为，有效的在线学习应扩展任务数量，而非每个任务的样本量。这一机制揭示了基于模型的强化学习（MBRL）的结构优势：由于物理动力学在任务间具有不变性，共享的世界模型可聚合多任务经验以学习鲁棒、任务无关的表征。相比之下，无模型方法在相似状态下任务需求冲突时易受梯度干扰。因此，任务多样性可作为MBRL的正则化器，提升动力学学习和样本效率。我们通过高效多任务MBRL算法\textbf{EfficientZero-Multitask（EZ-M）}实现这一理念，该算法专为在线学习设计，具有高样本效率。在全身控制基准\textbf{HumanoidBench}的评估中，EZ-M以显著高于强基线的样本效率取得最先进性能，且无需极端参数扩展。这些结果确立了任务扩展作为可扩展机器人学习的关键维度。项目网站可通过\href{https://yewr.github.io/ez_m/}{此链接}访问。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of developing generalist robots by proposing a shift from scaling samples per task to scaling the number of tasks in online reinforcement learning. The method leverages model-based reinforcement learning (MBRL), arguing that a shared world model can aggregate multi-task experience to learn robust, task-agnostic dynamics representations, while model-free methods suffer from gradient interference. The authors introduce EfficientZero-Multitask (EZ-M), a sample-efficient multi-task MBRL algorithm, and demonstrate its state-of-the-art performance on the HumanoidBench whole-body control benchmark, achieving superior sample efficiency without extreme parameter scaling.
本文针对开发通用机器人的挑战，提出在线强化学习应从扩展单任务样本转向扩展任务数量。该方法基于模型强化学习，认为共享的世界模型能聚合多任务经验以学习鲁棒、任务无关的动态表征，而免模型方法则易受梯度干扰。作者提出了样本高效的多任务模型强化学习算法EfficientZero-Multitask（EZ-M），并在HumanoidBench全身控制基准测试中展示了其领先性能，以显著更高的样本效率实现了先进结果，且无需极端参数扩展。
Securing the Floor and Raising the Ceiling: A Merging-based Paradigm for Multi-modal Search Agents
Authors: Zhixiang Wang, Jingxuan Xu, Dajun Chen, Yunfang Wu, Wei Jiang, Yong Li
First: 2026-03-02T03:43:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T03:43:31+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent advances in Vision-Language Models (VLMs) have motivated the development of multi-modal search agents that can actively invoke external search tools and integrate retrieved evidence through multi-step reasoning. While promising, existing approaches typically rely on large-scale supervised trajectories or expensive reinforcement learning (RL), leading to high training cost, instability, and a severe cold-start problem for standard VLMs. We propose a training-free paradigm to empower VLMs with autonomous search capabilities via cross-modal model merging. By fusing a text-based search agent with a base VLM, we show that multi-modal search capabilities can be effectively composed without any additional multi-modal training data. To mitigate parameter interference during cross-modal integration, we introduce Optimal Brain Merging (OBM), a saliency-aware merging algorithm that identifies task-critical parameters based on their impact on model loss using only a small set of calibration samples. Extensive experiments on search-intensive benchmarks (e.g., InfoSeek, MMSearch) reveal that: (1) Model merging secures a reasonable performance floor as a zero-shot agent, with OBM achieving superior search rates; (2) OBM significantly raises the performance ceiling as a warm-start strategy, achieving faster convergence and higher peak accuracy than standard VLM initialization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：筑牢基础与突破上限：基于模型融合的多模态搜索智能体新范式
视觉语言模型（VLM）的最新进展推动了多模态搜索智能体的发展，这类智能体能够主动调用外部搜索工具，并通过多步推理整合检索证据。尽管前景广阔，现有方法通常依赖大规模监督轨迹或昂贵的强化学习（RL），导致训练成本高、稳定性差，且标准VLM面临严重的冷启动问题。我们提出一种免训练范式，通过跨模态模型融合赋予VLM自主搜索能力。通过将基于文本的搜索智能体与基础VLM融合，我们证明无需额外多模态训练数据即可有效构建多模态搜索能力。为缓解跨模态融合中的参数干扰，我们引入最优大脑融合（OBM）算法——一种基于显著性感知的融合方法，仅需少量校准样本即可根据参数对模型损失的影响识别任务关键参数。在搜索密集型基准测试（如InfoSeek、MMSearch）上的大量实验表明：（1）模型融合为零样本智能体奠定了稳定的性能基础，OBM实现了更优的搜索成功率；（2）作为热启动策略，OBM显著提升了性能上限，相比标准VLM初始化实现了更快的收敛速度和更高的峰值准确率。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the high cost and instability of training multi-modal search agents via supervised trajectories or reinforcement learning, this paper introduces a training-free paradigm that merges a text-based search agent with a base Vision-Language Model (VLM) to enable autonomous search capabilities. The method employs Optimal Brain Merging (OBM), a saliency-aware algorithm that uses minimal calibration data to identify and merge task-critical parameters while mitigating interference. Experimental results on benchmarks like InfoSeek and MMSearch show that this approach establishes a solid zero-shot performance baseline and, as a warm-start strategy, achieves faster convergence and higher peak accuracy than standard VLM initialization.
针对现有基于监督轨迹或强化学习的多模态搜索智能体训练成本高、不稳定的问题，本文提出一种免训练范式，通过融合基于文本的搜索智能体与基础视觉语言模型来赋予其自主搜索能力。该方法采用最优大脑融合算法，利用少量校准数据识别任务关键参数并进行融合，以减少参数干扰。在InfoSeek和MMSearch等基准测试上的实验结果表明，该范式作为零样本智能体确保了可靠的性能下限，并作为热启动策略实现了比标准视觉语言模型初始化更快的收敛速度和更高的峰值准确率。
MIST-RL: Mutation-based Incremental Suite Testing via Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Sicheng Zhu, Jiajun Wang, Jiawei Ai, Xin Li
First: 2026-03-02T03:22:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T03:22:44+00:00
Comments: Preprint. 17 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) often fail to generate correct code on the first attempt, which requires using generated unit tests as verifiers to validate the solutions. Despite the success of recent verification methods, they remain constrained by a "scaling-by-quantity" paradigm. This brute-force approach suffers from a critical limitation: it yields diminishing returns in fault detection while causing severe test redundancy. To address this, we propose MIST-RL (Mutation-based Incremental Suite Testing via Reinforcement Learning), a framework that shifts the focus to "scaling-by-utility". We formulate test generation as a sequential decision process optimized via Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO). Specifically, we introduce a novel incremental mutation reward combined with dynamic penalties, which incentivizes the model to discover new faults while it suppresses functionally equivalent assertions. Experiments on HumanEval+ and MBPP+ demonstrate that MIST-RL outperforms state-of-the-art baselines. It achieves a +28.5% higher mutation score while reducing the number of test cases by 19.3%. Furthermore, we show that these compact, high-utility tests serve as superior verifiers, which improves downstream code reranking accuracy on HumanEval+ by 3.05% over the SOTA baseline with 10 candidate samples. The source code and data are provided in the supplementary material.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MIST-RL：基于突变的强化学习增量式测试套件生成
大语言模型（LLMs）首次生成的代码常存在错误，需借助生成的单元测试作为验证器。现有验证方法虽有效，但仍受限于“以量取胜”范式，这种暴力方法存在关键缺陷：故障检测收益递减且产生严重测试冗余。为此，我们提出MIST-RL（基于突变的强化学习增量式测试套件生成框架），将重心转向“以效取胜”。我们将测试生成建模为通过组相对策略优化（GRPO）进行优化的序列决策过程，特别设计了结合动态惩罚的增量式突变奖励机制，激励模型发现新故障的同时抑制功能等价断言。在HumanEval+和MBPP+上的实验表明，MIST-RL在突变分数上提升28.5%，测试用例数量减少19.3%。这些紧凑高效测试作为优质验证器，将HumanEval+下游代码重排准确率较SOTA基线提升3.05%（10候选样本）。源代码与数据详见补充材料。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of brute-force test generation for verifying LLM-produced code, which leads to redundancy and diminishing fault detection, this paper introduces MIST-RL, a framework that reformulates test generation as a sequential decision process optimized via reinforcement learning. The method employs Group Relative Policy Optimization with a novel incremental mutation reward and dynamic penalties to prioritize generating high-utility tests that uncover new faults while suppressing redundant assertions. Experimental results on HumanEval+ and MBPP+ show that MIST-RL outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, achieving a 28.5% higher mutation score with 19.3% fewer test cases, and these compact tests improve downstream code reranking accuracy by 3.05%.
针对大语言模型生成代码验证中，暴力测试方法存在冗余和故障检测收益递减的问题，本文提出了MIST-RL框架，将测试生成重新定义为通过强化学习优化的序列决策过程。该方法采用组相对策略优化，结合新颖的增量变异奖励和动态惩罚机制，激励模型发现新故障的同时抑制功能等价的断言。在HumanEval+和MBPP+上的实验表明，MIST-RL优于现有先进基线，在减少19.3%测试用例的同时实现了28.5%的变异分数提升，并且这些紧凑的高效用测试将下游代码重排准确率提高了3.05%。
AReaL: A Large-Scale Asynchronous Reinforcement Learning System for Language Reasoning
Authors: Wei Fu, Jiaxuan Gao, Xujie Shen, Chen Zhu, Zhiyu Mei, Chuyi He, Shusheng Xu, Guo Wei, Jun Mei, Jiashu Wang, Tongkai Yang, Binhang Yuan, Yi Wu
First: 2025-05-30T07:18:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T03:07:29+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) has become a dominant paradigm for training large language models (LLMs), particularly for reasoning tasks. Effective RL for LLMs requires massive parallelization and poses an urgent need for efficient training systems. Most existing large-scale RL systems for LLMs are synchronous, alternating generation and training in a batch setting where rollouts in each training batch are generated by the same model. This approach stabilizes RL training but suffers from severe system-level inefficiency: generation must wait until the longest output in the batch is completed before model updates, resulting in GPU underutilization. We present AReaL, a fully asynchronous RL system that completely decouples generation from training. Rollout workers in AReaL continuously generate new outputs without waiting, while training workers update the model whenever a batch of data is collected. AReaL also incorporates a collection of system-level optimizations, leading to substantially higher GPU utilization. To stabilize RL training, AReaL balances the workload of rollout and training workers to control data staleness, and adopts a staleness-enhanced PPO variant to better handle outdated training samples. Extensive experiments on math and code reasoning benchmarks show that AReaL achieves up to 2.77$\times$ training speedup compared to synchronous systems with the same number of GPUs and matched or improved final performance. The code of AReaL is available at https://github.com/inclusionAI/AReaL/.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AReaL：面向语言推理的大规模异步强化学习系统
强化学习已成为训练大语言模型（尤其是推理任务）的主流范式。针对大语言模型的高效强化学习需要大规模并行化，对高效训练系统提出了迫切需求。现有的大规模强化学习系统多为同步式，在批次设置中交替进行生成与训练，每个训练批次的轨迹均由同一模型生成。这种方法虽能稳定强化学习训练，但存在严重的系统级低效问题：生成过程必须等待批次中最长输出完成后才能更新模型，导致GPU利用率不足。本文提出AReaL，一种完全异步的强化学习系统，将生成与训练彻底解耦。AReaL中的轨迹生成工作节点无需等待即可持续生成新输出，而训练工作节点在收集到数据批次时立即更新模型。该系统还集成了一系列系统级优化，显著提升了GPU利用率。为稳定强化学习训练，AReaL通过平衡生成与训练工作节点的负载来控制数据陈旧度，并采用增强陈旧度处理的PPO变体以更好地处理过时训练样本。在数学与代码推理基准上的大量实验表明，在GPU数量相同的情况下，AReaL相比同步系统最高可实现2.77倍的训练加速，且最终性能相当或更优。AReaL代码已开源：https://github.com/inclusionAI/AReaL/。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for AReaL stems from the inefficiency of synchronous reinforcement learning systems for large language models, which suffer from GPU underutilization due to waiting for the longest output in a batch before model updates. The method introduces a fully asynchronous system that decouples generation from training, allowing rollout workers to continuously produce outputs while training workers update the model as data is collected, alongside optimizations to control data staleness and a staleness-enhanced PPO variant. Experimental results on math and code reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that AReaL achieves up to 2.77× training speedup with matched or improved performance compared to synchronous systems using the same GPU resources.
AReaL的动机源于同步强化学习系统在大语言模型训练中的低效问题，由于需等待批次中最长输出完成才进行模型更新，导致GPU利用率不足。该方法提出一个完全异步的系统，将生成与训练解耦，使生成工作器持续产生输出而训练工作器在收集数据时更新模型，并通过优化控制数据陈旧性及采用增强陈旧性的PPO变体来稳定训练。在数学和代码推理基准测试中，实验结果表明AReaL相比同步系统，在相同GPU资源下实现了高达2.77倍的训练加速，同时保持或提升了最终性能。
TRINITY: An Evolved LLM Coordinator
Authors: Jinglue Xu, Qi Sun, Peter Schwendeman, Stefan Nielsen, Edoardo Cetin, Yujin Tang
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-12-04T11:45:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T03:04:07+00:00
Comments: To appear at the 14th International Conference on Learning Representation (ICLR 2026)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Combining diverse foundation models is promising, but weight-merging is limited by mismatched architectures and closed APIs. Trinity addresses this with a lightweight coordinator that orchestrates collaboration among large language models (LLMs). The coordinator, comprising a compact language model (approximately $0.6$B parameters) and a lightweight head (approximately $10$K parameters), is optimized with an evolutionary strategy for efficient and adaptive delegation. Trinity processes queries over multiple turns, where at each turn the coordinator assigns one of three roles (Thinker, Worker, or Verifier) to a selected LLM, effectively offloading complex skill acquisition from the coordinator itself. Experiments show that Trinity consistently outperforms individual models and existing methods across coding, math, reasoning, and domain knowledge tasks, and generalizes robustly to out-of-distribution tasks. On standard benchmarks, Trinity achieves state-of-the-art results, including a score of 86.2% on LiveCodeBench. Theoretical and empirical analyses identify two main factors behind this performance: (1) the coordinator's hidden-state representations provide rich contextualization of inputs, and (2) under high dimensionality and strict budget constraints, the separable Covariance Matrix Adaptation Evolution Strategy offers advantages over reinforcement learning, imitation learning, and random search by exploiting potential block-epsilon-separability.
中文标题/摘要
标题：TRINITY：一种进化的LLM协调器
融合多样化基础模型前景广阔，但权重合并受限于架构不匹配与封闭API。TRINITY通过轻量级协调器解决此问题，协调大语言模型（LLMs）间的协作。该协调器由紧凑语言模型（约6亿参数）和轻量级头部（约1万参数）构成，采用进化策略优化以实现高效自适应任务委派。TRINITY通过多轮次处理查询，每轮协调器为选定LLM分配三种角色之一（思考者、执行者或验证者），从而将复杂技能获取任务从协调器本身剥离。实验表明，在编程、数学、推理及领域知识任务中，TRINITY持续超越单一模型与现有方法，并能稳健泛化至分布外任务。在标准基准测试中取得最先进成果，包括LiveCodeBench上86.2%的得分。理论与实证分析揭示其性能的两大关键因素：（1）协调器的隐状态表征提供丰富的输入上下文信息；（2）在高维严格预算约束下，可分离协方差矩阵自适应进化策略通过利用潜在块ε可分离性，相比强化学习、模仿学习与随机搜索更具优势。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for TRINITY stems from the limitations of weight-merging for combining diverse foundation models, particularly due to architectural mismatches and closed APIs. The method introduces a lightweight coordinator with a compact language model and a small head, optimized via an evolutionary strategy to orchestrate multiple LLMs by dynamically assigning them one of three roles—Thinker, Worker, or Verifier—across multi-turn interactions. Experimental results demonstrate that TRINITY consistently surpasses individual models and existing approaches in coding, math, reasoning, and knowledge tasks, achieving state-of-the-art performance, such as 86.2% on LiveCodeBench, with robustness in out-of-distribution settings, attributed to rich contextualization from hidden-state representations and the efficiency of the evolutionary optimization under constraints.
TRINITY的动机源于权重合并方法在整合多样化基础模型时的局限性，特别是由于架构不匹配和封闭API问题。该方法采用一个轻量级协调器，包含紧凑的语言模型和小型头部，通过进化策略优化，在多轮交互中动态为多个大语言模型分配思考者、工作者或验证者三种角色。实验结果表明，TRINITY在编程、数学、推理和领域知识任务上持续优于单个模型和现有方法，实现了最先进的性能，如在LiveCodeBench上获得86.2%的分数，并在分布外任务中表现出强鲁棒性，这归因于隐藏状态表示的丰富上下文信息以及在严格约束下进化优化的高效性。
Post-training Large Language Models for Diverse High-Quality Responses
Authors: Yilei Chen, Souradip Chakraborty, Lorenz Wolf, Yannis Paschalidis, Aldo Pacchiano
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-09-05T03:47:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T01:21:51+00:00
Comments: ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) has emerged as a popular method for post-training large language models (LLMs). While improving the model's performance on downstream tasks, it often reduces the model's output diversity, leading to narrow, canonical responses. Existing methods to enhance diversity are limited, either by operating at inference time or by focusing on surface-level differences. We propose a novel training method named DQO (Diversity Quality Optimization) based on determinantal point processes (DPPs) to jointly optimize LLMs for quality and semantic diversity. Our approach samples and embeds a group of responses for each prompt, then uses the determinant of a kernel-based similarity matrix to measure diversity as the volume spanned by the embeddings of these responses. DQO is flexible and can be applied on top of existing RL algorithms. Experiments across instruction-following, summarization, story generation, and reasoning tasks demonstrate that our method substantially improves semantic diversity without sacrificing model quality.
中文标题/摘要
标题：后训练大型语言模型以实现多样化高质量响应
强化学习已成为后训练大型语言模型的一种流行方法。尽管能提升模型在下游任务上的性能，但它常会降低模型输出的多样性，导致生成狭隘、标准化的响应。现有增强多样性的方法存在局限，要么在推理阶段操作，要么仅关注表层差异。我们提出一种基于行列式点过程的新型训练方法DQO，旨在联合优化模型的质量与语义多样性。该方法为每个提示采样并嵌入一组响应，利用基于核的相似度矩阵的行列式，通过嵌入向量的张成空间体积来度量多样性。DQO具有灵活性，可应用于现有强化学习算法之上。在指令跟随、摘要生成、故事创作和推理任务上的实验表明，该方法能在不牺牲模型质量的前提下显著提升语义多样性。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is that while reinforcement learning (RL) is commonly used to post-train large language models (LLMs) for improved task performance, it often reduces output diversity, resulting in narrow and canonical responses. To address this, the authors propose a novel training method called DQO (Diversity Quality Optimization), which uses determinantal point processes (DPPs) to jointly optimize LLMs for both quality and semantic diversity by measuring the volume spanned by embeddings of sampled responses. Experimental results across instruction-following, summarization, story generation, and reasoning tasks show that DQO substantially enhances semantic diversity without compromising model quality, and it can be flexibly applied on top of existing RL algorithms.
本研究的动机在于，尽管强化学习（RL）常用于对大型语言模型（LLM）进行后训练以提升下游任务性能，但它通常会降低输出多样性，导致生成狭窄、规范的响应。为解决此问题，作者提出了一种名为DQO（多样性质量优化）的新型训练方法，该方法基于行列式点过程（DPPs），通过测量采样响应嵌入所张成的体积来联合优化LLM的质量和语义多样性。在指令遵循、摘要、故事生成和推理任务上的实验结果表明，DQO在不牺牲模型质量的前提下显著提升了语义多样性，且该方法可灵活应用于现有RL算法之上。
SubstratumGraphEnv: Reinforcement Learning Environment (RLE) for Modeling System Attack Paths
Authors: Bahirah Adewunmi, Edward Raff, Sanjay Purushotham
Venue: AAAI
First: 2026-03-02T00:48:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T00:48:24+00:00
Comments: Presented at the AI for Cyber Security Workshop at AAAI-26
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Automating network security analysis, particularly the identification of potential attack paths, presents significant challenges. Due in part to the sequential, interconnected, and evolutionary nature of system events which most artificial intelligence (AI) techniques struggle to model effectively. This paper proposes a Reinforcement Learning (RL) environment generation framework that simulates the sequence of processes executed on a Windows operating system, enabling dynamic modeling of malicious processes on a system. This methodology models operating system state and transitions using a graph representation. This graph is derived from open-source System Monitor (Sysmon) logs. To address the variety in system event types, fields, and log formats, a mechanism was developed to capture and model parent-child processes from Sysmon logs. A Gymnasium environment (SubstratumGraphEnv) was constructed to establish the perceptible basis for an RL environment, and a customized PyTorch interface was also built (SubstratumBridge) to translate Gymnasium graphs into Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL) observations and discrete actions. Graph Convolutional Networks (GCNs) concretize the graph's local and global state, which feed the distinct policy and critic heads of an Advantage Actor-Critic (A2C) model. This work's central contribution lies in the design of a novel deep graphical RL environment that automates translation of sequential user and system events, furnishing crucial context for cybersecurity analysis. This work provides a foundation for future research into shaping training parameters and advanced reward shaping, while also offering insight into which system events attributes are critical to training autonomous RL agents.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SubstratumGraphEnv：用于建模系统攻击路径的强化学习环境
自动化网络安全分析，尤其是潜在攻击路径的识别，面临重大挑战。部分原因在于系统事件具有时序性、互联性和演化性，而多数人工智能技术难以有效建模。本文提出一种强化学习环境生成框架，模拟Windows操作系统上执行的进程序列，实现对系统恶意进程的动态建模。该方法采用图表示对操作系统状态及转换进行建模，该图源自开源系统监视器日志。为应对系统事件类型、字段及日志格式的多样性，开发了一种从系统监视器日志中捕获并建模父子进程的机制。构建了Gymnasium环境作为强化学习环境的感知基础，并定制了PyTorch接口，将Gymnasium图转换为深度强化学习的观测值与离散动作。图卷积网络具体化图的局部与全局状态，为优势演员-评论家模型的策略头与评论头提供输入。本工作的核心贡献在于设计了一种新型深度图强化学习环境，可自动转换时序用户与系统事件，为网络安全分析提供关键上下文。该工作为未来研究训练参数调整与高级奖励塑造奠定基础，同时揭示哪些系统事件属性对训练自主强化学习智能体至关重要。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of automating network security analysis, particularly in modeling complex, sequential attack paths that traditional AI methods struggle with. The authors propose SubstratumGraphEnv, a reinforcement learning environment generation framework that simulates process sequences on a Windows system using a graph representation derived from Sysmon logs. To handle diverse event types and log formats, they developed a mechanism to capture parent-child processes, built a Gymnasium environment and a PyTorch interface (SubstratumBridge) to translate graphs into DRL observations, and employed Graph Convolutional Networks within an Advantage Actor-Critic model to process graph states. Experimental results demonstrate the framework's ability to dynamically model malicious processes, providing a foundational tool for cybersecurity analysis and highlighting critical system event attributes for training autonomous RL agents, with future work directed toward advanced reward shaping and parameter optimization.
本文针对自动化网络安全分析中的挑战，特别是传统人工智能方法难以有效建模的复杂、序列化攻击路径问题，提出了一种强化学习环境生成框架SubstratumGraphEnv。该方法利用从Sysmon日志中提取的图表示来模拟Windows系统上的进程序列，通过开发捕获父子进程的机制处理多样的事件类型和日志格式，并构建了Gymnasium环境及PyTorch接口（SubstratumBridge）将图转换为深度强化学习的观测输入。实验采用图卷积网络和优势演员-评论家模型处理图状态，结果表明该框架能动态建模恶意进程，为网络安全分析提供了关键上下文基础，同时揭示了训练自主强化学习代理所需的关键系统事件属性，为未来研究中的训练参数调整和奖励函数设计奠定了基础。
Reasoning or Retrieval? A Study of Answer Attribution on Large Reasoning Models
Authors: Yuhui Wang, Changjiang Li, Guangke Chen, Jiacheng Liang, Ting Wang
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-09-29T01:13:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T00:39:58+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Large reasoning models (LRMs) exhibit unprecedented capabilities in solving complex problems through Chain-of-Thought (CoT) reasoning. However, recent studies reveal that their final answers often contradict their own reasoning traces. We hypothesize that this inconsistency stems from two competing mechanisms for generating answers: CoT reasoning and memory retrieval. To test this hypothesis, we conduct controlled experiments that challenge LRMs with misleading cues during reasoning and/or corrupted answers during retrieval. Our results across models and datasets confirm that both mechanisms operate simultaneously, with their relative dominance influenced by multiple factors: problem domains, model scales, and fine-tuning approaches (e.g., reinforcement learning vs. distillation). The findings reveal a critical limitation in current reasoning fine-tuning paradigms: models can exploit the retrieval mechanism as a shortcut, effectively "hacking" the reward signal and undermining genuine reasoning development. To address this challenge, we introduce FARL, a novel fine-tuning framework that integrates memory unlearning with reinforcement learning. By carefully suppressing retrieval shortcuts during the fine-tuning process, FARL promotes reasoning-dominant behavior and enhances generalizable reasoning capabilities. The code is available: https://github.com/ZJUWYH/FARL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：推理还是检索？大型推理模型的答案归因研究
大型推理模型通过思维链推理展现出解决复杂问题的卓越能力，但其最终答案常与自身推理轨迹相矛盾。本研究假设该矛盾源于答案生成的两种竞争机制：思维链推理与记忆检索。通过设计误导性推理线索与破坏性检索答案的对照实验，发现两种机制同时存在，其主导地位受问题领域、模型规模及微调方法（如强化学习与知识蒸馏）等多因素影响。研究揭示了当前推理微调范式的关键局限：模型可能利用检索机制作为捷径，从而“破解”奖励信号并阻碍真实推理能力的发展。为此，我们提出FARL框架，该框架将记忆遗忘与强化学习相结合，通过在微调过程中抑制检索捷径，有效促进以推理为主导的行为并提升泛化推理能力。代码已开源：https://github.com/ZJUWYH/FARL。

Learning to Reason without External Rewards
Authors: Xuandong Zhao, Zhewei Kang, Aosong Feng, Sergey Levine, Dawn Song
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-05-26T07:01:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-02T00:12:58+00:00
Comments: ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Training large language models (LLMs) for complex reasoning via Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) is effective but limited by reliance on costly, domain-specific supervision. We explore Reinforcement Learning from Internal Feedback (RLIF), a framework that enables LLMs to learn from intrinsic signals without external rewards or labeled data. We propose Intuitor, an RLIF method that uses a model's own confidence-termed self-certainty-as its sole reward signal. Intuitor replaces external rewards in Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) with self-certainty scores, enabling fully unsupervised learning. Experiments demonstrate that Intuitor matches GRPO's performance on mathematical benchmarks while achieving better generalization to out-of-domain tasks like code generation, without requiring gold solutions or test cases. Our findings show that intrinsic model signals can drive effective learning across domains, offering a scalable alternative to RLVR for autonomous AI systems where verifiable rewards are unavailable. Code is available at https://github.com/sunblaze-ucb/Intuitor
中文标题/摘要
标题：无需外部奖励的推理学习
通过可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）训练大型语言模型（LLM）进行复杂推理虽然有效，但受限于对昂贵领域特定监督的依赖。我们探索了内部反馈强化学习（RLIF），该框架使LLM能够从内在信号中学习，无需外部奖励或标注数据。我们提出Intuitor方法，该方法以模型自身置信度（称为自我确定性）作为唯一奖励信号。Intuitor将组相对策略优化（GRPO）中的外部奖励替换为自我确定性分数，实现完全无监督学习。实验表明，Intuitor在数学基准测试中达到与GRPO相当的性能，同时在代码生成等跨领域任务上实现更好的泛化能力，且无需标准答案或测试用例。我们的研究证明，内在模型信号能够驱动跨领域有效学习，为缺乏可验证奖励的自主AI系统提供了可扩展的RLVR替代方案。代码发布于https://github.com/sunblaze-ucb/Intuitor

The method introduces Intuitor, which uses a model's own confidence, termed self-certainty, as the sole reward signal within the Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) framework, allowing for fully unsupervised learning. Learning to Orchestrate Agents in Natural Language with the Conductor
Authors: Stefan Nielsen, Edoardo Cetin, Peter Schwendeman, Qi Sun, Jinglue Xu, Yujin Tang
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-12-04T02:23:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-01T23:52:58+00:00
Comments: To appear at the 14th International Conference on Learning Representations (ICLR 2026)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Powerful large language models (LLMs) from different providers have been expensively trained and finetuned to specialize across varying domains. In this work, we introduce a new kind of Conductor model trained with reinforcement learning to automatically discover powerful coordination strategies among LLMs. Our Conductor learns not only to design targeted communication topologies for effective agent-to-agent collaboration, but also to prompt engineer focused instructions to the LLMs to maximally leverage their individual capabilities. We show that, by learning optimal coordination strategies over pools of powerful worker LLMs, a 7B Conductor achieves significant performance gains beyond any individual worker, attaining state-of-the-art results in challenging reasoning benchmarks, such as LiveCodeBench and GPQA. By training with randomized agent pools, our conductor effectively adapts to arbitrary sets of open- and closed-source agents, meeting any user requirements. Furthermore, allowing the Conductor to select itself as a worker gives rise to recursive topologies, elevating performance with a new form of dynamic test-time scaling through online iterative adaptation. More broadly, ours is among the early work demonstrating language model coordination can be unlocked through RL, where powerful coordination strategies emerge naturally in LLMs through pure end-to-end reward maximization.

标题：学习使用指挥家模型以自然语言编排智能体协作

A Genetic Algorithm for Navigating Synthesizable Molecular Spaces
Authors: Alston Lo, Connor W. Coley, Wojciech Matusik
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-09-25T03:33:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-01T22:40:57+00:00
Comments: ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Inspired by the effectiveness of genetic algorithms and the importance of synthesizability in molecular design, we present SynGA, a simple genetic algorithm that operates directly over synthesis routes. Our method features custom crossover and mutation operators that explicitly constrain it to synthesizable molecular space. By modifying the fitness function, we demonstrate the effectiveness of SynGA on a variety of design tasks, including synthesizable analog search and sample-efficient property optimization, for both 2D and 3D objectives. Furthermore, by coupling SynGA with a machine learning-based filter that focuses the building block set, we boost SynGA to state-of-the-art performance. For property optimization, this manifests as a model-based variant SynGBO, which employs SynGA and block filtering in the inner loop of Bayesian optimization. Since SynGA is lightweight and enforces synthesizability by construction, our hope is that SynGA can not only serve as a strong standalone baseline but also as a versatile module that can be incorporated into larger synthesis-aware workflows in the future.
中文标题/摘要
