PAC Guarantees for Reinforcement Learning: Sample Complexity, Coverage, and Structure
Authors: Joshua Steier
First: 2026-03-01T22:33:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-01T22:33:16+00:00
Comments: 43 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
When data is scarce or mistakes are costly, average-case metrics fall short. What a practitioner needs is a guarantee: with probability at least $1-δ$, the learned policy is $\varepsilon$-close to optimal after $N$ episodes. This is the PAC promise, and between 2018 and 2025 the RL theory community made striking progress on when such promises can be kept. We survey that progress. Our organizing tool is the Coverage-Structure-Objective (CSO) framework, proposed here, which decomposes nearly every PAC sample complexity result into three factors: coverage (how data were obtained), structure (intrinsic MDP or function-class complexity), and objective (what the learner must deliver). CSO is not a theorem but an interpretive template that identifies bottlenecks and makes cross-setting comparison immediate. The technical core covers tight tabular baselines and the uniform-PAC bridge to regret; structural complexity measures (Bellman rank, witness rank, Bellman-Eluder dimension) governing learnability with function approximation; results for linear, kernel/NTK, and low-rank models; reward-free exploration as upfront coverage investment; and pessimistic offline RL where inherited coverage is the binding constraint. We provide practitioner tools: rate lookup tables indexed by CSO coordinates, Bellman residual diagnostics, coverage estimation with deployment gates, and per-episode policy certificates. A final section catalogs open problems, separating near-term targets from frontier questions where coverage, structure, and computation tangle in ways current theory cannot resolve.
中文标题/摘要
标题：强化学习的PAC保证：样本复杂度、覆盖度与结构
当数据稀缺或错误代价高昂时，平均性能指标已显不足。实践者需要的是保证：以至少$1-δ$的概率，学习策略在$N$轮后达到$\varepsilon$接近最优。这正是PAC承诺，而2018至2025年间强化学习理论界在此承诺何时可实现方面取得突破性进展。本文系统梳理该进展。我们提出并采用覆盖-结构-目标（CSO）框架作为组织工具，将几乎所有PAC样本复杂度结果分解为三个要素：覆盖度（数据获取方式）、结构（MDP或函数类的内在复杂性）与目标（学习者需达成的任务）。CSO并非定理，而是识别瓶颈、实现跨场景即时比较的阐释模板。技术核心涵盖：紧致的表格方法基线及连接遗憾的uniform-PAC桥梁；控制函数逼近可学习性的结构复杂度度量（贝尔曼秩、见证秩、贝尔曼-埃尔鲁德维数）；线性、核/NTK及低秩模型的结果；作为前期覆盖投资的免奖励探索；以及以继承覆盖度为关键约束的悲观离线强化学习。我们提供实践工具：按CSO坐标索引的速率查询表、贝尔曼残差诊断、带部署门限的覆盖度估计、逐轮策略证书。末章分类开放问题，区分近期目标与覆盖度、结构及计算深度纠缠而现有理论尚未能解决的前沿课题。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for high-confidence performance guarantees in data-scarce or safety-critical applications, this survey paper synthesizes recent progress (2018-2025) on Probably Approximately Correct (PAC) guarantees for reinforcement learning, introducing the Coverage-Structure-Objective (CSO) framework as an interpretive lens. The method involves decomposing sample complexity results into three factors: coverage (data collection), structure (MDP or function class complexity), and objective (learner's goal), enabling systematic comparison across settings. Key experimental and theoretical results covered include tight tabular baselines, structural complexity measures like Bellman rank for function approximation, analyses for linear and kernel models, reward-free exploration, and pessimistic offline RL, alongside practical tools such as rate lookup tables and policy certificates.
本文旨在为数据稀缺或安全关键型应用提供高置信度的性能保证，综述了2018年至2025年间强化学习中概率近似正确（PAC）保证的研究进展，并提出了覆盖-结构-目标（CSO）框架作为解释工具。方法上，该框架将样本复杂度结果分解为三个因素：覆盖（数据获取方式）、结构（MDP或函数类的内在复杂性）和目标（学习器的输出要求），从而支持跨设置的系统比较。主要实验与理论结果包括：紧致的表格化基线、用于函数近似的贝尔曼秩等结构复杂性度量、线性和核模型的分析、无奖励探索以及悲观离线强化学习，同时还提供了速率查询表和政策证书等实用工具。
Theoretical Perspectives on Data Quality and Synergistic Effects in Pre- and Post-Training Reasoning Models
Authors: Adel Javanmard, Baharan Mirzasoleiman, Vahab Mirrokni
First: 2026-03-01T21:58:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-01T21:58:09+00:00
Comments: 35 pages, 5 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) are pretrained on massive datasets and later instruction-tuned via supervised fine-tuning (SFT) or reinforcement learning (RL). Best practices emphasize large, diverse pretraining data, whereas post-training operates differently: SFT relies on smaller, high-quality datasets, while RL benefits more from scale, with larger amounts of feedback often outweighing label quality. Yet it remains unclear why pretraining and RL require large datasets, why SFT excels on smaller ones, and what defines high-quality SFT data. In this work, we theoretically analyze transformers trained on an in-context weight prediction task for linear regression. Our analysis reveals several key findings: $(i)$ balanced pretraining data can induce latent capabilities later activated during post-training, and $(ii)$ SFT learns best from a small set of examples challenging for the pretrained model, while excessively large SFT datasets may dilute informative pretraining signals. In contrast, RL is most effective on large-scale data that is not overly difficult for the pretrained model. We validate these theoretical insights with experiments on large nonlinear transformer architectures.
中文标题/摘要
标题：预训练与后训练推理模型中数据质量与协同效应的理论视角
大语言模型（LLMs）通过海量数据集进行预训练，随后通过监督微调（SFT）或强化学习（RL）进行指令调优。最佳实践强调预训练数据需规模大且多样化，而后训练则不同：SFT依赖较小规模的高质量数据集，而RL更受益于规模效应，大量反馈通常比标签质量更重要。然而，为何预训练和RL需要大规模数据、为何SFT在小数据集上表现优异，以及高质量SFT数据的定义仍不明确。本研究通过理论分析，在基于上下文权重预测任务的线性回归场景下训练Transformer模型，得出关键发现：$(i)$ 平衡的预训练数据可激发后训练中激活的潜在能力；$(ii)$ SFT最佳学习数据是少量对预训练模型具有挑战性的样本，过大的SFT数据集可能稀释预训练中的有效信号。相比之下，RL在规模大且对预训练模型难度适中的数据上效果最佳。我们通过大型非线性Transformer架构的实验验证了这些理论见解。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates why pretraining and reinforcement learning (RL) for large language models benefit from large datasets, while supervised fine-tuning (SFT) excels with smaller, high-quality data. The authors provide a theoretical analysis using transformers trained on an in-context weight prediction task for linear regression. Their key findings are that balanced pretraining data can create latent capabilities activated later, SFT learns most effectively from a small set of examples that are challenging for the pretrained model, and RL performs best on large-scale data that is not overly difficult. These theoretical insights are validated through experiments on large nonlinear transformer architectures.
本文研究了为何大型语言模型的预训练和强化学习需要大量数据，而监督微调在小规模高质量数据上表现更佳。作者通过对线性回归的上下文权重预测任务中的Transformer进行理论分析，得出关键发现：平衡的预训练数据可诱导后期被激活的潜在能力；监督微调从小部分对预训练模型具有挑战性的样本中学习效果最好；而强化学习则在规模大且难度不过高的数据上最有效。这些理论见解通过在大规模非线性Transformer架构上的实验得到了验证。
Integrating LTL Constraints into PPO for Safe Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Maifang Zhang, Hang Yu, Qian Zuo, Cheng Wang, Vaishak Belle, Fengxiang He
First: 2026-03-01T21:55:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-01T21:55:24+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
This paper proposes Proximal Policy Optimization with Linear Temporal Logic Constraints (PPO-LTL), a framework that integrates safety constraints written in LTL into PPO for safe reinforcement learning. LTL constraints offer rigorous representations of complex safety requirements, such as regulations that broadly exist in robotics, enabling systematic monitoring of safety requirements. Violations against LTL constraints are monitored by limit-deterministic Büchi automata, and then translated by a logic-to-cost mechanism into penalty signals. The signals are further employed for guiding the policy optimization via the Lagrangian scheme. Extensive experiments on the Zones and CARLA environments show that our PPO-LTL can consistently reduce safety violations, while maintaining competitive performance, against the state-of-the-art methods. The code is at https://github.com/EVIEHub/PPO-LTL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：将LTL约束集成至PPO算法实现安全强化学习
本文提出带线性时序逻辑约束的近端策略优化框架（PPO-LTL），通过将LTL形式化安全约束集成至PPO算法实现安全强化学习。LTL约束可严格表征机器人等领域广泛存在的复杂安全规范，支持对安全要求的系统性监测。通过极限确定性布奇自动机监测LTL约束违反情况，并经由逻辑-代价转换机制生成惩罚信号。该信号进一步通过拉格朗日方案指导策略优化。在Zones与CARLA环境中的大量实验表明，相较于前沿方法，PPO-LTL能在保持竞争力的性能表现下持续降低安全违规率。代码开源地址：https://github.com/EVIEHub/PPO-LTL。
Summary / 总结
This paper is motivated by the need to enforce complex safety specifications, such as those in robotics, within reinforcement learning. The method introduces PPO-LTL, which integrates Linear Temporal Logic constraints into Proximal Policy Optimization by monitoring violations via limit-deterministic Büchi automata, converting them into penalty signals through a logic-to-cost mechanism, and optimizing policies using a Lagrangian scheme. Experimental results in Zones and CARLA environments demonstrate that PPO-LTL consistently reduces safety violations while maintaining competitive task performance compared to state-of-the-art methods.
本文的动机是在强化学习中强制执行复杂的安全规范，例如机器人领域中的规则。方法提出了PPO-LTL，通过极限确定性Büchi自动机监控线性时序逻辑约束的违反情况，利用逻辑到成本的机制将其转化为惩罚信号，并采用拉格朗日方案优化策略。在Zones和CARLA环境中的实验结果表明，与现有先进方法相比，PPO-LTL能持续减少安全违规，同时保持有竞争力的任务性能。
Beyond Reward: A Bounded Measure of Agent Environment Coupling
Authors: Wael Hafez, Cameron Reid, Amit Nazeri
First: 2026-03-01T21:38:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-01T21:38:39+00:00
Comments: 8 pages, 2 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Real-world reinforcement learning (RL) agents operate in closed-loop systems where actions shape future observations, making reliable deployment under distribution shifts a persistent challenge. Existing monitoring relies on reward or task metrics, capturing outcomes but missing early coupling failures. We introduce bipredictability (P) as the ratio of shared information in the observation, action, outcome loop to the total available information, a principled, real time measure of interaction effectiveness with provable bounds, comparable across tasks. An auxiliary monitor, the Information Digital Twin (IDT), computes P and its diagnostic components from the interaction stream. We evaluate SAC and PPO agents on MuJoCo HalfCheetah under eight agent, and environment-side perturbations across 168 trials. Under nominal operation, agents exhibit P = 0.33 plus minus 0.02, below the classical bound of 0.5, revealing an informational cost of action selection. The IDT detects 89.3% of perturbations versus 44.0% for reward based monitoring, with 4.4x lower median latency. Bipredictability enables early detection of interaction degradation before performance drops and provides a prerequisite signal for closed loop self regulation in deployed RL systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：超越奖励：一种有界的智能体环境耦合度量方法
现实世界中的强化学习智能体在闭环系统中运行，其行动会塑造未来的观测结果，这使得在分布偏移下实现可靠部署成为持续挑战。现有监测方法依赖奖励或任务指标，虽能捕捉结果但会遗漏早期的耦合故障。我们引入双可预测性作为观测、行动、结果循环中共享信息与总可用信息的比率，这是一种具有可证明界限、可跨任务比较的交互有效性原则性实时度量。辅助监测器信息数字孪生从交互流中计算双可预测性及其诊断分量。我们在MuJoCo HalfCheetah环境中对SAC和PPO智能体进行了168次试验，涵盖八类智能体与环境侧扰动。在标称运行下，智能体表现出0.33±0.02的双可预测性值，低于经典界限0.5，揭示了行动选择的信息成本。信息数字孪生能检测89.3%的扰动，而基于奖励的监测仅能检测44.0%，且中位延迟降低4.4倍。双可预测性可在性能下降前实现交互退化的早期检测，并为部署强化学习系统的闭环自我调节提供先决信号。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of reliably deploying reinforcement learning agents in real-world closed-loop systems where actions influence future observations, this paper introduces bipredictability (P) as a bounded, task-agnostic measure of agent-environment coupling effectiveness, computed via an auxiliary Information Digital Twin (IDT) monitor from the interaction stream. The method provides a principled, real-time metric capturing shared information in the observation-action-outcome loop relative to total available information. Experimental results on MuJoCo HalfCheetah with SAC and PPO agents under various perturbations show that under normal operation, agents exhibit a bipredictability of 0.33 ± 0.02, below the classical 0.5 bound, indicating an informational cost of action selection, and the IDT detects 89.3% of perturbations versus 44.0% for reward-based monitoring with 4.4x lower median latency, enabling early detection of interaction degradation before performance drops.
针对强化学习智能体在现实世界闭环系统中因动作影响未来观测而难以可靠部署的挑战，本文提出了双可预测性（P）作为衡量智能体-环境耦合有效性的有界、任务无关的度量，通过一个辅助的信息数字孪生（IDT）监控器从交互流中计算得出。该方法提供了一个原则性的实时指标，捕捉观察-动作-结果循环中的共享信息相对于总可用信息的比例。在MuJoCo HalfCheetah环境中对SAC和PPO智能体进行多种扰动的实验结果表明，在正常操作下，智能体的双可预测性为0.33 ± 0.02，低于经典界限0.5，揭示了动作选择的信息成本；IDT检测到89.3%的扰动，而基于奖励的监控仅检测到44.0%，且中位延迟降低了4.4倍，从而能够在性能下降前早期检测到交互退化。
DRPO: Efficient Reasoning via Decoupled Reward Policy Optimization
Authors: Gang Li, Yan Chen, Ming Lin, Tianbao Yang
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-10-06T04:18:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-01T21:16:57+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent large reasoning models (LRMs) driven by reinforcement learning algorithms (e.g., GRPO) have achieved remarkable performance on challenging reasoning tasks. However, these models suffer from overthinking, generating unnecessarily long and redundant reasoning even for simple questions, which substantially increases computational cost and response latency. While existing methods incorporate length rewards to GRPO to promote concise reasoning, they incur significant performance degradation. We identify the root cause: when rewards for correct but long rollouts are penalized, GRPO's group-relative advantage function can assign them negative advantages, actively discouraging valid reasoning. To overcome this, we propose Decoupled Reward Policy Optimization (DRPO), a novel framework that decouples the length-based learning signal of correct rollouts from incorrect ones. DRPO ensures that reward signals for correct rollouts are normalized solely within the positive group, shielding them from interference by negative samples. The DRPO's objective is grounded in integrating an optimized positive data distribution, which maximizes length-based rewards under a KL regularization, into a discriminative objective. We derive a closed-form solution for this distribution, enabling efficient computation of the objective and its gradients using only on-policy data and importance weighting. Of independent interest, this formulation is general and can incorporate other preference rewards of positive data beyond length. Experiments on mathematical reasoning tasks demonstrate DRPO's significant superiority over six efficient reasoning baselines. Notably, with a 1.5B model, our method achieves 77\% length reduction with only 1.1\% performance loss on simple questions like GSM8k dataset, while the follow-up baseline sacrifices 4.3\% for 68\% length reduction.
中文标题/摘要
标题：DRPO：基于解耦奖励策略优化的高效推理方法
近期基于强化学习算法（如GRPO）的大型推理模型在复杂推理任务中取得显著性能，但存在过度思考问题：即使面对简单问题也会生成冗长冗余的推理过程，大幅增加计算成本与响应延迟。现有方法通过在GRPO中引入长度奖励以提升推理简洁性，却导致性能显著下降。我们发现根本原因在于：当对正确但冗长的推理轨迹进行惩罚时，GRPO的组间相对优势函数可能赋予其负优势值，从而抑制有效推理。为此，我们提出解耦奖励策略优化框架，其核心创新在于将正确推理轨迹与错误推理轨迹的长度学习信号解耦处理。DRPO确保正确推理轨迹的奖励信号仅在正样本组内归一化，避免受负样本干扰。该框架目标函数基于优化正样本数据分布构建，在KL正则化约束下最大化长度奖励，并融入判别式目标。我们推导出该分布的闭式解，使得仅需使用同策略数据和重要性权重即可高效计算目标函数及其梯度。值得注意的是，该框架具有通用性，可兼容长度之外的其他正样本偏好奖励。数学推理任务实验表明，DRPO在六种高效推理基线方法中具有显著优势。以15亿参数模型为例，在GSM8k等简单问题上，本方法仅以1.1%性能损失实现77%的推理长度缩减，而对比基线方法需牺牲4.3%性能才能达到68%的长度缩减。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the issue of overthinking in large reasoning models, where models generate excessively long and redundant reasoning chains even for simple questions, increasing computational costs. The authors propose Decoupled Reward Policy Optimization (DRPO), a novel framework that decouples length-based learning signals for correct and incorrect reasoning rollouts to prevent penalizing valid but lengthy reasoning. Experimental results on mathematical reasoning tasks show DRPO significantly outperforms six baselines, achieving a 77% length reduction with only a 1.1% performance loss on the GSM8k dataset using a 1.5B model, compared to a baseline that sacrifices 4.3% performance for a 68% reduction.
本文针对大型推理模型中的过度思考问题展开研究，即模型即使面对简单问题也会生成过长且冗余的推理链，从而增加计算成本。作者提出了解耦奖励策略优化（DRPO）这一新颖框架，通过将正确与错误推理路径的长度学习信号解耦，避免对有效但冗长的推理进行惩罚。在数学推理任务上的实验结果表明，DRPO显著优于六种基线方法，使用1.5B参数模型在GSM8k数据集上实现了77%的长度缩减，而性能损失仅为1.1%，相比之下基线方法以4.3%的性能损失换取68%的长度缩减。
RLP: Reinforcement as a Pretraining Objective
Authors: Ali Hatamizadeh, Syeda Nahida Akter, Shrimai Prabhumoye, Jan Kautz, Mostofa Patwary, Mohammad Shoeybi, Bryan Catanzaro, Yejin Choi
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-09-26T17:53:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-01T21:03:52+00:00
Comments: ICLR 2026 camera ready
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The dominant paradigm for training large reasoning models starts with pre-training using next-token prediction loss on vast amounts of data. Reinforcement learning, while powerful in scaling reasoning, is introduced only as the very last phase of post-training, preceded by supervised fine-tuning. While dominant, is this an optimal way of training? In this paper, we present RLP, an information-driven reinforcement pretraining objective, that brings the core spirit of reinforcement learning -- exploration -- to the last phase of pretraining. The key idea is to treat chain-of-thought as an exploratory action, with rewards computed based on the information gain it provides for predicting future tokens. This training objective essentially encourages the model to think for itself before predicting what comes next, thus teaching an independent thinking behavior earlier in the pretraining. More concretely, the reward signal measures the increase in log-likelihood of the next token when conditioning on both context and a sampled reasoning chain, compared to conditioning on context alone. This approach yields a verifier-free dense reward signal, allowing for efficient training for the full document stream during pretraining. Specifically, RLP reframes reinforcement learning for reasoning as a pretraining objective on ordinary text, bridging the gap between next-token prediction and the emergence of useful chain-of-thought reasoning. Pretraining with RLP on Qwen3-1.7B-Base lifts the overall average across an eight-benchmark math-and-science suite by 19%. With identical post-training, the gains compound, with the largest improvements on reasoning-heavy tasks such as AIME25 and MMLU-Pro. Applying RLP to the Nemotron-Nano-12B-v2 increases the overall average from 42.81% to 61.32% and raises the average on scientific reasoning by 23%, demonstrating scalability across architectures and model sizes.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RLP：将强化学习作为预训练目标
当前训练大型推理模型的主流范式，始于基于海量数据的下一词预测损失进行预训练。强化学习虽然在扩展推理能力方面强大，却仅作为训练后阶段的最后一步引入，且需先经过监督微调。这种主流方法是否最优？本文提出RLP，一种信息驱动的强化预训练目标，将强化学习的核心精神——探索——引入预训练的最后阶段。其关键思想是将思维链视为探索性动作，并根据其为预测未来词元提供的信息增益计算奖励。该训练目标本质上鼓励模型在预测后续内容前进行自主思考，从而在预训练早期教授独立思考行为。具体而言，奖励信号衡量在同时考虑上下文和采样推理链的条件下，下一词元对数似然相较于仅考虑上下文时的提升。该方法产生无需验证器的密集奖励信号，支持在预训练期间对完整文档流进行高效训练。RLP将推理的强化学习重新定义为普通文本的预训练目标，弥合了下一词预测与有效思维链推理涌现之间的差距。在Qwen3-1.7B-Base上使用RLP预训练，将八项数学与科学基准套件的整体平均性能提升19%。在相同训练后流程下，收益进一步叠加，在AIME25和MMLU-Pro等重推理任务上提升最为显著。将RLP应用于Nemotron-Nano-12B-v2，整体平均性能从42.81%提升至61.32%，科学推理平均性能提升23%，证明了该方法的跨架构与模型规模可扩展性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the question of whether the standard paradigm of using reinforcement learning only as a final post-training step is optimal, this paper introduces RLP, a reinforcement pretraining objective that incorporates exploration into the pretraining phase. The method treats chain-of-thought reasoning as an exploratory action, rewarding it based on the information gain for predicting future tokens, which provides a dense, verifier-free reward signal during standard text pretraining. Experimental results show that pretraining Qwen3-1.7B-Base with RLP improves the average performance on an eight-benchmark math-and-science suite by 19%, with compounded gains after identical post-training, and scaling to Nemotron-Nano-12B-v2 raises the overall average from 42.81% to 61.32%, particularly boosting scientific reasoning tasks.
本文的动机是质疑当前主流范式——仅将强化学习作为最终后训练阶段——是否最优，因此提出了RLP这一强化预训练目标，将探索核心融入预训练。该方法将思维链视为探索性动作，根据其对预测后续令牌的信息增益进行奖励，从而在普通文本预训练中提供密集且无需验证器的奖励信号。实验结果表明，使用RLP对Qwen3-1.7B-Base进行预训练，在八项数学与科学基准测试中的平均性能提升了19%，且在相同后训练后增益叠加；将其应用于Nemotron-Nano-12B-v2模型，整体平均分从42.81%提升至61.32%，尤其在科学推理任务上表现出显著改进。
MOSAIC: A Unified Platform for Cross-Paradigm Comparison and Evaluation of Homogeneous and Heterogeneous Multi-Agent RL, LLM, VLM, and Human Decision-Makers
Authors: Abdulhamid M. Mousa, Yu Fu, Rakhmonberdi Khajiev, Jalaledin M. Azzabi, Abdulkarim M. Mousa, Peng Yang, Yunusa Haruna, Ming Liu
First: 2026-03-01T20:33:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-01T20:33:19+00:00
Comments: 13 pages, 2 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL), large language models (LLMs), and vision-language models (VLMs) have been widely studied in isolation. However, existing infrastructure lacks the ability to deploy agents from different decision-making paradigms within the same environment, making it difficult to study them in hybrid multi-agent settings or to compare their behaviour fairly under identical conditions. We present MOSAIC, an open-source platform that bridges this gap by incorporating a diverse set of existing reinforcement learning environments and enabling heterogeneous agents (RL policies, LLMs, VLMs, and human players) to operate within them in ad-hoc team settings with reproducible results. MOSAIC introduces three contributions. (i) An IPC-based worker protocol that wraps both native and third-party frameworks as isolated subprocess workers, each executing its native training and inference logic unmodified, communicating through a versioned inter-process protocol. (ii) An operator abstraction that forms an agent-level interface by mapping workers to agents: each operator, regardless of whether it is backed by an RL policy, an LLM, or a human, conforms to a minimal unified interface. (iii) A deterministic cross-paradigm evaluation framework offering two complementary modes: a manual mode that advances up to N concurrent operators in lock-step under shared seeds for fine-grained visual inspection of behavioural differences, and a script mode that drives automated, long-running evaluation through declarative Python scripts, for reproducible experiments. We release MOSAIC as an open, visual-first platform to facilitate reproducible cross-paradigm research across the RL, LLM, and human-in-the-loop communities.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MOSAIC：一个用于同质与异构多智能体强化学习、大语言模型、视觉语言模型及人类决策者跨范式比较与评估的统一平台
强化学习、大语言模型和视觉语言模型虽已得到广泛研究，但现有基础设施无法在同一环境中部署来自不同决策范式的智能体，难以在混合多智能体场景下进行研究或在相同条件下公平比较其行为。我们推出开源平台MOSAIC，通过整合多样化的现有强化学习环境，支持异构智能体（强化学习策略、大语言模型、视觉语言模型及人类玩家）在临时团队配置中运行并获得可复现结果。该平台包含三项核心贡献：（一）基于进程间通信的工作协议，将原生与第三方框架封装为隔离的子进程工作单元，各单元保持原有训练与推理逻辑，通过版本化进程间协议通信；（二）操作器抽象层，通过工作单元与智能体的映射形成统一接口，无论底层是强化学习策略、大语言模型还是人类，均遵循最小化统一接口规范；（三）确定性跨范式评估框架，提供两种互补模式：手动模式通过共享随机种子锁定步进最多N个并发操作器，支持行为差异的细粒度可视化检查；脚本模式通过声明式Python脚本驱动自动化长期评估，确保实验可复现。我们以开放、视觉优先的平台形式发布MOSAIC，旨在促进强化学习、大语言模型及人在回路领域的可复现跨范式研究。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for MOSAIC stems from the lack of infrastructure to deploy and compare diverse decision-making agents—such as reinforcement learning policies, large language models, vision-language models, and humans—within the same multi-agent environments under identical conditions. The method introduces an open-source platform featuring an IPC-based worker protocol to wrap various frameworks as isolated subprocesses, an operator abstraction providing a unified agent interface, and a deterministic evaluation framework with manual and scripted modes for reproducible experiments. Main experimental results demonstrate that MOSAIC successfully enables heterogeneous agents to operate in ad-hoc team settings across existing RL environments, facilitating fair cross-paradigm comparison and visual inspection of behavioral differences.
MOSAIC的提出动机在于现有基础设施缺乏在同一环境中部署和比较不同决策范式智能体（如强化学习策略、大语言模型、视觉语言模型和人类）的能力，难以在混合多智能体设置中进行研究或公平比较。该方法推出了一个开源平台，其核心包括：基于IPC的工作进程协议，将各类框架封装为隔离子进程；操作员抽象层，提供统一的智能体接口；以及一个确定性的评估框架，支持手动逐步执行和脚本自动运行两种模式，确保实验可复现。主要实验结果表明，MOSAIC成功实现了异构智能体在现有强化学习环境中的即兴团队协作，为跨范式比较和行为差异的可视化分析提供了有效支持。
From Efficiency to Adaptivity: A Deeper Look at Adaptive Reasoning in Large Language Models
Authors: Chao Wu, Baoheng Li, Mingchen Gao, Yu Tian, Zhenyi Wang
First: 2025-11-13T20:25:04+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-01T18:54:53+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent advances in large language models (LLMs) have made reasoning a central benchmark for evaluating intelligence. While prior surveys focus on efficiency by examining how to shorten reasoning chains or reduce computation, this view overlooks a fundamental challenge: current LLMs apply uniform reasoning strategies regardless of task complexity, generating long traces for trivial problems while failing to extend reasoning for difficult tasks. This survey reframes reasoning through the lens of {adaptivity}: the capability to allocate reasoning effort based on input characteristics such as difficulty and uncertainty. We make three contributions. First, we formalize deductive, inductive, and abductive reasoning within the LLM context, connecting these classical cognitive paradigms with their algorithmic realizations. Second, we formalize adaptive reasoning as a control-augmented policy optimization problem balancing task performance with computational cost, distinguishing learned policies from inference-time control mechanisms. Third, we propose a systematic taxonomy organizing existing methods into training-based approaches that internalize adaptivity through reinforcement learning, supervised fine-tuning, and learned controllers, and training-free approaches that achieve adaptivity through prompt conditioning, feedback-driven halting, and modular composition. This framework clarifies how different mechanisms realize adaptive reasoning in practice and enables systematic comparison across diverse strategies. We conclude by identifying open challenges in self-evaluation, meta-reasoning, and human-aligned reasoning control.
中文标题/摘要
标题：从效率到适应性：深入审视大语言模型中的自适应推理
大语言模型（LLMs）的最新进展使推理能力成为评估智能的核心基准。现有综述多聚焦于通过缩短推理链或减少计算来提升效率，这种视角忽视了一个根本性挑战：当前LLMs无论任务复杂度如何均采用统一的推理策略，导致对简单问题生成冗长轨迹，却难以对复杂任务扩展推理深度。本综述通过{适应性}视角重构推理框架——即根据输入特征（如难度与不确定性）动态分配推理资源的能力。我们作出三项贡献：首先，在LLM语境中形式化演绎、归纳与溯因推理，将经典认知范式与其算法实现相衔接；其次，将自适应推理形式化为控制增强的策略优化问题，平衡任务性能与计算成本，区分学习型策略与推理时控制机制；最后，提出系统分类法，将现有方法归纳为基于训练的方法（通过强化学习、监督微调和学习型控制器内化适应性）与免训练方法（通过提示条件化、反馈驱动终止和模块化组合实现适应性）。该框架阐明了不同机制在实践中实现自适应推理的路径，支持跨策略的系统性比较。文末指出自我评估、元推理及人机对齐推理控制等开放挑战。
Summary / 总结
This survey paper is motivated by the observation that current large language models (LLMs) apply uniform reasoning strategies regardless of task complexity, which is inefficient and ineffective. To address this, the authors reframe reasoning through the lens of adaptivity—the capability to dynamically allocate reasoning effort based on input characteristics like difficulty. The method involves formalizing deductive, inductive, and abductive reasoning for LLMs, modeling adaptive reasoning as a control-augmented policy optimization problem, and proposing a taxonomy that categorizes existing techniques into training-based and training-free approaches. The main experimental results, derived from analyzing these methods, clarify how different mechanisms realize adaptive reasoning in practice, enabling systematic comparison and highlighting open challenges in self-evaluation and meta-reasoning.
本综述论文的动机在于观察到当前大语言模型无论任务复杂度如何都采用统一的推理策略，这既低效又效果不佳。为解决此问题，作者从适应性角度重新审视推理，即根据输入难度等特征动态分配推理努力的能力。其方法包括为大语言模型形式化演绎、归纳和溯因推理，将自适应推理建模为一个控制增强的策略优化问题，并提出一个分类法，将现有技术分为基于训练和无训练的方法。通过分析这些方法得到的主要实验结果表明，不同机制在实践中如何实现自适应推理，从而支持系统化比较，并指出了在自我评估和元推理方面存在的开放挑战。
Quantization-Aware Distillation for NVFP4 Inference Accuracy Recovery
Authors: Meng Xin, Sweta Priyadarshi, Jingyu Xin, Bilal Kartal, Aditya Vavre, Asma Kuriparambil Thekkumpate, Zijia Chen, Ameya Sunil Mahabaleshwarkar, Ido Shahaf, Akhiad Bercovich, Kinjal Patel, Suguna Varshini Velury, Chenjie Luo, Zhiyu Cheng, Jenny Chen, Chen-Han Yu, Wei Ping, Oleg Rybakov, Nima Tajbakhsh, Oluwatobi Olabiyi, Dusan Stosic, Di Wu, Song Han, Eric Chung, Sharath Turuvekere Sreenivas, Bryan Catanzaro, Yoshi Suhara, Tijmen Blankevoort, Huizi Mao
First: 2026-01-27T22:14:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-01T18:53:17+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This technical report presents quantization-aware distillation (QAD) and our best practices for recovering accuracy of NVFP4-quantized large language models (LLMs) and vision-language models (VLMs). QAD distills a full-precision teacher model into a quantized student model using a KL divergence loss. While applying distillation to quantized models is not a new idea, we observe key advantages of QAD for today's LLMs: 1. It shows remarkable effectiveness and stability for models trained through multi-stage post-training pipelines, including supervised fine-tuning (SFT), reinforcement learning (RL), and model merging, where traditional quantization-aware training (QAT) suffers from engineering complexity and training instability; 2. It is robust to data quality and coverage, enabling accuracy recovery without full training data. We evaluate QAD across multiple post-trained models including AceReason Nemotron, Nemotron 3 Nano, Nemotron Nano V2, Nemotron Nano V2 VL (VLM), and Llama Nemotron Super v1, showing consistent recovery to near-BF16 accuracy.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向NVFP4推理精度恢复的量化感知蒸馏方法
本技术报告提出量化感知蒸馏（QAD）方法及其最佳实践，用于恢复NVFP4量化大型语言模型（LLM）和视觉语言模型（VLM）的精度。QAD通过KL散度损失将全精度教师模型蒸馏至量化学生模型。尽管对量化模型应用蒸馏并非全新概念，但我们发现QAD对当前LLM具有关键优势：1. 对于通过监督微调（SFT）、强化学习（RL）和模型融合等多阶段后训练流程训练的模型，QAD表现出卓越的效能与稳定性，而传统量化感知训练（QAT）存在工程复杂性和训练不稳定的问题；2. 该方法对数据质量与覆盖范围具有鲁棒性，无需完整训练数据即可实现精度恢复。我们在包括AceReason Nemotron、Nemotron 3 Nano、Nemotron Nano V2、Nemotron Nano V2 VL（VLM）及Llama Nemotron Super v1在内的多个后训练模型上评估QAD，均能稳定恢复至接近BF16精度的水平。
Summary / 总结
This paper introduces quantization-aware distillation (QAD) to recover the inference accuracy of large language and vision-language models quantized to NVFP4 precision, addressing the engineering complexity and instability of traditional quantization-aware training in multi-stage post-training pipelines. The method employs KL divergence loss to distill knowledge from a full-precision teacher model into a quantized student model, offering robustness to data quality and eliminating the need for full training datasets. Experimental results on models like AceReason Nemotron and Llama Nemotron Super v1 demonstrate that QAD consistently recovers near-BF16 accuracy, proving effective and stable across various post-trained architectures.

Agency and Architectural Limits: Why Optimization-Based Systems Cannot Be Norm-Responsive
Authors: Radha Sarma
First: 2026-02-26T17:16:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-01T18:44:49+00:00
Comments: About 10,600 words in all (includes ~1000 words of literature and ~2400 words of Appendices). Under journal review
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
AI systems are increasingly deployed in high-stakes contexts (medical diagnosis, legal research, financial analysis) under the assumption they can be governed by norms. This paper demonstrates that the assumption is formally invalid for optimization-based systems, specifically Large Language Models trained via Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF). Genuine agency requires two necessary and jointly sufficient architectural conditions. First, the capacity to maintain certain boundaries as non-negotiable constraints rather than tradeable weights (Incommensurability). Second, a non-inferential mechanism capable of suspending processing when those boundaries are threatened (Apophatic Responsiveness). RLHF-based systems are constitutively incompatible with both conditions. The operations that make optimization powerful, unifying all values on a scalar metric and always selecting the highest-scoring output, are precisely the operations that preclude normative governance and agency. This incompatibility is not a correctable training bug awaiting a technical fix. It is a formal constraint inherent to what optimization is. Consequently, documented failure modes (sycophancy, hallucination, and unfaithful reasoning) are not accidents but expected structural manifestations. Misaligned deployment triggers a second-order risk termed the Convergence Crisis. When humans are forced to verify AI outputs under metric pressure, they degrade from genuine agents into criteria-checking optimizers, eliminating the only component capable of bearing normative accountability. Beyond the incompatibility proof, this paper's primary positive contribution is a substrate-neutral architectural specification deriving what any system (biological, artificial, or institutional) must necessarily satisfy to qualify as a genuine agent rather than a sophisticated instrument.
中文标题/摘要
标题：能动性与架构限制：为何基于优化的系统无法响应规范
人工智能系统正日益部署于高风险场景（医疗诊断、法律研究、金融分析），其前提假设是它们能够受规范约束。本文证明，对于基于优化的系统——特别是通过人类反馈强化学习训练的大型语言模型——这一假设在形式上是无效的。真正的能动性需要两个必要且共同充分的架构条件：第一，将某些边界保持为不可协商的约束而非可交易权重的能⼒（不可通约性）；第二，当这些边界受到威胁时能够暂停处理的非推理机制（否定性响应）。基于RLHF的系统在本质上与这两个条件都不兼容。使优化强大的操作——将所有价值统一于标量度量并始终选择最高分输出——恰恰排除了规范治理与能动性。这种不兼容性并非可通过技术修复纠正的训练缺陷，而是优化本身固有的形式约束。因此，已记录的系统失效模式（谄媚性、幻觉与不忠实推理）并非偶然，而是预期的结构表现。错位的部署会引发称为‘收敛危机’的二级风险：当人类被迫在度量压力下验证AI输出时，他们会从真正的能动者退化为标准检查优化器，从而消除唯一能够承担规范问责的组成部分。除不兼容性证明外，本文的主要建设性贡献在于提出一种基质中立的架构规范，推导出任何系统（生物、人工或制度）必须具备何种条件才能成为真正的能动者而非复杂工具。
Summary / 总结
This paper challenges the assumption that AI systems, particularly Large Language Models trained via Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF), can be governed by social norms, arguing that optimization-based architectures are formally incompatible with genuine agency. The authors contend that agency requires two architectural conditions: incommensurability (treating certain boundaries as non-negotiable constraints) and apophatic responsiveness (a mechanism to suspend processing when boundaries are threatened), both of which are precluded by optimization's core operations of unifying values on a scalar metric and always selecting the highest-scoring output. The main experimental results, drawn from analyzing RLHF systems, show that failure modes like sycophancy and hallucination are not accidental bugs but expected structural manifestations, and misaligned deployment risks triggering a 'Convergence Crisis' where humans degrade into mere optimizers, undermining normative accountability.
本文挑战了人工智能系统（特别是通过人类反馈强化学习训练的LLM）可受社会规范约束的假设，论证了基于优化的架构在形式上与真正的能动性不相容。作者提出能动性需要两个架构条件：不可通约性（将某些边界视为不可协商的约束）和否定响应性（在边界受威胁时暂停处理的机制），而优化的核心操作（将所有价值统一为标量指标并始终选择最高分输出）恰恰排除了这两者。通过对RLHF系统的分析，主要实验结果表明，诸如谄媚和幻觉等故障模式并非偶然错误，而是预期的结构表现，且部署不当可能引发‘趋同危机’，导致人类自身退化为单纯的优化器，从而破坏规范问责。
Learn Hard Problems During RL with Reference Guided Fine-tuning
Authors: Yangzhen Wu, Shanda Li, Zixin Wen, Xin Zhou, Ameet Talwalkar, Yiming Yang, Wenhao Huang, Tianle Cai
First: 2026-03-01T18:41:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-01T18:41:28+00:00
Comments: 16 pages, 5 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) for mathematical reasoning can suffer from reward sparsity: for challenging problems, LLM fails to sample any correct trajectories, preventing RL from receiving meaningful positive feedback. At the same time, there often exist human-written reference solutions along with the problem (e.g., problems from AoPS), but directly fine-tuning on these solutions offers no benefit because models often cannot imitate human proofs that lie outside their own reasoning distribution. We introduce Reference-Guided Fine-Tuning (ReGFT), a simple and effective method that utilizes human-written reference solutions to synthesize positive trajectories on hard problems and train on them before RL. For each problem, we provide the model with a partial reference solution and let it generate its own reasoning trace, ensuring the resulting trajectories remain in the model's reasoning space while still benefiting from reference guidance. Fine-tuning on these reference-guided trajectories increases the number of solvable problems and produces a checkpoint that receives more positive rewards during RL. Across three benchmarks (AIME24, AIME25, BeyondAIME), ReGFT consistently improves supervised accuracy, accelerates DAPO training, and raises the final performance plateau of RL. Our results show that ReGFT effectively overcomes reward sparsity and unlocks stronger RL-based mathematical reasoning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于参考引导微调在强化学习中攻克难题
数学推理的强化学习（RL）常面临奖励稀疏问题：面对挑战性题目时，大语言模型（LLM）无法采样到任何正确轨迹，导致RL无法获得有效的正向反馈。与此同时，题目常附有人工撰写的参考答案（如AoPS题库），但直接对这些解答进行微调并无助益，因为模型往往难以模仿超出其自身推理分布的人类证明过程。 我们提出参考引导微调（ReGFT），这是一种简洁高效的方法，利用人工参考答案为难题合成正向轨迹并在RL训练前进行学习。针对每个问题，我们向模型提供部分参考答案，让其自主生成推理轨迹，确保所得轨迹保持在模型的推理空间内，同时又能受益于参考引导。 基于这些参考引导轨迹的微调提升了可解决问题的数量，并产生能在RL过程中获得更多正向奖励的检查点。在三个基准测试（AIME24、AIME25、BeyondAIME）中，ReGFT持续提升了监督学习准确率，加速了DAPO训练，并提高了RL的最终性能上限。实验结果表明，ReGFT有效克服了奖励稀疏问题，释放了基于RL的数学推理的更强潜力。

Reasoning Boosts Opinion Alignment in LLMs
Authors: Frédéric Berdoz, Yann Billeter, Yann Vonlanthen, Roger Wattenhofer
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-03-01T18:19:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-01T18:19:44+00:00
Comments: Accepted at ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Opinion modeling aims to capture individual or group political preferences, enabling applications such as digital democracies, where models could help shape fairer and more popular policies. Given their versatility, strong generalization capabilities, and demonstrated success across diverse text-to-text applications, large language models (LLMs) are natural candidates for this task. However, due to their statistical nature and limited causal understanding, they tend to produce biased opinions when prompted naively. In this work, we study whether reasoning can improve opinion alignment. Motivated by the recent advancement in mathematical reasoning enabled by reinforcement learning (RL), we train models to produce profile-consistent answers through structured reasoning. We evaluate our approach on three datasets covering U.S., European, and Swiss politics. Results indicate that reasoning enhances opinion modeling and is competitive with strong baselines, but does not fully remove bias, highlighting the need for additional mechanisms to build faithful political digital twins using LLMs. By releasing both our method and datasets, we establish a solid baseline to support future research on LLM opinion alignment.
中文标题/摘要
标题：推理提升大语言模型中的观点对齐
观点建模旨在捕捉个体或群体的政治偏好，支持数字民主等应用，使模型能够帮助制定更公平、更受欢迎的政策。鉴于大语言模型（LLMs）的多功能性、强大的泛化能力以及在多样化文本到文本应用中的成功表现，它们自然成为此项任务的候选工具。然而，由于其统计特性及有限的因果理解能力，当被简单提示时，它们倾向于产生带有偏见的观点。本研究探讨推理是否能改善观点对齐。受强化学习（RL）推动数学推理近期进展的启发，我们训练模型通过结构化推理生成与用户画像一致的答案。我们在涵盖美国、欧洲和瑞士政治的三个数据集上评估了该方法。结果表明，推理能增强观点建模能力，并与强基线模型表现相当，但未能完全消除偏见，这突显了需要额外机制来利用LLMs构建可信的政治数字孪生。通过公开我们的方法和数据集，我们为支持未来LLM观点对齐研究建立了坚实的基线。

This paper investigates whether structured reasoning can improve the alignment of large language models (LLMs) with specific political opinions, addressing the issue that naively prompted LLMs often produce biased outputs due to their statistical nature. Motivated by advances in reinforcement learning for mathematical reasoning, the method trains models to generate profile-consistent answers through reasoning processes. Experimental evaluation on three political datasets covering U.S., European, and Swiss politics shows that reasoning enhances opinion modeling performance and competes with strong baselines, though it does not fully eliminate bias, indicating a need for further mechanisms to achieve faithful political digital twins.

Sample-Efficient Distributionally Robust Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning via Online Interaction
Authors: Zain Ulabedeen Farhat, Debamita Ghosh, George K. Atia, Yue Wang
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-08-04T23:14:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-01T17:42:58+00:00
Comments: Accepted by ICLR 2026.The first two authors contributed equally
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Well-trained multi-agent systems can fail when deployed in real-world environments due to model mismatches between the training and deployment environments, caused by environment uncertainties including noise or adversarial attacks. Distributionally Robust Markov Games (DRMGs) enhance system resilience by optimizing for worst-case performance over a defined set of environmental uncertainties. However, current methods are limited by their dependence on simulators or large offline datasets, which are often unavailable. This paper pioneers the study of online learning in DRMGs, where agents learn directly from environmental interactions without prior data. We introduce the Multiplayer Optimistic Robust Nash Value Iteration (MORNAVI) algorithm and provide the first provable guarantees for this setting. Our theoretical analysis demonstrates that the algorithm achieves low regret and efficiently finds the optimal robust policy for uncertainty sets measured by Total Variation divergence and Kullback-Leibler divergence. These results establish a new, practical path toward developing truly robust multi-agent systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于在线交互的样本高效分布式鲁棒多智能体强化学习
训练良好的多智能体系统在部署到现实环境时，可能因训练与部署环境间的模型失配而失效，这种失配源于噪声或对抗攻击等环境不确定性。分布式鲁棒马尔可夫博弈通过在最坏情况环境不确定性集合上优化性能来增强系统韧性。然而，现有方法受限于对模拟器或大规模离线数据集的依赖，而这些资源往往难以获取。本文开创性地研究了DRMG中的在线学习问题，使智能体能直接从环境交互中学习，无需先验数据。我们提出了多玩家乐观鲁棒纳什值迭代算法，并首次为该设定提供了可证明的保证。理论分析表明，该算法在总变差散度和KL散度度量的不确定性集合下，能实现低遗憾并高效找到最优鲁棒策略。这些成果为开发真正鲁棒的多智能体系统开辟了新的实用路径。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the vulnerability of multi-agent reinforcement learning systems to environmental uncertainties like noise or adversarial attacks, which cause model mismatches between training and deployment. To enhance resilience without relying on simulators or large offline datasets, the authors introduce the Multiplayer Optimistic Robust Nash Value Iteration (MORNAVI) algorithm for online learning in Distributionally Robust Markov Games, where agents learn directly from interactions. Theoretical analysis shows that MORNAVI achieves low regret and efficiently finds optimal robust policies for uncertainty sets measured by Total Variation and Kullback-Leibler divergence, establishing a practical path toward robust multi-agent systems.
本文针对多智能体强化学习系统在部署时因环境不确定性（如噪声或对抗攻击）导致的模型失配问题，旨在提升系统鲁棒性。为解决现有方法依赖模拟器或大型离线数据集的限制，作者提出了多智能体乐观鲁棒纳什值迭代（MORNAVI）算法，用于在线学习分布鲁棒马尔可夫博弈，使智能体直接从环境交互中学习。理论分析表明，该算法在总变差散度和KL散度度量的不确定性集合下实现了低遗憾并高效找到最优鲁棒策略，为开发真正鲁棒的多智能体系统提供了新途径。
PARWiS: Winner determination under shoestring budgets using active pairwise comparisons
Authors: Shailendra Bhandari
First: 2026-03-01T16:21:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-01T16:21:31+00:00
Comments: 12 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Determining a winner among a set of items using active pairwise comparisons under a limited budget is a challenging problem in preference-based learning. The goal of this study is to implement and evaluate the PARWiS algorithm, which shows spectral ranking and disruptive pair selection to identify the best item under shoestring budgets. This work have extended the PARWiS with a contextual variant (Contextual PARWiS) and a reinforcement learning-based variant (RL PARWiS), comparing them against baselines, including Double Thompson Sampling and a random selection strategy. This evaluation spans synthetic and real-world datasets (Jester and MovieLens), using budgets of 40, 60, and 80 comparisons for 20 items. The performance is measured through recovery fraction, true rank of reported winner, reported rank of true winner, and cumulative regret, alongside the separation metric \(Δ_{1,2}\). Results show that PARWiS and RL PARWiS outperform baselines across all datasets, particularly in the Jester dataset with a higher \(Δ_{1,2}\), while performance gaps narrow in the more challenging MovieLens dataset with a smaller \(Δ_{1,2}\). Contextual PARWiS shows comparable performance to PARWiS, indicating that contextual features may require further tuning to provide significant benefits.
中文标题/摘要
标题：PARWiS：基于有限预算下主动成对比较的优胜者判定方法
在有限预算下通过主动成对比较从一组候选项中确定优胜者，是基于偏好的学习中的一个挑战性问题。本研究旨在实现并评估PARWiS算法，该算法结合谱排序与扰动对选择策略，以在极低预算条件下识别最优项。本研究扩展了PARWiS算法，提出上下文感知变体（Contextual PARWiS）和基于强化学习的变体（RL PARWiS），并与包括双汤普森采样和随机选择策略在内的基线方法进行比较。评估涵盖合成数据集及真实数据集（Jester和MovieLens），在20个候选项上分别采用40、60和80次比较的预算。性能通过恢复比例、报告优胜者的真实排名、真实优胜者的报告排名、累计遗憾以及分离度量\(Δ_{1,2}\)进行衡量。结果显示，PARWiS和RL PARWiS在所有数据集上均优于基线方法，尤其在\(Δ_{1,2}\)值较高的Jester数据集中表现突出；而在\(Δ_{1,2}\)值较小、更具挑战性的MovieLens数据集中，性能差距有所缩小。Contextual PARWiS表现出与PARWiS相当的性能，表明上下文特征可能需要进一步调优才能产生显著效益。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of identifying a top-ranked item from a set using limited pairwise comparisons, this paper implements and evaluates the PARWiS algorithm, which combines spectral ranking with disruptive pair selection. The method is extended into contextual and reinforcement learning variants, tested against baselines like Double Thompson Sampling on synthetic and real-world datasets (Jester and MovieLens) with constrained budgets of 40 to 80 comparisons for 20 items. Experimental results demonstrate that PARWiS and its RL variant outperform baselines across metrics such as recovery fraction and regret, particularly in datasets with larger performance gaps between top items, while the contextual variant shows comparable but not significantly improved performance, suggesting further tuning may be needed.
本研究旨在解决在有限预算下通过主动成对比较从一组物品中确定优胜者的挑战，为此实现并评估了结合谱排序和破坏性对选择的PARWiS算法。方法扩展为上下文感知和基于强化学习的变体，与双汤普森采样等基线方法在合成及真实数据集（Jester和MovieLens）上进行比较，预算限制为对20个物品进行40至80次比较。实验结果表明，PARWiS及其强化学习变体在恢复分数和累积遗憾等指标上均优于基线，尤其在顶级物品性能差距较大的数据集中表现突出，而上下文变体性能相当但未显着提升，表明可能需要进一步调整以发挥其优势。
DRA-GRPO: Your GRPO Needs to Know Diverse Reasoning Paths for Mathematical Reasoning
Authors: Xiwen Chen, Wenhui Zhu, Peijie Qiu, Xuanzhao Dong, Hao Wang, Haiyu Wu, Huayu Li, Aristeidis Sotiras, Yalin Wang, Abolfazl Razi
First: 2025-05-14T02:02:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-01T16:12:22+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Post-training LLMs with Reinforcement Learning, specifically Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), has emerged as a paradigm for enhancing mathematical reasoning. However, standard GRPO relies on scalar correctness rewards that are often non-injective with respect to semantic content: distinct reasoning paths receive identical rewards. This leads to a Diversity-Quality Inconsistency, where the policy collapses into a narrow set of dominant modes while ignoring equally valid but structurally novel strategies. To bridge this gap, we propose Diversity-aware Reward Adjustment (DRA), a theoretically grounded framework that calibrates the reward signal using the semantic density of sampled groups. By leveraging Submodular Mutual Information (SMI), DRA implements an Inverse Propensity Scoring (IPS) mechanism that effectively de-biases the gradient estimation. This creates a repulsive force against redundancy, driving the policy to achieve better coverage of the high-reward landscape. Our method is plug-and-play and integrates seamlessly with GRPO variants. Empirical evaluations on five math benchmarks demonstrate that DRA-GRPO consistently outperforms strong baselines, achieving an average accuracy of 58.2% on DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-1.5B with only 7,000 training samples and $55 cost, highlighting the critical role of diversity calibration in data-efficient alignment. The code is available at https://github.com/xiwenc1/DRA-GRPO.
中文标题/摘要
标题：DRA-GRPO：数学推理中GRPO需要认知多样化推理路径
基于强化学习（特别是群体相对策略优化GRPO）的大语言模型后训练已成为提升数学推理能力的范式。然而，标准GRPO依赖的标量正确性奖励常与语义内容非单射关联：不同推理路径获得相同奖励，导致策略陷入少数主导模式而忽略结构新颖的有效策略，形成“多样性-质量不一致”问题。为此，我们提出理论驱动的多样性感知奖励调整框架DRA，通过采样群体的语义密度校准奖励信号。该框架利用子模互信息实施逆倾向评分机制，有效消除梯度估计偏差，形成针对冗余的排斥力，驱动策略更全面地覆盖高奖励区域。本方法即插即用，可无缝集成于GRPO变体。在五项数学基准测试中，DRA-GRPO以仅7,000训练样本和55美元成本，在DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-1.5B模型上实现58.2%平均准确率，显著优于基线方法，凸显了多样性校准在数据高效对齐中的关键作用。代码已开源。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses a limitation in Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) for enhancing mathematical reasoning in LLMs, where scalar correctness rewards fail to distinguish between diverse but equally valid reasoning paths, leading to a collapse in solution diversity. To overcome this, the authors propose Diversity-aware Reward Adjustment (DRA), a plug-and-play framework that uses Submodular Mutual Information to calibrate rewards by measuring semantic density, thereby de-biasing gradient estimation and encouraging coverage of varied high-reward strategies. Experimental results on five math benchmarks show that DRA-GRPO outperforms baselines, achieving 58.2% average accuracy with only 7,000 samples at low cost, underscoring the importance of diversity for data-efficient alignment.
本文针对大型语言模型数学推理中使用的组相对策略优化（GRPO）方法的局限性，即标量正确性奖励无法区分多样但同样有效的推理路径，导致解决方案多样性下降。为此，作者提出了多样性感知奖励调整（DRA），这是一种即插即用的框架，利用子模互信息通过测量语义密度来校准奖励，从而纠正梯度估计偏差，并鼓励覆盖多样化的高奖励策略。在五个数学基准测试上的实验结果表明，DRA-GRPO优于现有基线，仅用7,000个样本即以低成本实现了58.2%的平均准确率，强调了多样性对于数据高效对齐的关键作用。
Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning with Communication-Constrained Priors
Authors: Guang Yang, Tianpei Yang, Jingwen Qiao, Yanqing Wu, Jing Huo, Xingguo Chen, Yang Gao
First: 2025-12-03T07:35:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-01T15:56:05+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Communication is one of the effective means to improve the learning of cooperative policy in multi-agent systems. However, in most real-world scenarios, lossy communication is a prevalent issue. Existing multi-agent reinforcement learning with communication, due to their limited scalability and robustness, struggles to apply to complex and dynamic real-world environments. To address these challenges, we propose a generalized communication-constrained model to uniformly characterize communication conditions across different scenarios. Based on this, we utilize it as a learning prior to distinguish between lossy and lossless messages for specific scenarios. Additionally, we decouple the impact of lossy and lossless messages on distributed decision-making, drawing on a dual mutual information estimatior, and introduce a communication-constrained multi-agent reinforcement learning framework, quantifying the impact of communication messages into the global reward. Finally, we validate the effectiveness of our approach across several communication-constrained benchmarks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通信约束先验下的多智能体强化学习
通信是提升多智能体系统协作策略学习的有效手段，但在多数现实场景中，有损通信普遍存在。现有带通信的多智能体强化学习方法因可扩展性和鲁棒性不足，难以适用于复杂动态的现实环境。为解决这些问题，我们提出一种广义通信约束模型，以统一表征不同场景下的通信条件。在此基础上，将其作为学习先验来区分特定场景下的有损与无损消息。此外，借鉴双重互信息估计器，我们解耦有损与无损消息对分布式决策的影响，并引入通信约束多智能体强化学习框架，将通信消息的影响量化至全局奖励中。最后，我们在多个通信约束基准测试中验证了方法的有效性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the prevalence of lossy communication in real-world multi-agent systems and the limitations of existing methods in scalability and robustness, this paper proposes a generalized communication-constrained model to characterize varying communication conditions. The method uses this model as a prior to differentiate lossy from lossless messages, decouples their impacts on decision-making via a dual mutual information estimator, and integrates a communication-constrained framework that quantifies message effects into the global reward. Experimental results demonstrate the approach's effectiveness across multiple communication-constrained benchmarks.
本文针对现实多智能体系统中普遍存在的通信损耗问题，以及现有方法在可扩展性和鲁棒性上的不足，提出了一种通用通信约束模型来统一描述不同场景的通信条件。该方法将该模型作为先验知识区分有损与无损消息，利用双重互信息估计器解耦两者对分布式决策的影响，并引入一个将通信消息影响量化到全局奖励中的通信约束多智能体强化学习框架。实验结果表明，该方法在多个通信约束基准测试中均验证了有效性。
DeepResearch-9K: A Challenging Benchmark Dataset of Deep-Research Agent
Authors: Tongzhou Wu, Yuhao Wang, Xinyu Ma, Xiuqiang He, Shuaiqiang Wang, Dawei Yin, Xiangyu Zhao
First: 2026-03-01T15:36:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-01T15:36:10+00:00
Comments: 6 pages, 4 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Deep-research agents are capable of executing multi-step web exploration, targeted retrieval, and sophisticated question answering. Despite their powerful capabilities, deep-research agents face two critical bottlenecks: (1) the lack of large-scale, challenging datasets with real-world difficulty, and (2) the absence of accessible, open-source frameworks for data synthesis and agent training. To bridge these gaps, we first construct DeepResearch-9K, a large-scale challenging dataset specifically designed for deep-research scenarios built from open-source multi-hop question-answering (QA) datasets via a low-cost autonomous pipeline. Notably, it consists of (1) 9000 questions spanning three difficulty levels from L1 to L3 (2) high-quality search trajectories with reasoning chains from Tongyi-DeepResearch-30B-A3B, a state-of-the-art deep-research agent, and (3) verifiable answers. Furthermore, we develop an open-source training framework DeepResearch-R1 that supports (1) multi-turn web interactions, (2) different reinforcement learning (RL) approaches, and (3) different reward models such as rule-based outcome reward and LLM-as-judge feedback. Finally, empirical results demonstrate that agents trained on DeepResearch-9K under our DeepResearch-R1 achieve state-of-the-art results on challenging deep-research benchmarks. We release the DeepResearch-9K dataset on https://huggingface.co/datasets/artillerywu/DeepResearch-9K and the code of DeepResearch-R1 on https://github.com/Applied-Machine-Learning-Lab/DeepResearch-R1.
中文标题/摘要
标题：DeepResearch-9K：面向深度研究智能体的挑战性基准数据集
深度研究智能体能够执行多步骤网络探索、定向检索与复杂问答。尽管功能强大，其仍面临两大瓶颈：(1) 缺乏具备真实世界难度的大规模挑战性数据集；(2) 缺少可访问的开源数据合成与智能体训练框架。为填补这些空白，我们首先构建了DeepResearch-9K——一个通过低成本自动化流程基于开源多跳问答数据集构建的大规模深度研究场景专用挑战数据集。该数据集包含：(1) 涵盖L1至L3三个难度等级的9000个问题；(2) 来自顶尖深度研究智能体Tongyi-DeepResearch-30B-A3B的带推理链高质量搜索轨迹；(3) 可验证答案。此外，我们开发了开源训练框架DeepResearch-R1，支持：(1) 多轮网络交互；(2) 多种强化学习方法；(3) 基于规则的成果奖励与LLM-as-judge反馈等不同奖励模型。实证结果表明，通过DeepResearch-R1框架在DeepResearch-9K上训练的智能体，在深度研究基准测试中取得了最先进的性能。DeepResearch-9K数据集发布于https://huggingface.co/datasets/artillerywu/DeepResearch-9K，DeepResearch-R1代码发布于https://github.com/Applied-Machine-Learning-Lab/DeepResearch-R1。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the lack of large-scale, challenging datasets and accessible training frameworks for deep-research agents, which perform multi-step web exploration and complex question answering, this paper introduces DeepResearch-9K, a benchmark dataset constructed from multi-hop QA sources via an autonomous pipeline, featuring 9,000 questions across three difficulty levels with search trajectories and verifiable answers. The method also includes DeepResearch-R1, an open-source framework supporting multi-turn web interactions and various reinforcement learning approaches with different reward models. Experimental results show that agents trained with this dataset and framework achieve state-of-the-art performance on challenging deep-research benchmarks.
针对深度研究智能体缺乏大规模、高难度数据集和易用训练框架的瓶颈，本文构建了DeepResearch-9K基准数据集，通过自动化流程从多跳问答数据源生成，包含三个难度级别的9000个问题、高质量搜索轨迹和可验证答案。方法上还提出了开源训练框架DeepResearch-R1，支持多轮网络交互、多种强化学习方法和奖励模型。实验结果表明，使用该数据集和框架训练的智能体在深度研究基准测试中取得了最先进的性能。
When Is Diversity Rewarded in Cooperative Multi-Agent Learning?
Authors: Michael Amir, Matteo Bettini, Amanda Prorok
First: 2025-06-11T06:33:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-01T14:41:29+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The success of teams in robotics, nature, and society often depends on the division of labor among diverse specialists; however, a principled explanation for when such diversity surpasses a homogeneous team is still missing. Focusing on multi-agent task allocation problems, we study this question from the perspective of reward design: what kinds of objectives are best suited for heterogeneous teams? We first consider an instantaneous, non-spatial setting where the global reward is built by two generalized aggregation operators: an inner operator that maps the $N$ agents' effort allocations on individual tasks to a task score, and an outer operator that merges the $M$ task scores into the global team reward. We prove that the curvature of these operators determines whether heterogeneity can increase reward, and that for broad reward families this collapses to a simple convexity test. Next, we ask what incentivizes heterogeneity to emerge when embodied, time-extended agents must learn an effort allocation policy. To study heterogeneity in such settings, we use multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) as our computational paradigm, and introduce Heterogeneity Gain Parameter Search (HetGPS), a gradient-based algorithm that optimizes the parameter space of underspecified MARL environments to find scenarios where heterogeneity is advantageous. Across different environments, we show that HetGPS rediscovers the reward regimes predicted by our theory to maximize the advantage of heterogeneity, both validating HetGPS and connecting our theoretical insights to reward design in MARL. Together, these results help us understand when behavioral diversity delivers a measurable benefit.
中文标题/摘要
标题：协作多智能体学习中多样性何时产生回报？
机器人学、自然界及社会中的团队成功常依赖于不同专业个体间的分工协作，然而对于多样性团队何时优于同质团队，仍缺乏系统性理论解释。聚焦于多智能体任务分配问题，我们从奖励设计的角度研究该问题：何种目标函数最适合异构团队？首先考虑瞬时非空间场景，其全局奖励由两个广义聚合算子构建：内层算子将N个智能体在各项任务上的努力分配映射为任务得分，外层算子将M个任务得分合并为团队全局奖励。我们证明这些算子的曲率决定了异构性能否提升奖励，且对于广泛奖励函数族可简化为凸性检验。接着探究当具身化、时序延展的智能体需通过学习形成努力分配策略时，何种机制会激励异构性产生。为此采用多智能体强化学习（MARL）作为计算范式，提出异构增益参数搜索算法（HetGPS），该梯度算法通过优化未完全指定MARL环境的参数空间，寻找异构性具有优势的场景。在不同环境中，HetGPS重新发现了理论预测能最大化异构优势的奖励机制，既验证了算法有效性，也将理论洞见与MARL奖励设计相连接。这些成果共同揭示了行为多样性产生可量化收益的适用条件。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates when behavioral diversity benefits cooperative multi-agent teams, motivated by the need for a principled understanding of division of labor. The method combines theoretical analysis of reward functions, using generalized aggregation operators to model task allocation, with a practical multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) algorithm called HetGPS that searches for environmental parameters favoring heterogeneity. Experimental results show that the curvature of reward operators predicts when heterogeneity increases reward, and HetGPS successfully identifies reward regimes where diverse teams outperform homogeneous ones, bridging theory and MARL applications.
本文研究行为多样性何时有益于合作多智能体团队，动机在于需要从原理上理解分工的优势。方法结合了对奖励函数的理论分析（使用广义聚合算子建模任务分配）和一种实用的多智能体强化学习算法HetGPS，该算法通过搜索环境参数来寻找有利于异质性的场景。实验结果表明，奖励算子的曲率可以预测异质性何时能提高奖励，并且HetGPS成功发现了使多样化团队优于同质团队的奖励机制，从而将理论见解与多智能体强化学习实践联系起来。
GEM: A Gym for Agentic LLMs
Authors: Zichen Liu, Anya Sims, Keyu Duan, Changyu Chen, Simon Yu, Xiangxin Zhou, Haotian Xu, Shaopan Xiong, Bo Liu, Chenmien Tan, Chuen Yang Beh, Weixun Wang, Hao Zhu, Weiyan Shi, Diyi Yang, Michael Shieh, Yee Whye Teh, Wee Sun Lee, Min Lin
First: 2025-10-01T15:55:57+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-01T14:06:03+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The training paradigm for large language models (LLMs) is moving from static datasets to experience-based learning, where agents acquire skills via interacting with complex environments. To facilitate this transition we introduce GEM (General Experience Maker), an open-source environment simulator designed for the age of LLMs. Analogous to OpenAI-Gym for traditional reinforcement learning (RL), GEM provides a standardized framework for the environment-agent interface, including asynchronous vectorized execution for high throughput, and flexible wrappers for easy extensibility. GEM also features a diverse suite of environments, robust integrated tools, and single-file example scripts demonstrating using GEM with five popular RL training frameworks. Along with this, we also provide a set of baselines across 24 environments using REINFORCE with Return Batch Normalization (ReBN), which -- unlike GRPO -- is compatible with the full RL setting of dense per-turn rewards and offers better credit assignment. We further conduct apple-to-apple benchmarking of PPO, GRPO and REINFORCE in both single- and multi-turn settings using GEM to shed light on the algorithmic designs. Lastly, GEM also functions as a convenient evaluation toolkit besides a training environment. We hope this framework can help accelerate future agentic LLM research.
中文标题/摘要
标题：GEM：面向智能体化大语言模型的训练场
大语言模型（LLMs）的训练范式正从静态数据集转向基于经验的学习，即智能体通过与环境交互获取技能。为促进这一转变，我们推出GEM（通用经验生成器）——一个专为LLM时代设计的开源环境模拟器。类比传统强化学习中的OpenAI-Gym，GEM提供了标准化的环境-智能体接口框架，包含支持高吞吐的异步向量化执行机制，以及便于扩展的灵活封装器。GEM还具备多样化的环境套件、鲁棒的集成工具，以及展示其与五种主流RL训练框架结合使用的单文件示例脚本。同时，我们基于带回报批量归一化的REINFORCE算法（ReBN）在24个环境中建立基准测试集——与GRPO不同，ReBN兼容密集单步奖励的完整RL设定，并提供更优的信用分配机制。进一步，我们利用GEM在单轮与多轮场景中对PPO、GRPO和REINFORCE进行公平基准测试，以揭示算法设计特性。此外，GEM除作为训练环境外，亦可作为便捷的评估工具包。我们希望该框架能助力未来智能体化LLM研究的加速发展。

DIVA-GRPO: Enhancing Multimodal Reasoning through Difficulty-Adaptive Variant Advantage
Authors: Haowen Gao, Zhenyu Zhang, Liang Pang, Fangda Guo, Hongjian Dou, Guannan Lv, Shaoguo Liu, Tingting Gao, Huawei Shen, Xueqi Cheng
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-03-01T13:47:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-01T13:47:35+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ICLR 2026. Code and models are available at https://github.com/Siaaaaaa1/DIVA-GRPO
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) with group relative policy optimization (GRPO) has become a widely adopted approach for enhancing the reasoning capabilities of multimodal large language models (MLLMs). While GRPO enables long-chain reasoning without a critic, it often suffers from sparse rewards on difficult problems and advantage vanishing when group-level rewards are too consistent for overly easy or hard problems. Existing solutions (sample expansion, selective utilization, and indirect reward design) often fail to maintain enough variance in within-group reward distributions to yield clear optimization signals. To address this, we propose DIVA-GRPO, a difficulty-adaptive variant advantage method that adjusts variant difficulty distributions from a global perspective. DIVA-GRPO dynamically assesses problem difficulty, samples variants with appropriate difficulty levels, and calculates advantages across local and global groups using difficulty-weighted and normalized scaling. This alleviates reward sparsity and advantage vanishing while improving training stability. Extensive experiments on six reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that DIVA-GRPO outperforms existing approaches in training efficiency and reasoning performance. Code: https://github.com/Siaaaaaa1/DIVA-GRPO
中文标题/摘要

The proposed method, DIVA-GRPO, addresses these issues by dynamically assessing problem difficulty, sampling variants with appropriate difficulty levels, and calculating advantages using difficulty-weighted and normalized scaling across local and global groups to enhance optimization signals and stability. Experimental results on six reasoning benchmarks show that DIVA-GRPO outperforms existing approaches in both training efficiency and reasoning performance.

Online Causal Kalman Filtering for Stable and Effective Policy Optimization
Authors: Shuo He, Lang Feng, Xin Cheng, Lei Feng, Bo An
First: 2026-02-11T07:57:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-01T13:35:19+00:00
Comments: Preprint
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning for large language models suffers from high-variance token-level importance sampling (IS) ratios, which would destabilize policy optimization at scale. To improve stability, recent methods typically use a fixed sequence-level IS ratio for all tokens in a sequence or adjust each token's IS ratio separately, thereby neglecting temporal off-policy derivation across tokens in a sequence. In this paper, we first empirically identify that local off-policy deviation is structurally inconsistent at the token level, which may distort policy-gradient updates across adjacent tokens and lead to training collapse. To address the issue, we propose Online Causal Kalman Filtering for stable and effective Policy Optimization (KPO). Concretely, we model the desired IS ratio as a latent state that evolves across tokens and apply a Kalman filter to update this state online and autoregressively based on the states of past tokens, regardless of future tokens. The resulting filtered IS ratios preserve token-wise local structure-aware variation while strongly smoothing noise spikes, yielding more stable and effective policy updates. Experimentally, KPO achieves superior results on challenging math reasoning datasets compared with state-of-the-art counterparts.
中文标题/摘要
标题：在线因果卡尔曼滤波实现稳定高效策略优化
大语言模型的强化学习面临高方差词元级重要性采样比率问题，这会导致大规模策略优化失稳。现有方法通常对序列中所有词元使用固定的序列级重要性采样比率，或单独调整各词元比率，忽略了序列中词元间的时间离策略推导。本文首先通过实证发现，局部离策略偏差在词元层面存在结构性不一致，可能扭曲相邻词元间的策略梯度更新并导致训练崩溃。为解决该问题，我们提出基于在线因果卡尔曼滤波的稳定高效策略优化方法。具体而言，我们将目标重要性采样比率建模为跨词元演化的潜在状态，并应用卡尔曼滤波器基于历史词元状态在线自回归更新该状态，无需依赖未来词元。经滤波处理的重要性采样比率在保留词元级局部结构感知变化的同时，有效平滑噪声尖峰，从而产生更稳定高效的策略更新。实验表明，在具有挑战性的数学推理数据集上，该方法取得了优于现有先进模型的结果。

The motivation for this work is to address the instability in reinforcement learning for large language models caused by high-variance token-level importance sampling ratios, which can lead to training collapse. The method proposed, Online Causal Kalman Filtering for Policy Optimization (KPO), models the importance sampling ratio as a latent state evolving across tokens and applies a Kalman filter to update it online and autoregressively, smoothing noise while preserving local token-wise structure. Experimental results show that KPO achieves superior performance on challenging math reasoning datasets compared to state-of-the-art methods, demonstrating more stable and effective policy optimization.

Feasible Pairings for Decentralized Integral Controllability of Non-Square Systems
Authors: Yuhao Tong, Steven W. Su
First: 2026-03-01T12:42:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-01T12:42:26+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper investigates the determination of feasible input-output pairings for the decentralized integral controllability of non-square systems. The relevance of this problem extends beyond traditional industrial processes into modern AI research, particularly Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning (MARL), where environments frequently act as strongly non-square mappings that evaluate high-dimensional joint action spaces via comparatively low-dimensional global rewards. To address the stability of these complex distributed architectures, we extend the concept of D-stability to non-square matrices, providing a crucial mathematical foundation. We formally define D-stability for non-square matrices as a direct generalization of the square case. By introducing the concept of ``Squared Matrices'', which are derived from specific column selections of the non-square formulation and directly correspond to candidate control pairings, we establish a fundamental link between the stability of these square sub-components and the original non-square system. Ultimately, we propose sufficient conditions under which the individual Volterra-Lyapunov stability of these squared components guarantees the extended D-stability of the non-square matrix, thereby providing a rigorous method to identify feasible pairings that ensure robust decentralized control across both classical and data-driven applications.
中文标题/摘要
标题：非方系统分散积分可控性的可行配对研究
本文研究了非方系统分散积分可控性中可行输入-输出配对的确定方法。该问题的相关性不仅限于传统工业过程，还延伸至现代人工智能研究，特别是多智能体强化学习（MARL）领域，其中环境常表现为强非方映射，通过相对低维的全局奖励评估高维联合动作空间。为确保这类复杂分布式架构的稳定性，我们将D稳定性概念推广至非方矩阵，提供了关键的数学基础。我们正式将非方矩阵的D稳定性定义为方阵情况的直接推广。通过引入“方化矩阵”概念（该矩阵源自非方公式的特定列选择，并直接对应候选控制配对），我们建立了这些方化子组件稳定性与原非方系统之间的根本联系。最终，我们提出了充分条件，证明当这些方化组件各自满足Volterra-Lyapunov稳定性时，可保证非方矩阵的扩展D稳定性，从而为经典和数据驱动应用提供了一种识别可行配对的严格方法，以确保鲁棒的分散控制。
