The method introduces 'Squared Matrices' derived from column selections of the non-square system, linking the stability of these square components to the original system. The main experimental results establish sufficient conditions under which Volterra-Lyapunov stability of the squared matrices guarantees extended D-stability of the non-square matrix, providing a rigorous framework for identifying robust control pairings in both classical and data-driven applications.
本文旨在解决复杂分布式系统（包括多智能体强化学习中常见的非方映射）的稳定性问题，通过将D稳定性概念扩展至非方矩阵，以确定去中心化积分可控性的可行输入输出配对。方法上引入了从非方系统列选择导出的“方阵”，将这些方阵子组件的稳定性与原系统联系起来。主要实验结果建立了充分条件，证明这些方阵的Volterra-Lyapunov稳定性可确保非方矩阵的扩展D稳定性，从而为经典和数据驱动应用中的鲁棒控制配对识别提供了严谨的理论框架。
Counterfactual Credit Guided Bayesian Optimization
Authors: Qiyu Wei, Haowei Wang, Richard Allmendinger, Mauricio A. Álvarez
First: 2025-10-06T10:34:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-01T12:28:54+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Bayesian optimization has emerged as a prominent methodology for optimizing expensive black-box functions by leveraging Gaussian process surrogates, which focus on capturing the global characteristics of the objective function. However, in numerous practical scenarios, the primary objective is not to construct an exhaustive global surrogate, but rather to quickly pinpoint the global optimum. Due to the aleatoric nature of the sequential optimization problem and its dependence on the quality of the surrogate model and the initial design, it is restrictive to assume that all observed samples contribute equally to the discovery of the optimum in this context. In this paper, we introduce Counterfactual Credit Guided Bayesian Optimization (CCGBO), a novel framework that explicitly quantifies the contribution of individual historical observations through counterfactual credit. By incorporating counterfactual credit into the acquisition function, our approach can selectively allocate resources in areas where optimal solutions are most likely to occur. We prove that CCGBO retains sublinear regret. Empirical evaluations on various synthetic and real-world benchmarks demonstrate that CCGBO consistently reduces simple regret and accelerates convergence to the global optimum.
中文标题/摘要
标题：反事实信用引导的贝叶斯优化
贝叶斯优化已成为通过高斯过程代理模型优化昂贵黑盒函数的重要方法，其侧重于捕捉目标函数的全局特征。然而，在许多实际场景中，主要目标并非构建详尽的全局代理模型，而是快速定位全局最优解。由于序列优化问题的随机性及其对代理模型质量和初始设计的依赖性，假设所有观测样本对最优解的发现具有同等贡献具有局限性。本文提出反事实信用引导的贝叶斯优化（CCGBO）这一新颖框架，通过反事实信用显式量化个体历史观测的贡献度。通过将反事实信用融入采集函数，我们的方法能够在最优解最可能出现的区域选择性分配资源。我们证明CCGBO保持次线性遗憾。在多种合成与真实基准测试中的实证评估表明，CCGBO能持续降低简单遗憾并加速向全局最优解的收敛。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the need to accelerate the search for a global optimum in Bayesian optimization, rather than building a comprehensive global surrogate model, by recognizing that not all historical observations equally contribute to finding the optimum. The method introduces Counterfactual Credit Guided Bayesian Optimization (CCGBO), which quantifies the contribution of each past observation using counterfactual credit and integrates this into the acquisition function to prioritize resource allocation in promising regions. Experimental results on synthetic and real-world benchmarks show that CCGBO consistently reduces simple regret and speeds up convergence to the global optimum while maintaining sublinear regret guarantees.
本文的动机在于，贝叶斯优化中并非所有历史观测都同等有助于寻找全局最优解，因此需要加速全局最优点的搜索，而非构建全面的全局代理模型。方法上提出了反事实信用引导的贝叶斯优化（CCGBO），通过反事实信用量化每个历史观测的贡献，并将其融入采集函数，以在最有希望的区域优先分配资源。实验结果表明，在合成和真实世界基准测试中，CCGBO能持续降低简单遗憾并加速收敛到全局最优解，同时保持次线性遗憾保证。
Separating Ansatz Discovery from Deployment on Larger Problems: Reinforcement Learning for Modular Circuit Design
Authors: Gloria Turati, Simone Foderà, Riccardo Nembrini, Maurizio Ferrari Dacrema, Paolo Cremonesi
First: 2025-07-21T18:40:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-01T11:58:57+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
As quantum computing continues to gain attention, there is growing interest in how classical machine learning can assist quantum workflows in practice. Automated circuit design, sometimes referred to as Quantum Architecture Search (QAS), is a natural application but relies on the ability to model the quantum system to support learning as the number of qubits grows. This challenge is central to QAS, and much of the current literature that proposes new ways to model the ansatz focuses on small systems, often around ten qubits. In this work, we propose a complementary approach that separates a small-scale structure discovery phase, where a reusable modular circuit block is learned on small instances where classical learning is feasible, from a deployment phase, where the blocks are used to create the ansatz required for larger problems. To this end, we introduce Reinforcement Learning for Variational Quantum Circuits (RLVQC), formulating QAS as a sequential decision-making problem. We evaluate our methodology on Quadratic Unconstrained Binary Optimization (QUBO) instances derived from Maximum Cut, Maximum Clique, and Minimum Vertex Cover. Our RLVQC Block model is trained to discover a modular two-qubit block that can generalize QAOA-style methods and that is often beneficial compared to learning non-modular ansatzes. The blocks discovered on n=8 instances remain effective when deployed on larger instances (n=12 and n=16), supporting the feasibility of reusing learned modular structure across problem sizes. While we do not aim to establish a new state-of-the-art solver or an advantage over classical methods, our results provide evidence that modular ansatz structure can be learned on smaller instances and then extended to larger ones without requiring learning on systems with a large number of qubits, where quantum computing becomes interesting but classical computation becomes impractical.
中文标题/摘要
标题：将变分结构发现与大规模问题部署分离：面向模块化电路设计的强化学习方法
随着量子计算持续受到关注，经典机器学习如何实际辅助量子工作流日益成为研究热点。自动电路设计（常称为量子架构搜索）是自然应用方向，但其依赖于对量子系统的建模能力以支持随量子比特数增长的学习过程。这一挑战是量子架构搜索的核心问题，当前多数提出新变分结构建模方法的文献聚焦于小型系统（通常约十个量子比特）。本研究提出一种互补性方法：将小规模结构发现阶段（在经典学习可行的小型实例上学习可复用的模块化电路单元）与部署阶段（利用该单元构建大规模问题所需的变分结构）相分离。为此，我们提出变分量子电路的强化学习方法，将量子架构搜索建模为序列决策问题。我们在基于最大割、最大团和最小顶点覆盖衍生的二次无约束二进制优化实例上评估该方法。训练的强化学习变分量子电路模块模型能够发现可推广量子近似优化算法风格方法的模块化双量子比特单元，相比非模块化变分结构通常更具优势。在n=8实例上发现的模块在部署至更大规模实例（n=12与n=16）时仍保持有效性，这证实了跨问题规模复用学习所得模块化结构的可行性。虽然本研究不旨在建立新的最先进求解器或证明其相对经典方法的优势，但结果证明模块化变分结构可在小型实例上学习，并无需在量子计算具有研究价值但经典计算已不切实际的大规模量子比特系统上重新学习，即可扩展至更大规模问题。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of scaling automated quantum circuit design (Quantum Architecture Search, QAS) to larger qubit counts where classical simulation becomes infeasible, this work proposes a two-phase approach that separates small-scale structure discovery from deployment. The method, named Reinforcement Learning for Variational Quantum Circuits (RLVQC), formulates QAS as a sequential decision-making problem to discover a reusable, modular two-qubit circuit block on small (n=8) problem instances. Experimental results on QUBO problems derived from Maximum Cut, Maximum Clique, and Minimum Vertex Cover show that the discovered blocks generalize QAOA-style methods, often outperform non-modular ansatzes, and remain effective when deployed on larger instances (n=12 and n=16), demonstrating the feasibility of transferring learned modular structure across problem sizes without requiring direct learning on large quantum systems.
本研究旨在解决量子架构搜索（QAS）在量子比特数增加时难以通过经典计算进行模拟的扩展性挑战，提出了一种将小规模结构发现与大规模部署分离的两阶段方法。该方法称为变分量子电路的强化学习（RLVQC），将QAS构建为一个序列决策问题，用于在小规模（n=8）问题实例上发现可重用的模块化双量子比特电路块。在基于最大割、最大团和最小顶点覆盖的QUBO问题上的实验结果表明，所发现的模块能推广QAOA风格的方法，通常优于非模块化拟设，并且在部署到更大实例（n=12和n=16）时仍保持有效，这证明了无需在大型量子系统上直接学习即可将习得的模块化结构跨问题规模转移的可行性。
UME-R1: Exploring Reasoning-Driven Generative Multimodal Embeddings
Authors: Zhibin Lan, Liqiang Niu, Fandong Meng, Jie Zhou, Jinsong Su
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-11-01T05:04:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-01T11:57:54+00:00
Comments: Accepted by ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
The remarkable success of multimodal large language models (MLLMs) has driven advances in multimodal embeddings, yet existing models remain inherently discriminative, limiting their ability to benefit from reasoning-driven generation paradigm. In this work, we pioneer the exploration of generative embeddings, unifying embedding tasks within a generative paradigm. We propose UME-R1, a universal multimodal embedding framework consisting of a two-stage training strategy: a cold-start supervised fine-tuning equips the model with reasoning capabilities and enables it to generate both discriminative and generative embeddings; a subsequent reinforcement learning enhances reasoning and further optimizes generative embedding quality. This pioneering work reveals four key insights: 1) generative embeddings unlock substantial performance gains over conventional discriminative embeddings by leveraging the powerful generative reasoning capabilities of MLLMs; 2) discriminative and generative embeddings are complementary, whose combined oracle performance far exceeding that of either alone; 3) RL can effectively enhance generative embeddings, establishing a scalable optimization paradigm.; 4) repeated sampling at inference boosts downstream task coverage (pass@k), highlighting the inference-time scalability potential of generative embeddings. Evaluated on the MMEB-V2 benchmark across 78 tasks spanning video, image, and visual documents, UME-R1 significantly outperforms conventional discriminative embedding models and offers a foundation for more interpretable, reasoning-driven generative multimodal embeddings. Our code, models, and datasets will be publicly available at https://github.com/XMUDeepLIT/UME-R1.
中文标题/摘要
标题：UME-R1：探索推理驱动的生成式多模态嵌入
多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）的显著成功推动了多模态嵌入的发展，但现有模型本质上仍是判别式的，限制了其从推理驱动的生成范式中获益的能力。本研究率先探索生成式嵌入，将嵌入任务统一于生成范式。我们提出UME-R1，一个通用多模态嵌入框架，采用两阶段训练策略：冷启动监督微调赋予模型推理能力，使其能同时生成判别式和生成式嵌入；后续强化学习增强推理并进一步优化生成式嵌入质量。这项开创性工作揭示了四个关键发现：1）生成式嵌入通过利用MLLMs强大的生成推理能力，相比传统判别式嵌入带来显著性能提升；2）判别式与生成式嵌入具有互补性，二者组合的预言性能远超单一类型；3）强化学习能有效增强生成式嵌入，建立可扩展的优化范式；4）推理时重复采样提升下游任务覆盖率（pass@k），凸显生成式嵌入在推理时的可扩展潜力。在涵盖视频、图像和视觉文档的78个任务的MMEB-V2基准测试中，UME-R1显著优于传统判别式嵌入模型，并为更具可解释性、推理驱动的生成式多模态嵌入奠定基础。代码、模型和数据集将公开于https://github.com/XMUDeepLIT/UME-R1。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of inherently discriminative multimodal embeddings, this work pioneers a reasoning-driven generative paradigm to unify embedding tasks. The method introduces UME-R1, a universal multimodal embedding framework trained via a two-stage strategy: supervised fine-tuning for initial reasoning and embedding generation, followed by reinforcement learning to enhance reasoning and optimize generative embedding quality. Key experimental results on the MMEB-V2 benchmark across 78 tasks show that generative embeddings substantially outperform conventional discriminative ones, with their combination yielding even greater gains, while reinforcement learning effectively improves generative embeddings and repeated sampling boosts inference-time coverage, establishing a scalable optimization approach.
本研究针对现有多模态嵌入模型固有的判别式局限性，率先探索推理驱动的生成式范式以统一嵌入任务。方法上提出了UME-R1通用多模态嵌入框架，采用两阶段训练策略：通过监督微调赋予模型推理能力以生成判别式和生成式嵌入，再通过强化学习增强推理并优化生成式嵌入质量。在MMEB-V2基准的78个任务上的主要实验结果表明，生成式嵌入显著优于传统判别式嵌入，两者结合能实现更大性能提升，强化学习可有效优化生成式嵌入，而推理时重复采样提高了任务覆盖度，为可扩展的优化范式奠定了基础。
MM-DeepResearch: A Simple and Effective Multimodal Agentic Search Baseline
Authors: Huanjin Yao, Qixiang Yin, Min Yang, Ziwang Zhao, Yibo Wang, Haotian Luo, Jingyi Zhang, Jiaxing Huang
First: 2026-03-01T11:13:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-01T11:13:22+00:00
Comments: Technical report
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
We aim to develop a multimodal research agent capable of explicit reasoning and planning, multi-tool invocation, and cross-modal information synthesis, enabling it to conduct deep research tasks. However, we observe three main challenges in developing such agents: (1) scarcity of search-intensive multimodal QA data, (2) lack of effective search trajectories, and (3) prohibitive cost of training with online search APIs. To tackle them, we first propose Hyper-Search, a hypergraph-based QA generation method that models and connects visual and textual nodes within and across modalities, enabling to generate search-intensive multimodal QA pairs that require invoking various search tools to solve. Second, we introduce DR-TTS, which first decomposes search-involved tasks into several categories according to search tool types, and respectively optimize specialized search tool experts for each tool. It then recomposes tool experts to jointly explore search trajectories via tree search, producing trajectories that successfully solve complex tasks using various search tools. Third, we build an offline search engine supporting multiple search tools, enabling agentic reinforcement learning without using costly online search APIs. With the three designs, we develop MM-DeepResearch, a powerful multimodal deep research agent, and extensive results shows its superiority across benchmarks. Code is available at https://github.com/HJYao00/MM-DeepResearch
中文标题/摘要
标题：MM-DeepResearch：一种简单有效的多模态智能体搜索基线
我们旨在开发一种具备显式推理与规划、多工具调用及跨模态信息融合能力的多模态研究智能体，以执行深度研究任务。然而，我们发现开发此类智能体面临三大挑战：(1) 搜索密集型多模态问答数据稀缺；(2) 缺乏有效的搜索轨迹；(3) 使用在线搜索API训练成本过高。为此，我们首先提出Hyper-Search——一种基于超图的问答生成方法，通过建模并连接模态内与跨模态的视觉与文本节点，生成需要调用多种搜索工具解决的搜索密集型多模态问答对。其次，我们提出DR-TTS方法：先根据搜索工具类型将涉及搜索的任务分解为若干类别，并针对每类工具分别优化专用搜索工具专家；随后重组工具专家，通过树搜索协同探索搜索轨迹，生成能利用多种搜索工具成功解决复杂任务的轨迹。最后，我们构建了支持多搜索工具的离线搜索引擎，使智能体强化学习无需依赖高成本的在线搜索API。基于这三项设计，我们开发了强大的多模态深度研究智能体MM-DeepResearch，大量实验结果表明其在多个基准测试中均具优越性。代码发布于 https://github.com/HJYao00/MM-DeepResearch
Summary / 总结
The paper aims to develop a multimodal research agent capable of deep research through explicit reasoning, multi-tool use, and cross-modal synthesis, but faces challenges including scarce search-intensive multimodal QA data, ineffective search trajectories, and high costs of online API training. To address these, the method introduces Hyper-Search for generating search-intensive multimodal QA pairs via hypergraph modeling, DR-TTS for decomposing tasks by tool type and optimizing specialized experts recomposed via tree search to explore effective trajectories, and an offline search engine to enable cost-efficient agentic reinforcement learning. Experimental results demonstrate that the resulting MM-DeepResearch agent achieves superior performance across benchmarks, validating the effectiveness of the proposed approaches.
本文旨在开发一种能够通过显式推理、多工具调用和跨模态合成进行深度研究的多模态研究智能体，但面临搜索密集型多模态问答数据稀缺、搜索轨迹效率低下以及在线API训练成本高昂等挑战。为解决这些问题，方法提出了Hyper-Search，通过超图建模生成搜索密集型多模态问答对；DR-TTS将任务按工具类型分解并优化专用专家，再通过树搜索重组以探索有效轨迹；以及构建离线搜索引擎以支持低成本智能体强化学习。实验结果表明，所开发的MM-DeepResearch智能体在多个基准测试中表现优异，验证了所提方法的有效性。
Adaptive Context Length Optimization with Low-Frequency Truncation for Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Wenchang Duan, Yaoliang Yu, Jiwan He, Yi Shi
First: 2025-10-30T11:32:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-01T11:04:04+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recently, deep multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) has demonstrated promising performance for solving challenging tasks, such as long-term dependencies and non-Markovian environments. Its success is partly attributed to conditioning policies on large fixed context length. However, such large fixed context lengths may lead to limited exploration efficiency and redundant information. In this paper, we propose a novel MARL framework to obtain adaptive and effective contextual information. Specifically, we design a central agent that dynamically optimizes context length via temporal gradient analysis, enhancing exploration to facilitate convergence to global optima in MARL. Furthermore, to enhance the adaptive optimization capability of the context length, we present an efficient input representation for the central agent, which effectively filters redundant information. By leveraging a Fourier-based low-frequency truncation method, we extract global temporal trends across decentralized agents, providing an effective and efficient representation of the MARL environment. Extensive experiments demonstrate that the proposed method achieves state-of-the-art (SOTA) performance on long-term dependency tasks, including PettingZoo, MiniGrid, Google Research Football (GRF), and StarCraft Multi-Agent Challenge v2 (SMACv2).
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于低频截断的自适应上下文长度优化用于多智能体强化学习
近年来，深度多智能体强化学习（MARL）在解决长期依赖与非马尔可夫环境等复杂任务中展现出优异性能，其成功部分依赖于对固定长上下文的条件策略。然而，过长的固定上下文可能导致探索效率受限与信息冗余。本文提出一种新型MARL框架，旨在获取自适应且高效的上下文信息。具体而言，我们设计了一个中央智能体，通过时序梯度分析动态优化上下文长度，以增强探索能力并促进MARL收敛至全局最优。为进一步提升上下文长度的自适应优化能力，我们为中央智能体构建了高效的输入表征，可有效过滤冗余信息。通过基于傅里叶变换的低频截断方法，我们提取去中心化智能体间的全局时序趋势，为MARL环境提供高效表征。大量实验表明，该方法在长期依赖任务（包括PettingZoo、MiniGrid、谷歌研究足球（GRF）及星际争霸多智能体挑战赛v2（SMACv2））中取得了最先进的性能。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the inefficiency of using large fixed context lengths in deep multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL), which can hinder exploration and introduce redundant information. To tackle this, the authors propose a novel MARL framework where a central agent dynamically optimizes context length through temporal gradient analysis, thereby improving exploration and convergence to global optima. Additionally, they enhance this adaptive optimization by employing a Fourier-based low-frequency truncation method to filter redundant information and extract global temporal trends across decentralized agents, resulting in an efficient input representation. Experimental results show that this method achieves state-of-the-art performance on long-term dependency tasks in environments such as PettingZoo, MiniGrid, Google Research Football, and StarCraft Multi-Agent Challenge v2.
本文针对深度多智能体强化学习中固定大上下文长度导致的探索效率低下和冗余信息问题，提出了一种新颖的框架。该方法通过一个中心智能体，利用时间梯度分析动态优化上下文长度，以增强探索能力并促进收敛至全局最优解。同时，采用基于傅里叶的低频截断方法，过滤冗余信息并提取分散智能体间的全局时间趋势，从而提供高效的环境表示。大量实验表明，该方法在PettingZoo、MiniGrid、Google Research Football和StarCraft Multi-Agent Challenge v2等长期依赖任务上取得了最先进的性能。
